
-----title
开化 (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　寓居衢州开化灵山寺之西轩，识僧修意。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　与毛随上书斥为邪籍，皆罢吏归乡。有诗，时间不可确考，姑系于此。作品：《龙尾砚同毛彦时随联句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷七。）</span>《神霄宫知宫陈应常邀乡人集道堂余不果往毛彦时有诗诸公皆和见率同作次韵一首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_527192' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527192' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527192?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙尾砚同毛彦时随联句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527192")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527192_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527192'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527192'>歙水清以駃，歙山文且坚<span class='inlineComment2'>（程）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527192'>谁持玉斧琢，制此月样圆。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527192'>想当结绳后，要使鸟迹传。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527192'>雕锼见骨格，岂与瓦砾全<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527192'>陂<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>陀百氏圃，泓澄九经渊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527192'>墨海不复见，柯岩那可肩。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527192'>星稀涵纬象，眉绿生春妍<span class='inlineComment2'>（程）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527192'>规模异镕铁，濡写殊怀铅。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527192'>正当秋兔颖，发此霜松烟<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527192'>一从毛褚游，几作虫鱼笺。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527192'>徵辞想妃子，揾首怀张颠。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527192'>宁同李生瘗，聊续胡公镌<span class='inlineComment2'>（程）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527192'>常疑老蚌壳，浸润成膏妍<span class='inlineComment2'>（毛）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527192'>坚踰鹅池铸，质射铜台埏。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527192'>纷纷况多伪，渴雀同栀鞭<span class='inlineComment2'>（程）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527192'>琳坳隐多水，十手寄所宣。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527192'>池光潋墨色，云气开毫联。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527192'>翔鸾及垂露，逸势徒飞骞。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527192'>谁云过圭璧，或用磨戈鋋。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527192'>吾今欲焚弃，负耒归园田。<div id='poem_sentence_19_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_527192'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_527192_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527192'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_527192_0'>⑴ 原作故，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527192_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527164' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527164' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527164?labeling=true' target='_blank'>神霄宫知宫陈应常邀乡人集道堂余不果往毛彦时有诗诸公皆和见率同作次韵一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527164")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527164_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527164'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527164'>南枝月明乌鹊飞，北风惊沙燕马嘶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527164'>倦游乃有故乡念，强学处士听朝鸡。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527164'>马蹄得得乌帽底，与日竞走东还西。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527164'>安知神府在人境，晓雾十里飞香猊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527164'>咄嗟似与化人遇，宫殿盘郁穷烟霏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527164'>瑛房蕊箧浩无极，当关九虎何由窥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527164'>仙郎邀客自清旦，阒若岫户临江湄。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527164'>向来同是烂柯客，石梁跨野长虹垂。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527164'>登晨未辨七盟盖，祈年欲采三华芝。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527164'>授书忽作蕊珠吏，云篆岂特传盟威。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527164'>故人一笑共清景，常谈曲谨皆芟夷。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527164'>而余煮饼北窗卧，正坐世网缠绵之。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527164'>枣瓜麟脯不同举，但见䌽笔方交驰。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527164'>萧然俯仰在环堵，穷巷偪仄仍喧卑。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527164'>高堂修竹寄遐想，况烹雪乳调清丝。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527164'>径须暇日一寻胜，眼中尘袂空成帷。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527164_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527164'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_527164_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　寓居衢州开化灵山寺，与江纬、江褒交游，酬唱颇多。作品：《同江彦文纬江仲嘉褒度菱湖岭游三衢诸山道灵真出入岩谷胜绝可骇杂然有卜筑之意然此地寥阒人所不争小隐不难致顾吾曹出处何如耳二公皆修真养气精进不衰予晚闻此道又为忧病顿挫志倦体疲每思益友倘得静舍安余年资二子以待老岂不乐哉作诗叙游且志本末岩谷之胜实自仲嘉发之予尝闻而赋诗，所谓“武陵迷汉魏，妙喜断山川”者也》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷二。程俱，为江氏门人，从游于江纬。江纬，字彦文。侄少虞、少齐、汉与汪藻、程俱、李处权、赵子昼七人从游，时人指为文中七虎，遂扁讲学之所为七贤堂。七贤堂在开化县南三十五里华川黄泥岭下。）</span>《江仲嘉书称去常山灵真洞半里许得林壑殊胜余记昔过谢源道中乱峰峭壁间竹树荟蘙今仲嘉所称得非此耶因寄百二十字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_526948' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526948' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526948?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同江彦文纬江仲嘉褒度菱湖岭游三衢诸山道灵真出入岩谷胜绝可骇杂然有卜筑之意然此地寥阒人所不争小隐不难致顾吾曹出处何如耳二公皆脩真养气精进不衰予晚闻此道又为忧病顿挫志倦体疲每思益友傥得静舍安馀年资二子以待老岂不乐哉作诗叙游且志本末岩谷之胜实自仲嘉发之予尝闻而赋诗所谓武陵迷汉魏妙喜断山川者也</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526948")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526948_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526948'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526948'>我昔未省事，伥伥如病狂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526948'>仰规结绳初，下历汉魏唐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526948'>谓此纸中语，卷舒在行藏。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526948'>功名戾契取，有志要必偿。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526948'>趼足方不暇，何由放洪荒。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526948'>行年冠而字，世故颇已尝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526948'>试窥竺乾书，出入应帝王。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526948'>丘轲有妙蕴，合处如宫商。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526948'>形骸乃尘沫，笑唾却老方。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526948'>蹭蹬过二纪，身如浮海航。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526948'>风涛浩无际，寄命蛟鼍乡。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526948'>外为万绪婴，内以百虑戕。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526948'>摧颓不一偶，病骨无由强。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526948'>初心益乖迕，始觉计未良。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526948'>拟追赤松游，补我黥劓创。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526948'>惟时子真子，青衫尉南昌。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526948'>亦有虬须翁，种桃撷春芳。<div id='poem_sentence_16_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_526948'>不求飞霞佩，肯受紫锦囊。<div id='poem_sentence_17_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_526948'>至言无旁午，照用寂以忘。<div id='poem_sentence_18_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_526948'>尔来又十年，前却方徬徨。<div id='poem_sentence_19_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_526948'>何殊一日暴，正坐多歧亡。<div id='poem_sentence_20_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_526948'>虬须彼幽人，物化不可量。<div id='poem_sentence_21_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_526948'>子真日千里，似欲穷扶桑。<div id='poem_sentence_22_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_526948'>安知阡陌间，共此暇日长。<div id='poem_sentence_23_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_526948'>广文今稚川，腹有云笈章。<div id='poem_sentence_24_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_526948'>黄金傥可成，绿发不复苍。<div id='poem_sentence_25_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_526948'>养生百千门，一一登奥堂。<div id='poem_sentence_26_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_526948'>相从岩壑间，笑傲无羲皇。<div id='poem_sentence_27_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_526948'>衢山甚奇峭，不数三石梁。<div id='poem_sentence_28_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_526948'>嵚崎尽中空，玉室联珠房。<div id='poem_sentence_29_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_526948'>九日澬未落，洪波怒怀襄。<div id='poem_sentence_30_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_526948'>洄流荡沙壤，灵景忽以彰。<div id='poem_sentence_31_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_526948'>至今众玉聚，山骨堆琳琅。<div id='poem_sentence_32_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_526948'>峨空怒猊踞，出谷惊龙翔。<div id='poem_sentence_33_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_526948'>委蛇青童辙，散乱初平羊。<div id='poem_sentence_34_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_35_526948'>悬崖势欲坠，植笋森分行。<div id='poem_sentence_35_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_526948'>晨光乍映发，紫翠云霞张。<div id='poem_sentence_36_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_37_526948'>攀萝赵公岩，九土何茫茫。<div id='poem_sentence_37_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_526948'>岂无太平酒<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作醴）</span>，浣此膏谷肠。<div id='poem_sentence_38_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_39_526948'>侧身栖真洞，跼蹐仍跄踉。<div id='poem_sentence_39_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_40_526948'>深行得穹窿，陟降殊未央。<div id='poem_sentence_40_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_526948'>举头见空圆，歘若来飞光。<div id='poem_sentence_41_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_42_526948'>翠岩众山底，恍荡疑无旁。<div id='poem_sentence_42_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_43_526948'>故应却尘污，九垒苍屏障。<div id='poem_sentence_43_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_44_526948'>斯游固足乐，质象不可详。<div id='poem_sentence_44_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_526948'>要之大洞中，太山一毫芒。<div id='poem_sentence_45_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_526948'>回鞭灵真路，林涧森相望。<div id='poem_sentence_46_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_47_526948'>穷幽得岩谷，高青对峥嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_47_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_48_526948'>蛇行九锁中，宛转流泉声。<div id='poem_sentence_48_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_526948'>琤琮泻哀湍，力与乱石争。<div id='poem_sentence_49_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_50_526948'>悬瀑或寻丈，势汹洪河倾。<div id='poem_sentence_50_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_51_526948'>泠泠赴深窦，或如环佩鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_51_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_526948'>或于荟蘙中，琴筑时丁丁。<div id='poem_sentence_52_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_53_526948'>或穿嵌岩下，洄洑潴<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>深清。<div id='poem_sentence_53_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_54_526948'>或如铁堂硖，绝壁飞猿惊。<div id='poem_sentence_54_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_526948'>龙蛇走根干，薜蔓悬珠璎。<div id='poem_sentence_55_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_56_526948'>或如钴鉧西，竹树春冬荣。<div id='poem_sentence_56_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_526948'>低昂牛马饮，偃蹇熊罴登。<div id='poem_sentence_57_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_58_526948'>或如袁家渴，长阴昼冥冥。<div id='poem_sentence_58_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_59_526948'>草间兰茝香，石上楩楠青。<div id='poem_sentence_59_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_60_526948'>或如灊谷中，坡陀负崩腾。<div id='poem_sentence_60_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_61_526948'>或如三峡底，仰见匹练明。<div id='poem_sentence_61_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_62_526948'>联绵道林麓，左右临洮城。<div id='poem_sentence_62_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_63_526948'>行行川谷开，蔼蔼皋原平。<div id='poem_sentence_63_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_64_526948'>冥搜已复失，巧语未易名。<div id='poem_sentence_64_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_526948'>不意天壤间，云关敞金庭。<div id='poem_sentence_65_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_66_526948'>向来保幽遽，不挂世俗称。<div id='poem_sentence_66_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_67_526948'>轮蹄固无迹，樵牧或未经。<div id='poem_sentence_67_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_68_526948'>吾属岂神悟，权舆标地英。<div id='poem_sentence_68_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_69_526948'>昏嫁会当毕，衡茅兹可营。<div id='poem_sentence_69_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_70_526948'>二子早闻道，勤行得贞宁。<div id='poem_sentence_70_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_71_526948'>要收十年功，不止九府卿。<div id='poem_sentence_71_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_72_526948'>二树结佳实，五腴练飞琼。<div id='poem_sentence_72_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_526948'>处静已超静，留形要遗形。<div id='poem_sentence_73_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_74_526948'>我懒百不堪，寸田方力耕。<div id='poem_sentence_74_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_75_526948'>会从浮丘伯，及此洪崖生。<div id='poem_sentence_75_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_526948'>乘风御倒景，出入抚八纮。<div id='poem_sentence_76_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_77_526948'>下窥冰炭士，扰扰盘中蝇。<div id='poem_sentence_77_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_78_526948'>三人笑相视，事愿良难并。<div id='poem_sentence_78_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_79_526948'>此志不可负，无为滞尘缨。<div id='poem_sentence_79_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_526948'>清泉闻此言，白石相与盟。<div id='poem_sentence_80_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_81_526948'>作诗纪胜绝，亦用铭吾膺。<div id='poem_sentence_81_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_82_526948'></div><div id='poem_sentence_82_526948_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526948'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_53_526948_0'>⑴ 原作储，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526948_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527268' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527268' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527268?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江仲嘉书称去常山灵真洞半里许得林壑殊胜余记昔过谢源道中乱峰峭壁间竹树荟蘙今仲嘉所称得非此耶因寄百二十字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527268")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_527268_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527268'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527268'>闻说灵真路，旁开小洞天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527268'>苍峦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>閟清境，陆地接飞仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527268'>壁立惊猿挂，松枯老蔓缠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527268'>攒空永亭石，漱壑定林泉。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527268'>烟磴盘三径，玄窗属五便。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527268'>武陵迷汉魏，妙憙断山川。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527268'>腾绝端如此，经营有老焉。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527268'>烹鱼几折屐，命驾拟加鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527268'>易秃三千丈，宁辞四万钱。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527268'>把茅应早计，拱木叹流年。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527268'>鸿鹄须尘外，鹓鸾自日边。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527268'>人生各有在，雅志共超然。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527268'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_527268_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527268'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527268_0'>⑴ 原作蛮，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527268_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　是年过刘姓园居有诗，创作地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《过刘姓园居》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_526893' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526893' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526893?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过刘姓园居</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526893")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526893_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526893'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526893'>负郭三顷稻，并田五亩园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526893'>人生如此足，安用华其轩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526893'>亲戚居南陌，交游在东村。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526893'>有酒辄共醉，倾输见情言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526893'>三径杂桃李，九畦莳兰荪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526893'>黄柑百头奴，碧梧万支孙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526893'>山供景无尽，石映溪不浑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526893'>桑麻中馈任，布刈邻翁论。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526893'>下以活妻孥，上以奉凊温。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526893'>时从赤松子，亦访吴市门。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526893'>嗟我抱此志，十年若朝昏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526893'>家山眇天末，松菊岂复存。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526893'>兹园临官道，坐笑车马奔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526893'>前山复场圃，疏筑随坳墩。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526893'>我来适春秾，乱眼红青纷。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526893'>恍然动乡思，梦寄东飞云。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526893_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526893'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_526893_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　虞谟有和刘姓园居有诗，再用前韵作，因以叙出处之意。创作时间、地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《虞君明谟和刘姓园居诗再用前韵作因以叙出处之意》<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱中没有收录此诗，但据《北山小集》卷二《虞君明谟和刘姓园居诗再用前韵作因以叙出处之意》，此诗应与《过刘姓园居》诗创作时间比较接近，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_526937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>虞君明谟和刘氏园居诗再用前韵作因以叙出处之意</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526937")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526937'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526937'>靖节直有道，高怀俯黄园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526937'>翘足北窗下，超然诣羲轩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526937'>早悟俗中恶，归老三家村。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526937'>清诗有遗味，谁知本无言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526937'>回观一世间，不辨艾与荪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526937'>青黄饰断木，冠裳裹王孙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526937'>当时甚寒饿，声利终莫浑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526937'>公今二千石，此事安足论。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526937'>入当陪隽贤，峨冠宣与温。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526937'>出当仗汉节，登车金马门。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526937'>岂为尚平子，但毕儿女昏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526937'>我今乃穷士，壮图无一存。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526937'>摧颓风埃下，坐见岁月奔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526937'>归欤乃其分，卜胜如浮墩。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526937'>他年有馀食，会见脱世纷。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526937'>过我五湖上，一区同子云。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526937'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_526937_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　与虞谟燕集，再用《过刘姓园居》韵作诗，创作时间、地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《陪君明华燕集复用前韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（年谱中没有收录此诗，但据《北山小集》卷二《陪君明华燕集复用前韵》，此诗应与《虞君明谟和刘姓园居诗再用前韵作因以叙出处之意》诗创作时间比较接近，姑系于此。）</span><div id='poem_526938' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526938' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526938?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陪君明华燕集复用前韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1104年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526938")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526938_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526938'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526938'>华藏万竿玉，何殊辟疆园。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526938'>城中最佳处，时复过高轩。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526938'>危亭望北郭，依依远人村。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526938'>露叶有佳色，桃蹊亦无言。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526938'>累累古藤阴，附石如菖荪。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526938'>下有小衡霍，巑岏列儿孙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526938'>方池是鱼乐，水作千里浑。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526938'>座满北海客，文追谪仙论。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526938'>襟期樗散郑，目系忘言温。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526938'>斯须接棋战，坚壁如辕门。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526938'>不有覆舟虑，宁为注金昏。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526938'>越医死更起，齐霸亡为存。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526938'>日入万籁息，羁禽趣林奔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526938'>林间屹层台，此岂萧公墩。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526938'>徜徉步松月，香露时披纷。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526938'>胡床兴不浅，点缀无微云。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526938_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526938'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_526938_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>　是年游九华山有诗，创作地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《望九华》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_526897' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526897' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526897?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望九华</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526897")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526897_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526897'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526897'>卷帘坐对江南山，掠眼送青来亹亹。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526897'>云泉肺肠久厌饫，挂颊悠然聊复尔。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526897'>奇峰远澹忽四五，爽秀骎骎逼窗几<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526897'>平生九华盛名下，一见定知真是矣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526897'>非关目力睹天奥，正觉群山如聚米。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526897'>好人好人有高韵，不独江州孟公子。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526897'>直缘佳处无仕径，落莫道边同苦李。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526897'>大是忘年耐久交，藜杖青鞋结终始。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526897'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_526897_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526897'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_526897_0'>⑴ 四库本此下有峦重嶂复饶云烟，望中掩冉凝青紫二句</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526897_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化天王僧舍，喜佛事，专气辟谷，为云门院法华阁作记。作品：《衢州开化县云门院法华阁记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221699' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221699' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221699?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州开化县云门院法华阁记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221699")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221699_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221699'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221699'>无量众生，共一大觉海中，或游或沉，等无有二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221699_comment'></div>诸无明者，如沉水人，颠倒坠溺，东西踊偾，所向苦恼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221699_comment'></div>有善游者，无心于水，与汩俱出，与齐俱入，则此水者是游戏处，安肆快乐，无所疑畏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221699_comment'></div>惟东方十万亿国土中世界名曰震旦，一劫五浊，烦恼之聚，一切众生，选佛之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221699_comment'></div>何以故？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221699_comment'></div>是中众生业力虽厚，而其信心堪任大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221699_comment'></div>又如莲华，必于淤泥乃能生植，高原陆地不复能生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221699_comment'></div>诸烦恼中，即《大般若》「一念返照，超诸如来」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221699_comment'></div>是故过去诸佛说《妙法莲华经》时，光明示现，希有如是，好城国中乃有千万亿种疑惑众生，耆阇崛山乃有增上慢人，退席四众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221699_comment'></div>唯此震旦，一切众生，若智若愚，闻《法华》名莫不稽首，乃至庄严供养，舍诸所爱，无上慢者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221699_comment'></div>岂非耆阇之四众，不如震旦之众生也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221699_comment'></div>衢州开化县之北原寿圣云门院有比丘曰宝声，早受具戒，从义学师指授，演说修多罗教；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221699_comment'></div>晚归山中，于海商所得倭国金书《妙法莲华经》，为七宝函，庄严承事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221699_comment'></div>又建宝阁，上有诸佛及大菩萨阿罗汉像，旃檀髹采，金银丹垩，缯幡珠网，种种庄校，以作佛事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221699_comment'></div>前荣敞明，可布法席，后楹旷深，可以宴坐，四楯周匝，可以经行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221699_comment'></div>作于元丰之辛酉，成于绍圣之甲戌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221699_comment'></div>后十一年，宝声比丘从里人程俱说如是事，请记以文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221699_comment'></div>因随喜佛事，以偈赞云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_1221699'>住音然灯佛，从日月灯明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221699_comment'></div>及释迦牟尼，临入般涅槃，安坐说是法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221699_comment'></div>大通智胜佛，亦于三昧中，放无量光明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221699_comment'></div>最后说如是，四为法施会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221699_comment'></div>灭度僧祇众，如我观如来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221699_comment'></div>不独是时说，常说是经法，未曾有间断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221699_comment'></div>彼十六王子，及万亿菩萨，今见在世间，处处为法施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221699_comment'></div>众生自盲聋，不见如是事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221699_comment'></div>耆阇崛山中，授记诸佛子，舍利弗迦叶，乃至阿罗汉，学无学人等，普于人天前，付嘱当作佛，如我观释迦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221699_comment'></div>不独记是等，无量无央数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221699_comment'></div>五道诸众生，草木及山河，一一授佛记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221699_comment'></div>云当决定得，阿耨三菩提。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221699_comment'></div>众生自狭劣，不信如是事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221699_comment'></div>佛子应如是，福德无有量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221699_comment'></div>正使十地众，总持山海辩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221699_comment'></div>充满于大千，拟心共思量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221699_comment'></div>无复有是处，稽首于一切，《妙法莲华经》。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1221699_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年6月15日</a>　寓居衢州开化天王僧舍，喜佛事，专气辟谷。六月十五日，为谢原山照堂作记。作品：《照堂记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221703' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221703' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221703?labeling=true' target='_blank'>照堂记<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁四年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年6月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221703")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221703_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221703'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221703'>有大圆镜，纵广正等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221703_comment'></div>弥十方界，乃至微尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221703_comment'></div>数莲华藏，世界海中，一切所有，青黄赤白，小大长短，种种色像，于中示现。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221703_comment'></div>如水如眼，如摩尼珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221703_comment'></div>彼种种者，有是色像；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221703_comment'></div>而大圆镜，实无种种。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221703_comment'></div>彼色像者，有去来相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221703_comment'></div>而大圆镜，实无去来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221703_comment'></div>万像俱隐，寂即是照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221703_comment'></div>万像俱现，照即是寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221703_comment'></div>非作故然，无所受故，无取舍故，无分别故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221703_comment'></div>一切众生，各具如是，而大圆镜，以业习故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221703_comment'></div>事理取舍，为自障碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221703_comment'></div>识尘分别，为自盖缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221703_comment'></div>譬如有人，以诸泥涂，种种粪垢，埋裹古镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221703_comment'></div>又复有人，以旃檀末，和雪山泥，装校镜面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221703_comment'></div>是二人者，垢净不同，其于圆镜，等一蔽塞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221703_comment'></div>诸无明者，是粪垢喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221703_comment'></div>诸小法者，是香泥喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221703_comment'></div>皆失本来，真精妙明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221703_comment'></div>有一情念，堕凡圣边，无复是处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221703_comment'></div>诸来佛子，采集缘影，是死生本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221703_comment'></div>勿认此尘，作圆照解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221703_comment'></div>刹那刹那，森罗现前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221703_comment'></div>勿妄思惟，亦无断灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221703_comment'></div>当如我说，大圆镜照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221703_comment'></div>崇宁四年六月庚辰，北山程某为谢原山照堂比丘作如是说<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山小集》卷一八。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1221703'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1221703_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化天王僧舍，中秋前后，感怀赋诗。作品：《山中对酒》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗《北山小集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_526899' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526899' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526899?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山中对酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（乙酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526899")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526899_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526899'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526899'>秋容澹青山，爽秀雨皆足。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526899'>清溪照千仞，空翠疑可掬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526899'>何年顾兔窟，桂子堕山腹。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526899'>老香散深林，屑玉缀黄粟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526899'>朝来客衣动，一叶下空谷。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526899'>客心如棼丝，日月共烦促。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526899'>胸中尚磊块，陶写赖新渌。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526899'>要当酒千钟，浇我愁万斛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526899'>顾有独醒人，脩然倚枯木。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526899_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526899'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_526899_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　冬，寓居衢州开化县灵山寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年12月</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺。张超曾在常山县西驰官道十二里许建斋舍以憩往来客，卒。十二月，县佐崇仁彭君道其事梗概，为之作记。作品：《常山瑞相记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221706' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221706' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221706?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常山瑞相记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221706")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221706_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221706'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221706'>常山县西驰官道十二里许，居人张超饰斋舍道旁，以憩往来客，其严洁如阿兰若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221706_comment'></div>元祐三年十一月十五日，直斋南壁现观音菩萨像及种种物相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221706_comment'></div>初，倏忽莽苍，久之，如水墨然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221706_comment'></div>八年四月八日，复现斋内壁，四十日乃没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221706_comment'></div>凡壁间观音像一，居中，最大，坐石上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221706_comment'></div>见半面，合掌，叠一足，一足下蹋莲华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221706_comment'></div>大石立座后，有物挂其上，如珠璎，如衣带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221706_comment'></div>身光周之上有圆相，圆相中树三，比丘二，其一合掌立，其一拂袖行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221706_comment'></div>观音前猕猴一，举手向莲华下，若欲有所掇者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221706_comment'></div>稍前，师子一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221706_comment'></div>龙钜细四，皆奋拿上腾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221706_comment'></div>其二吐云气，又一龙衡身矫首下顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221706_comment'></div>龙首蛇身者一，亦蜿蜒趣上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221706_comment'></div>人首而异物一，大龙爪足一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221706_comment'></div>又稍前，壁端袍笏而立者一人，错人物间状云气者九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221706_comment'></div>观音后菩萨一，合掌而立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221706_comment'></div>居士二，对坐盘右，其一举手若谈话，其一若合掌听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221706_comment'></div>稍后，师子一，花草株一，猕猴在旁举手若欲摘花者一，龙二，皆妥身衡行，其一卬首，若欲奋者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221706_comment'></div>野人一，若持药草者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221706_comment'></div>稍后，壁端菩萨二，异处，其一若奉物供养他方者，其一合掌立壁之下陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221706_comment'></div>鱼五，其他脉理屈曲交互，如云如水者不胜数而下居多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221706_comment'></div>绍兴四年八月八日，又独现菩萨像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221706_comment'></div>某衢人，少走四方，间归省先陇，又率舟行，未始瞻敬其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221706_comment'></div>崇宁四年冬，客开化县之灵山寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221706_comment'></div>十二月，县佐崇仁彭君挥上谒郡治所，道张氏斋舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221706_comment'></div>时超已死，得其事梗槩，持墨臈本归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221706_comment'></div>他日以示某，某稽首已，说偈赞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1221706'>苇竹以为干，涂垩饰其外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221706_comment'></div>是中无自性，复非镜止水，云何照他方，现此胜境界？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221706_comment'></div>普门天人师，法身无有边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221706_comment'></div>海岸孤绝处，久示常住相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221706_comment'></div>鱼龙共游戏，草木助法音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221706_comment'></div>而此墙壁间，照现恐如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221706_comment'></div>得非妙明发，直见补陀聚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221706_comment'></div>又岂善逝者，断取彼境界，掷过三千刹，影落此土中？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221706_comment'></div>将非佛神通，于一弹指顷，化易殊胜境，纳此墙壁间？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221706_comment'></div>是中虽块陋，同一法海空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221706_comment'></div>其于照他方，正自无障翳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221706_comment'></div>其于纳大地，亦复无留碍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221706_comment'></div>不可思议故，法尔亦如然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221706_comment'></div>我作如是观，如幻人说幻。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1221706_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺，是年结识何蒙圣，或在此年寓居天王僧舍期间，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺，江袖赠酒，有诗谢之。创作地点或在此年寓居天王僧舍期间，姑系于此。作品：《谢江仲举惠酒》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527237' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527237' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527237?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢江仲举惠酒</a><span class='authorDate'>（乙酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527237")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527237_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527237'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527237'>山城无物可忘忧，但有平原病督邮。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527237'>知我囊中无白水，烦君若下出青州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527237'>芳甘未谢三羊酝，傲兀能消万古愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527237'>会待东郊春意动，鸣鞭乘兴草堂游。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527237_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527237'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527237_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺，创作地点或在此年寓居天王僧舍期间，姑系于此。作品：《有美一人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_526913' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526913' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526913?labeling=true' target='_blank'>有美一人<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（乙酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526913")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526913_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526913'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526913'>有美一人在昭君，藕丝为衣兰作裙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526913'>君初顾言淑且真，直欲载以黄金轮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526913'>人心变化如浮云，明妆觉暗笑作颦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526913'>何当还之承华茵，令君宴寝凝清芬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526913_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526913'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526913_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526914' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526914' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526914?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（乙酉）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526914_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526914'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526914'>有美一人在烟汀，朱颜朝涤玉壶冰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526914'>素手暮理朱丝绳。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526914'>语言窈窕丹凤鸣，坐持纨扇睇秋萤。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526914_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526914'>何当还之翡翠屏，为君把镜整衿缨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_526914_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526915' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526915' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526915?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（乙酉）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526915_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526915'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526915'>有美一人在南浦，月明采珠光照渚。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526915'>瑶衣被体金索缕，独抱幽寒沬烟雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526915'>何当置之白玉宇，为君歌阳春激楚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526915'></div><div id='poem_sentence_3_526915_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526915'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_526915_0'>⑴ 原注：“有美一人在南国”以下四首亡。时邹志完在昭州，曾子开在汀州，陈莹中在合浦。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526915_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺时，衢州常山县重建保安院，作文记之。创作地点或在此年寓居天王僧舍期间，姑系于此。作品：《衢州常山县重建保安院记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221698' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221698' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221698?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州常山县重建保安院记<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁四年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221698")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221698_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221698'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221698'>浙江道东尽信安郡，郡接荆、闽地，风气相薄，其山邃以廉，其水清以駃，故其氓俗悍以果，而其君子耿耿尚气敏于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221698_comment'></div>郡之望姓仕族，率占山水之胜以居，而浮屠氏之宫亦复相望原谷间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221698_comment'></div>其所依以为檀施主者，常在所谓望姓仕族，而仕族之广者曰江氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221698_comment'></div>常山县之谢原有僧舍，曰保安院，盖江氏之祖侍御公之所建者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221698_comment'></div>自侍御之世滋远，厦屋日隳，院之徒皆托处养私，不事其教，施施相睨，无所愧念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221698_comment'></div>诸孙戚之，则相与谋，以谓侍御种德不售，庆偿后人，咸克有家，用大芘于兹六世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221698_comment'></div>苟事之弗嗣，其克训于其德者几何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221698_comment'></div>矧是院之建实本于义，乡人能道之，盖非徼福以私己者，诸孙其可罢休以没其德实？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221698_comment'></div>然昔者栋宇故存，而仆者莫起，垫者莫支，至于坏且废，信人开士过之如无睹者，徒非其徒故耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221698_comment'></div>今诚得净修士主而兴之，宜无难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221698_comment'></div>开化报恩院僧文雅，盖净修者，盍请以来？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221698_comment'></div>雅之以身律众，小大斩斩，苗薅垢瀹，日劘月累，凡六年而后成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221698_comment'></div>其基则因故地辟之稍前，又益东筑，革面势以便川谷之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221698_comment'></div>其构则尽去摧腐，一备而新大之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221698_comment'></div>其象偶、其器具咸称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221698_comment'></div>盖为钱若干万，于是距始建百九十馀年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221698_comment'></div>今夫天下之人，自王公至匹夫，居必庐、寒必衣、饥必食，凡所以养生集类者，不取之以其力，则以其道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221698_comment'></div>惟浮屠氏不耕不蚕，不贸不作，安坐放言，而养生之物有须必具而加侈焉，世无与之争者，岂所谓取之以其道者耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221698_comment'></div>使其道可尊，其法可恃，其言可以明理而化物，则其为道也，不素餐兮莫大于是，亦何儒、释之分哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221698_comment'></div>苟无是也，名其名，服其服，安享侈厚，而曰我分盖如是，谓之盗释可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221698_comment'></div>若文雅，一为浮屠，终身守其教戒，又能作其废事，仰而睹其导师，俯而面其众，自称曰浮屠氏，中心无所忸焉，与世之盗道负愧者亦有间矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221698_comment'></div>故余乐为记之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221698_comment'></div>侍御讳景房，字某，仕吴越至侍御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221698_comment'></div>入皇朝，为沁水尉，有高行，为乡里敬信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221698_comment'></div>今开化诸江皆其后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221698_comment'></div>初，里人有讼，累不得直，公贻书吴越执政，道其冤，事得直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221698_comment'></div>里人进金十镒以谢，公笑斥之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221698_comment'></div>里人置金去，终不得辞，则以金买谢原地，立保安院云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221698_comment'></div>崇宁四年某月日，北山程俱记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1221698_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1105&endYear=1105')">1105年</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺时，有感“转徙四方，内外无所营”而赋诗。创作地点或在此年寓居天王僧舍期间，姑系于此。作品：《怀居赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1221281' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221281' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221281?labeling=true' target='_blank'>怀居赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1105年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221281")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221281_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221281'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221281'>士而怀居，弗可以为士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221281_comment'></div>蓬桑之志，见于始生，诚以岁月不可以坐失，力命不可以偏废，此古之圣贤所为汲汲遑遑者已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221281_comment'></div>余转徙四方，实自始生之年，今兹二十有八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221281_comment'></div>上不得谋道，下不得为贫，内外无所营，如病狂东西走者又三年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221281_comment'></div>旦暮将适东，慨然有疲薾之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221281_comment'></div>夫天地之大，春直而冬冥；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221281_comment'></div>昆虫之微，昼动而夜息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221281_comment'></div>余人也，役役曾不得少休，则其怀一日之安亦人之常情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221281_comment'></div>赋曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1221281'>岁作噩兮招摇指辰，戒余舟兮东征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221281_comment'></div>抱衾兮夜喟，接浙兮晨兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221281_comment'></div>逐飞橹兮无蒂，拥敝裘兮悬鹑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221281_comment'></div>山之连兮苍苍，水之駃兮潾潾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221281_comment'></div>我初来东兮芽甲始折，今之还兮甲者奋而芽者荣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221281_comment'></div>顾四时兮几何，嗟汲汲之圜清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221281_comment'></div>天囿余兮不释，亦驰驱而靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221281_comment'></div>余生魏而长吴兮，间蓬转乎四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221281_comment'></div>既侨食乎岐陇兮，又薄游乎宋梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221281_comment'></div>蹑龟峰之奇兮，酌桐江之清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221281_comment'></div>吊采石之英兮，叩灊山之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221281_comment'></div>由褓龀以迄今兮，与日月而竞驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221281_comment'></div>曾谋食之不遂兮，岂云道之敢营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221281_comment'></div>异匏瓜兮可系，羡侏儒之太仓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221281_comment'></div>怀铅刀兮一割，感二鸟之宠光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221281_comment'></div>耕兮不足以卒岁，仕兮不能以安亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221281_comment'></div>徒遑遑兮羁旅，操危心兮若零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221281_comment'></div>乱曰：禀气不妩，命不偶兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221281_comment'></div>进以分寸，退寻丈兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221281_comment'></div>三年以仕，七年饥兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221281_comment'></div>齿发日长，将及壮兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221281_comment'></div>才非卧龙，谁三顾兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221281_comment'></div>名谢文虎，无三书兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221281_comment'></div>笑长年之贫贱兮，悼道德之初心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221281_comment'></div>托妻孥于昏友兮，奉亲闱以北南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221281_comment'></div>怅宇宙之浩莫兮，茫不知乎安止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221281_comment'></div>仰浮云之苍漭兮，望白日之骎骎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221281_comment'></div>吾穷死其无憾兮，岂为余而咿喑也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1221281_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221281'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_30_1221281_0'>⑴ 孔明相玄德及韩愈登第时皆年二十八矣，退之登第时又谓之龙虎榜。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1221281_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年8月5日</a>　寓居衢州开化灵山寺，八月五日，为安养庵作记。作品：《安养庵记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221704' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221704' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221704?labeling=true' target='_blank'>安养庵记<span class='inlineComment2'>（崇宁五年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年8月5日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221704")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221704_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221704'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221704'>河沙刹中，有一世界，号安养国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221704_comment'></div>其国有无量寿如来，应供正遍，知明行足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221704_comment'></div>善逝世间，解无上士，调御丈夫天人，师佛世尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221704_comment'></div>其国境界，皆以七宝，装饰成就，广博严事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221704_comment'></div>其国众生，皆是宿具福智，化生莲中，住不退地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221704_comment'></div>其国寿命，无有边量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221704_comment'></div>一日一夜，此土一劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221704_comment'></div>其国六时，皆有天乐，微妙音声，及雨宝华，而共娱乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221704_comment'></div>其国花木，皆是莲华，如车轮大，及宝行树，交映周彻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221704_comment'></div>其国鸣禽，皆是如来变化所作，于一切时，演无量义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221704_comment'></div>以是种种，希有之事，故名安养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221704_comment'></div>从是安养国东方，过十万亿国土，有世界号曰娑婆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221704_comment'></div>诸国土中，无数伽蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221704_comment'></div>有一伽蓝，曰灵山聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221704_comment'></div>复有精舍，号安养庵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221704_comment'></div>是中有人，衣壤色衣，净除须发，处乞士众，名曰修意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221704_comment'></div>是庵无有七宝严事，但有墙壁栋宇，山溪丘坎，为其境界。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221704_comment'></div>是庵无有化生莲中，但有胎卵湿化，诸有情类，为其众生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221704_comment'></div>是庵无有无边寿命，但有五十七十，乃至百岁，为其寿限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221704_comment'></div>是庵六时无有雨华及诸天乐，但于昼夜餐饭食粥，撞钟击鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221704_comment'></div>是庵周匝，无有宝树及大莲华，但见山中，草木华茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221704_comment'></div>是庵无有变化众鸟演无量义，但闻虫鸟，自鸣自已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221704_comment'></div>以是现前，种种之事，亦名安养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221704_comment'></div>是乞士者，诸国土，亲事知识，得法藏已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221704_comment'></div>受用自在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221704_comment'></div>还归北山，结庵安居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221704_comment'></div>时北山中，有一居士，适游伽蓝，至安养庵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221704_comment'></div>谓大众言：现前种种，如上所说，与安养国，为一为异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221704_comment'></div>若作异见，断佛种子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221704_comment'></div>若作同见，是魔眷属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221704_comment'></div>安养世界，在一切处，而一切处，非安养国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221704_comment'></div>若作断见，彼释迦文，宁为虚语？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221704_comment'></div>若取法相，汝则孤负，无量寿尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221704_comment'></div>咄诸男子，各依位住，坐大道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221704_comment'></div>如不信承，请诣毗耶离城，当俟螺发梵王，为汝解说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221704_comment'></div>崇宁五年八月甲子，北山程俱记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1221704_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　寓居衢州开化县灵山寺，秋夜感怀作诗。作品：《山中秋夜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_526917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>山中秋夜</a><span class='authorDate'>（丙戌）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526917")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526917'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526917'>夜气挟秋至，飔然出户庭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526917'>空山答清漏，客梦忽以醒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526917'>林梢月未堕，流光委疏棂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526917'>冷露湿山桂，寒蕤动幽馨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526917'>整衣坐蒲团，破屋呈稀星。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526917'>我身<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作生）</span>本无涯，寒暑饱所经。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526917'>以彼泡电境，劳此草木形。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526917'>吾犹昔人耳，不与寒暑并。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526917'>蘧然返初枕，人境已两冥。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526917'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_526917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1106&endYear=1106')">1106年</a>　寓居衢州开化灵山寺，为灵山寺转轮经藏作记。作品：《衢州开化县灵山寺大藏记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221700' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221700' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221700?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州开化县灵山寺大藏记</a><span class='authorDate'>（1106年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221700")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221700_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221700'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221700'>寿圣灵山寺在开化为大僧坊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221700_comment'></div>崇宁元年，其徒从演始建转轮经藏，奔走勤事，五年而后成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221700_comment'></div>下固上壮，爽博宏致，校饰众具，炜奕严好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221700_comment'></div>圣像法籍，俨如化成，屹如宝聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221700_comment'></div>邑人程俱来至其所，竦仰正伫，说偈称赞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221700_comment'></div>演故具石宇下，来请记矣，遂以文其碑云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221700_comment'></div>其词曰：世界无尽如虚空，是故诸佛亦无尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221700_comment'></div>佛既无尽法亦尔，于诸缘起而出生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221700_comment'></div>我观清净法门海，十方导尊常演说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221700_comment'></div>一一念中一一说，如是展转难思劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221700_comment'></div>正使众生无数量，皆获三昧闻持藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221700_comment'></div>于此导尊所说法，不能共记一品义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221700_comment'></div>设复笔高须弥聚，濡以万亿恒河水，等三千界大经卷，不能书佛所说法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221700_comment'></div>那由他中一少分，况此五千四十卷，何异大地一尘末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221700_comment'></div>人中师子无畏者，于第一义安不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221700_comment'></div>如斯清净法门海，一言演说尽无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221700_comment'></div>正使一切诸众生，皆获智慧三昧海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221700_comment'></div>不能了此一言者，思惟究竟云何说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221700_comment'></div>设复毛端滴海尽，此诸水滴可知数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221700_comment'></div>乃至微尘悉可知，叵思议此甚深法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221700_comment'></div>则是五千四十卷，一字一句法无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221700_comment'></div>我今普愿群生类，皆获摩诃法宝藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221700_comment'></div>真如实际以为地，覆以喜舍慈哀宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221700_comment'></div>清净平等之大轮，贯以忍力金刚轴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221700_comment'></div>无碍机关极明利，运以解脱神通力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221700_comment'></div>菩萨心珠饰其上，一一常放大智光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221700_comment'></div>种种方便为华鬘，妙行缯䌽为幡盖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221700_comment'></div>七净之华以为网，梵音深妙为宝铃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221700_comment'></div>涂以大愿功德香，布以觉分菡萏华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221700_comment'></div>护以方等调柔帙，百千三昧为实函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221700_comment'></div>中有无尽陀罗尼，非生盲人所能睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221700_comment'></div>如我今者如是说，所说如幻说如响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221700_comment'></div>若人于此一大教，初心回向如来藏，是人已获无碍智，是知诸佛秘密说。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1221700_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='a48f4999dd0d4b5d9b311f13c28f00f9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a48f4999dd0d4b5d9b311f13c28f00f9");'><span id='a48f4999dd0d4b5d9b311f13c28f00f9_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1108')">1107-1108年</a>，30-31岁</div><div id='a48f4999dd0d4b5d9b311f13c28f00f9' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，归省松楸。会僧修意于衢州开化灵山寺。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年4月1日</a>　在监常州市易务任上，归省松楸，居衢州开化。四月一日，代表叔王涣之作文。作品：《衢州溪桥记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221705' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221705' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221705?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州溪桥记<span class='inlineComment2'>（为王八侍郎作。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221705")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221705_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221705'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221705'>衢之为郡，郊邑疆理错处众山间，大溪贯其中，东会浙江入于海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221705_comment'></div>其源实出岩谷畎涧，至郡城始大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221705_comment'></div>郡西三邑之人输赋租、走期会、适市井，与行旅之出入荆闽者，皆绝溪往来，深则杭，浅则揭以涉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221705_comment'></div>春夏积雨，四山之水从地出，所谓岩谷畎涧之流与大溪相吞激，势益张怒，操舟绝流，失毫发便辄覆溺漂转，漫不见踪迹，人皆病之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221705_comment'></div>大观元年，邦人相与谋跨溪为梁，裒其材用于众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221705_comment'></div>越明年春三月，梁成，凡三十五架，其修二百六十步，会其费庸为钱四百万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221705_comment'></div>于是负乘扶携，往来不择昼夜，虽大水时至，安如平地然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221705_comment'></div>有为邦人请于余者曰：「衢，公之故乡，溪桥之功，衢之大利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221705_comment'></div>公不书，无以示来者，俾知始事之勤与溪桥之有无利害也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221705_comment'></div>则叙其所以，畀刻诸石焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221705_comment'></div>二年夏四月辛巳，显谟阁待制、荆湖南路安抚使王涣之记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1221705_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2c977f5c534f4072aac367a734e39872_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2c977f5c534f4072aac367a734e39872");'><span id='2c977f5c534f4072aac367a734e39872_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1133')">1132-1133年</a>，55-56岁</div><div id='2c977f5c534f4072aac367a734e39872' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　回乡后，上谢表。时寓居衢州开化云门院。作品：《提举江州太平观谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。清《浙江通志》二百三十三《寺观.衢州府.开化县》载：“云门院：《衢州府志》在县西云台乡，宋开宝中建，程俱退寓于此。”）</span><div id='poem_1221537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221537?labeling=true' target='_blank'>提举江州太平观谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221537")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221537'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221537'>臣某言：臣昨任中书舍人，二月二十二日，准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，罢中书舍人，提举江州太平观，任便居住，仍免谢辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221537_comment'></div>臣于当日出门，至本贯衢州开化县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221537_comment'></div>寻准告命，已祗受讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221537_comment'></div>承乏冒荣，久知非据；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221537_comment'></div>罪深责薄，仰戴厚恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221537_comment'></div>感极涕零，扪心增惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221537_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221537_comment'></div>伏念臣戆迂成性，忧患俱生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221537_comment'></div>无乘机应变之才，有至愚极陋之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221537_comment'></div>束发从仕，浪怀畎亩之忠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221537_comment'></div>诣阙上书，妄陈蠡管之见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221537_comment'></div>少不历事，愚无所知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221537_comment'></div>方权臣立党以锢人，而以谓当两忘元祐、熙丰之别；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221537_comment'></div>省檄讲求于遗利，而以谓不若罢明金、花石之纲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221537_comment'></div>虽云应诏以献言，要为越职而多事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221537_comment'></div>栖迟选调，盖十六年；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221537_comment'></div>出入效官，于今三纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221537_comment'></div>晚逢圣主，误被睿知，召从田庐，亟寘词掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221537_comment'></div>夫以权德舆之器业，李卫公之才猷，宋绶之该通，韩维之方格，乃始不由科第，自致清华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221537_comment'></div>又若杨大年之一世英豪，欧阳修之诸儒领袖，安石之经术，苏轼之文章，故皆不待试言，径司辞命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221537_comment'></div>如臣何者，滥继前修，续貂之诮是惭，窥豹之知曷有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221537_comment'></div>以兹感激，誓竭铅驽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221537_comment'></div>念平生爱君忧国之诚，傥庶几千虑一得之效，居怀尸素之惧，窃恃奖知之私，每有陈论，颇蒙采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221537_comment'></div>迄缘蜚语，暴著宿愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221537_comment'></div>职在守符，不能效死而弗去；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221537_comment'></div>时方奋武，是宜明罚以示惩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221537_comment'></div>罪檗久萌，骇机当发，尚沾微禄，畀侍殊庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221537_comment'></div>复雁门之踦，虽非素望；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221537_comment'></div>失常山之守，仰繄曲全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221537_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下稽古聪明，遵王好恶，每于刑政之举，不忘忠厚之思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221537_comment'></div>致此懦庸，终繄宽惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221537_comment'></div>臣敢不抚躬知感，齰舌省愆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221537_comment'></div>年迫桑榆，无复报恩之所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221537_comment'></div>身依松槚，长为侥幸之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221537_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221537_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_35_1221537_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>　寓居衢州开化云门院期间，春，拜访僧修意，时修意病且衰矣。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年7月16日</a>　寓居衢州开化云门院期间，七月十六日夜月蚀，有诗。作品：《壬子七月十六日夜月蚀五首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527489' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527489' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527489?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬子七月十六日夜月蚀五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span
