id='poem_sentence_1_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527180'>闭门得长哦，有酒或细倾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527180'>谁云千里隔，回薄万古情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527180'>驾言从公游，上马短策横。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527180'>尘缨缚我急，有足安得行。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527180'>何当来上都，既见心始平。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527180'>为公赋三秋，寤叹空营营。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527180_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527180'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527180_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527181' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527181' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527181?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>同许学士亢宗干誉汎舟潩水</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527181_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527181'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527181'>往者巾柴车，追游卞山村。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527181'>今焉镇三辅，鼓吹喧谯门。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527181'>遥知手种松，浸有苍苔痕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527181'>许下今乐郊，胜事亦复繁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527181'>但令足兵食，饱暖同君恩。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527181'>长安举头见，煌煌太微垣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527181'>江湖与魏阙，一一寄默存。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527181'>正恐受釐室，虚怀待微言。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527181_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527181'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527181_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527182' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527182' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527182?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>同许学士亢宗干誉汎舟潩水</a><span class='authorDate'>（1118年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527182_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527182'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527182'>许侯盖静者，无乃祖远游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527182'>着身朝市间，深若无所求。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527182'>命驾眇千里，西湖正凉秋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527182'>是中有真趣，轩裳何悠悠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527182'>潩水清且姝，仙舟度深幽。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527182'>徐行问疾苦，怀新想平畴。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527182'>坐念方外乐，馋涎曲车流。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527182'>持觞会相属，我唱公当酬。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527182_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527182'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527182_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1118&endYear=1118')">1118年</a>　在汴京编修国朝会要所检阅文字任上。是年前后，生子行敏。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　转承议郎，赐五品服，时在汴京编修国朝会要所检阅文字任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1119&endYear=1119')">1119年</a>　为姊夫朱耜作墓志铭，时在汴京编修国朝会要所检阅文字任上。作品：《宣义郎知常州江阴县朱君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十二。）</span><div id='poem_1221794' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221794' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221794?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣义郎知常州江阴县朱君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和元年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221794")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221794_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221794'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221794'>公讳耜，字元益，吴郡吴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221794_comment'></div>曾大父讳亿，内殿崇班、閤门祗候，知邕州，赠刑部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221794_comment'></div>大父讳公绰，光禄卿，赠特进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221794_comment'></div>父讳长文，秘书省正字，博学笃行，以道出处，为时老儒，吴人尊之，号乐圃先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221794_comment'></div>元益幼以大父任补太庙斋郎，弱冠，赴吏部别试为第一，调婺州东阳主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221794_comment'></div>丁父忧，终丧，为杭州盐官尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221794_comment'></div>坐蝗蝻生境内免，再调鄂州江夏尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221794_comment'></div>以捕盗功迁宣义郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221794_comment'></div>丁母夫人夏氏忧，终丧，为太原府司录，不行，改知常州江阴县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221794_comment'></div>秩满代还，卒京师，实政和七年四月四日，享年四十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221794_comment'></div>元配程氏，我先人之仲女，淑慧过人，秀而不实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221794_comment'></div>继室顾氏，朝请大夫沂之女，婉懿有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221794_comment'></div>生四男子，曰愈、悫、懋，其一未名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221794_comment'></div>二女子，未嫁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221794_comment'></div>顾夫人前卒，既葬吴县至德乡南峰山龙池之西矣，至是以公之柩合葬焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221794_comment'></div>葬之日，实宣和元年二月三十日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221794_comment'></div>其弟通直郎、宗子学录发以状请铭于俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221794_comment'></div>俱获友于元益，于今二十八年矣，相与之厚，如元益者世无几人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221794_comment'></div>初，仲姊归朱氏，年始十六，元益齿先一岁，余固童子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221794_comment'></div>正字公有风裁，喜奖诱后学，目余奇童，或举余以励其子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221794_comment'></div>元益既亲厚，相与友又善也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221794_comment'></div>方是时，正字俾公专意于学，训饬如严师，子职之外，未尝与事接，余知其为良子弟而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221794_comment'></div>一旦出为吏，乃得东阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221794_comment'></div>东阳天下剧邑，元益年甚少，适行县令事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221794_comment'></div>余尝道至其邑省吾姊，庭讼日阅数百人，或杖或遣，或付曹对辩，斯须尽决，要为无所凝滞，而后知公可试以事也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221794_comment'></div>元益与人无所忤，犯而不校，循循不见圭角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221794_comment'></div>然在东阳时，县令有所施置，便于人而不可于上官者，僚佐不敢从，元益欣然书字唯谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221794_comment'></div>以父丧去官，时行义乌令，僚吏邑豪知其贫，率缣帛数百以赙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221794_comment'></div>元益毅然挥之，至追路数十百里，卒不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221794_comment'></div>尉盐官，岁久不雨，伤人田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221794_comment'></div>俾公行视，尽复旱田之赋，十蠲八九，计使不能以意夺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221794_comment'></div>余闻之，然后知公之自立如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221794_comment'></div>元益天姿近道，行官自江西回，会余于吴下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221794_comment'></div>观其外毁誉、甘澹泊，颓然加昔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221794_comment'></div>家益贫，不汲汲于禄仕，家人迫之行，裹粮而西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221794_comment'></div>遇亲故留辄移日，未尝接淅于路也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221794_comment'></div>盖所谓推而后行，曳而后往，若古之弃知云已者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221794_comment'></div>及为江阴，其政亦如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221794_comment'></div>然其爱物循理，不为扰人趣办以徼利一切者自若也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221794_comment'></div>至于乐善善，与人交，称士友所长，津津喜见颜间，若己预有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221794_comment'></div>客至，相与道古今、阅图史，怡然终日而不厌；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221794_comment'></div>兄弟同甘苦，衎衎如也，则正字之风流馀范犹有存云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221794_comment'></div>江阴令圭田租岁责八百斛，至元益按实取入，又会无年，伐归，室中犹四壁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221794_comment'></div>其遗孤闻讣假贷，乃能具丧服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221794_comment'></div>自元益之逝踰年矣，余言之未尝不出涕焉，非直以亲厚然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221794_comment'></div>铭其可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221794_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1221794'>九卿之门，实望吴下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221794_comment'></div>德名孔振，大自乐圃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221794_comment'></div>奕奕江阴，尚有其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221794_comment'></div>好古慕善，歉如渴饥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221794_comment'></div>亦持厥躬，淳白无悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221794_comment'></div>泛然有施，若退若昧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221794_comment'></div>我思旧交，契阔无几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221794_comment'></div>矧伊吉人，奇阨终世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221794_comment'></div>南峰之游，今子是藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221794_comment'></div>我怀之悲，寄此铭章。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1221794_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　在汴京编修国朝会要所检阅文字任上，为江大方作墓志铭，时间当在九月二十日与十一月五日之间。作品：《江器博墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1221800' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221800' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221800?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江器博墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221800")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221800_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221800'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221800'>江公讳大方，字器博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221800_comment'></div>江氏为信安望族，家世群从皆以业儒起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221800_comment'></div>大理评事讳相者，公之考也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221800_comment'></div>器博少多病，即从父兄丐其身，求异人方士，问卫生养性之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221800_comment'></div>学鼓琴隶书，有能名，精于是技者皆推下之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221800_comment'></div>筑室钱塘西湖上，间奕棋以自娱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221800_comment'></div>士之萧散旷达者，行李出于钱塘，往往从之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221800_comment'></div>中年生计益落，弃所居归故乡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221800_comment'></div>然浮寓去来，不能土着。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221800_comment'></div>故人与之厚，欲经纪其衣食者，遇辄死徙忧患，否则以事去官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221800_comment'></div>器博游益困，客吴中，无所遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221800_comment'></div>故延康殿学士、信安侯兄弟以乡里旧，以其兄彦楚之子妻其子参，留家南徐，居有庐，月有馈，公以是少休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221800_comment'></div>宣和二年九月二十日，以疾终于家，享年七十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221800_comment'></div>器博姿淳壹，与人无町畦，口不道世故，众座谈说是非如不闻，亦不省顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221800_comment'></div>尝为余言，少遇道人，授以内丹诀，当立静以月日时下，不以毫发累心，养之数年，庶有成，今日有饥寒迫，未可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221800_comment'></div>余叹曰：「公且老，岁月逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221800_comment'></div>使我得官南徐，治一室，如公言，为任衣食事，丹幸成，其授我诀」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221800_comment'></div>明年，余得倅镇江，私喜曰：「器博之言庶有合乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221800_comment'></div>未到，有改命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221800_comment'></div>后五年而公卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221800_comment'></div>参为余言，公病即不食，喜饮水，曰「吾梦游三茅，甚乐其死，顶热如火」云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221800_comment'></div>公有六男一女，曰某、某、某、某，与女子先卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221800_comment'></div>曰参，曰履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221800_comment'></div>以十一月五日葬公丹徒县金鼎山下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221800_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_1221800'>不昏若可以无累，不宦若可以为高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221800_comment'></div>绝学捐书，以游以遨，若可以度浊世而解天韬，而卒以不遭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221800_comment'></div>釜鼎之南，郁然三茅，其藏者形存，其梦者神交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221800_comment'></div>岂大块于此，息夫子之劳乎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1221800_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年12月24日</a>　迁秘书省著作佐郎，十二月二十四日，赐上舍出身，时在汴京。作品：《谢著作佐郎启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十一。）</span><div id='poem_1221633' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221633' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221633?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢著作佐郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1120年12月24日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221633")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221633_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221633'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221633'>半世江湖，无复弹冠之意；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221633_comment'></div>薄游都邑，居怀索米之惭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221633_comment'></div>敢期瓦砾之馀，谬玷丝纶之渥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221633_comment'></div>所蒙非据，以宠为虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221633_comment'></div>窃以中古以还，倚儒而治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221633_comment'></div>以谓用非所养，则遇事或难于任重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221633_comment'></div>学优而仕，则立朝无愧于面墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221633_comment'></div>苟陵阿之育未加，则薪槱之图曷继。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221633_comment'></div>故有绝编已老，莫知经济之方；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221633_comment'></div>素官称贤，或出草茅之士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221633_comment'></div>顾谁差之不预，岂才智之可诬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221633_comment'></div>是故祖宗以典籍之司，以为公卿与侍从之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221633_comment'></div>期奖成于望实，斯致慎于柬求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221633_comment'></div>以褎然晁、董之流，犹试言而后授；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221633_comment'></div>虽卓尔轲、雄之学，有陈义而力辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221633_comment'></div>人唯允谐，世则知贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221633_comment'></div>典坟具在，纵观海宇之奇书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221633_comment'></div>策牍兼资，多识朝廷之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221633_comment'></div>抑磨砻其器质，且殚洽其见闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221633_comment'></div>或许从宴间之游，或访以图回之务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221633_comment'></div>唯其养之有素，则亦用之弗疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221633_comment'></div>鸿惟上圣之临，益著右文之效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221633_comment'></div>股肱心膂，既相与立太平之基；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221633_comment'></div>杞梓圭璋，又兼收为无穷之用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221633_comment'></div>来英髦于数路，达遗滞于四聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221633_comment'></div>云构百梁，屹天衢之左界；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221633_comment'></div>龙章八法，焕紫殿之中居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221633_comment'></div>俨群玉之大开，仰奎文之下属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221633_comment'></div>合三馆一时之彦，登瀛洲者十有八人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221633_comment'></div>续六官九聚之书，䌷金匮于数千百载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221633_comment'></div>惟兰台之接武，实麟止之椎轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221633_comment'></div>文若孟坚，徒为令史；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221633_comment'></div>博如束皙，仅得佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221633_comment'></div>然裁成汉代之阳秋，无出其右；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221633_comment'></div>比次汲书之科斗，可考而知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221633_comment'></div>自非宏达之才，曷称招延之美？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221633_comment'></div>如某钝顽无似，孤贱数奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221633_comment'></div>早迷速化之方，几成独学之陋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221633_comment'></div>束发为养，华首益穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221633_comment'></div>尝闻君子长者之风，每尽乘田委吏之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221633_comment'></div>窃信简编之载，妄兴圳亩之怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221633_comment'></div>时非弗逢，事或大谬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221633_comment'></div>一官不偶，遂将归老圃之畴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221633_comment'></div>二顷无田，又时为禄仕之隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221633_comment'></div>实委心于穷达，聊寄适于艺文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221633_comment'></div>若将终身，奚暇外慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221633_comment'></div>何图名姓，误辱搜扬，释其州县之劳，命以编摩之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221633_comment'></div>逮从匠属，复厕英游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221633_comment'></div>况举袂成帷，时固多于俊异；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221633_comment'></div>而上车不落，独何取于惷庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221633_comment'></div>此盖某官斧藻圣猷，帡幪士类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221633_comment'></div>索渊微于系表，应事物于道枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221633_comment'></div>学该今古，而不忽于寸长；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221633_comment'></div>用周小大，而兼容于众善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221633_comment'></div>致兹连蹇，稍与选抡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221633_comment'></div>念固穷难进之馀，粗知分义；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221633_comment'></div>当省官遴选之际，尤觉叨踰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221633_comment'></div>敢不稍缉旧闻，益坚素守，仰副甄收之本意，永衔温厚之华褒！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221633_comment'></div>诚知背上之毛，何加于六翮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221633_comment'></div>傥比管中之豹，时见于一斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221633_comment'></div>过此以还，未知所措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_60_1221633_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1120&endYear=1120')">1120年</a>　迁秘书省著作佐郎，赐上舍出身，时在汴京。叶梦得道贺，有诗酬之。作品：《酬叶翰林喜某除官东观》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527284' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在汴京礼部员外郎任上，为吴中二老方子通、杨懿孺作墓志铭。作品：《莆阳方子通墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十三。）</span>《承奉郎致仕杨君墓铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1221799' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221799' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221799?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莆阳方子通墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和四年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221799")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221799_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221799'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221799'>宣和四年正月庚辰，兴化方公卒吴下，享年八十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221799_comment'></div>以三月乙亥葬于长洲武丘乡汝坟湖西先茔之南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221799_comment'></div>其婿奉议郎、亲贤宅讲书朱发请铭于史官尚书礼部员外郎程某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221799_comment'></div>某以不佞辞，不获，则叙而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221799_comment'></div>公讳惟深，字子通，世为莆阳人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221799_comment'></div>考讳龟年，终尚书屯田员外郎，葬吴，因留家不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221799_comment'></div>公生挺特，幼为文见称乡长者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221799_comment'></div>长则端敏，涵养滋大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221799_comment'></div>乡贡为第一，试礼部不第，即弃去吴下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221799_comment'></div>有田一廛，公与其弟躬出入耕穫，凡衣食之具，一毫必自己力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221799_comment'></div>间则读书，非苟诵其言而已也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221799_comment'></div>至于黄帝老庄之书，养生为寿者之说，其户庭堂奥、根源派别无不知，其所操之要则曰无为而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221799_comment'></div>于西方别传得其大指，不数为人剧谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221799_comment'></div>平居视之，犹欺魄木鸡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221799_comment'></div>及其论议古今道理，穷覈至到，确然莫能移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221799_comment'></div>然常以雅道自娱，一篇出，人传诵以熟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221799_comment'></div>舒王以知制诰卧钟山，得其诗，以谓精诣警绝，元、白、皮、陆有不到处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221799_comment'></div>方元丰、元祐间，公贤益闻，以韦布之士闭关陋巷，躬行不言，而孝友清介之风隐然称东南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221799_comment'></div>时朱先生长文隐乐圃，二人皆以学术为乡先生，士之往来吴下者至必礼于其庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221799_comment'></div>朱公晚起为太学博士，卒三馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221799_comment'></div>公后死三十年，然世终莫得而挽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221799_comment'></div>元符初，孙集贤杰以郎官使淮浙，风采震慑州郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221799_comment'></div>入境，遣从事问讯，且邀见，公辞焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221799_comment'></div>孙公至苏，即日造公门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221799_comment'></div>归荐诸朝，虽知公之不可以吏也，以谓善人国之纪、人之望也，庶几旌善人以风士类乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221799_comment'></div>辄报闻罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221799_comment'></div>崇宁中，诏举遗逸，蒲轮走四方，二浙特起无虚郡，吴以公应诏，人以为处士之雄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221799_comment'></div>复报闻罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221799_comment'></div>时宰相皆公故人，岂意其不可以起也，弗强焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221799_comment'></div>崇宁某年，有司举贡籍，以年格应补军州助教者，就赐敕牒袍笏于其家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221799_comment'></div>公得兴化军助教，命且至，或覸之曰：「是其志视轩裳圭组亡如也，何助教云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221799_comment'></div>是必辞」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221799_comment'></div>公曰：「君命也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221799_comment'></div>拜受唯谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221799_comment'></div>公长不踰中人，貌古骨强，目光如冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221799_comment'></div>居亲侧洞洞属属，兄弟訚訚如也，交际色勃如也，足躩如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221799_comment'></div>其岁时祭享自涤除，水火之役身先之，盖至老不变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221799_comment'></div>闾里庆吊，每先众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221799_comment'></div>其酬应曲折，虽小夫孺子，如见所畏者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221799_comment'></div>至于王公贵人，去就疏数，或见或不见，皆有辞，非苟然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221799_comment'></div>或曰：「公信无求于世矣，何自苦为是拘拘者邪」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221799_comment'></div>呜呼，是所以为方子已矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221799_comment'></div>夫以亢为高，以随为通，以放为达，以无忌惮为果，其似而非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221799_comment'></div>譬之䵷紫也，足以眩盲聋而不可以欺娄旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221799_comment'></div>且仁与礼，君子所不可斯须离者也，而谓处士可以去之乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221799_comment'></div>公初年四十，无子，其弟有子，以谓吾先人有后足矣，即屏居于外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221799_comment'></div>平生深于诗，遇得意，欣然忘食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221799_comment'></div>中年忽若有所不乐者，因绝笔不道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221799_comment'></div>夫卓绝之行可能，而常因循于所易；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221799_comment'></div>死生之决有不顾，而不能忘怀于嗜习，余于此知公之刚果绝人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221799_comment'></div>公预知死期，期至不乱，丧葬皆有治命云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221799_comment'></div>集其诗文为五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221799_comment'></div>母赵氏，参知政事文安公安仁之女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221799_comment'></div>继母王氏，封长寿县君，宣州观察使得一之孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221799_comment'></div>妻建安吴氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221799_comment'></div>公之葬，合诸吴氏之圹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221799_comment'></div>二女，长嫁郏杰而卒，季嫁乐圃先生之仲子发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221799_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_57_1221799'>猗欤方公，行峻而礼恭，徒人而志独，学该而守约，吴越之瞻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221799_comment'></div>一介不以与人，非以为俭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221799_comment'></div>一介不以取诸人，非以为廉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221799_comment'></div>盖妄取害于义，妄与害于仁，造端于取与之微，而贤否之分不容发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221799_comment'></div>故君子于此，若是其严也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221799_comment'></div>古之人有眇六合以为隘，捐一瓢以为烦，是以遁世绝迹，穷苦其身而不悔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221799_comment'></div>故独善、济物，不可得而兼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221799_comment'></div>虽位三旌、马千驷，吾知其不以烦浊易安恬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221799_comment'></div>之人所以怀宝不试，宁老死而伏嵁岩也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1221799_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221801' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221801' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221801?labeling=true' target='_blank'>承奉郎致仕杨君墓铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221801")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221801_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221801'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221801'>吴郡有二老焉，或仕或不仕，皆隐者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221801_comment'></div>居城之东北曰方公，居城之东南曰杨公，余少壮客吴下获交焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221801_comment'></div>宣和四年春，二老相继没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221801_comment'></div>方氏既以铭为请，杨公之没实二月丁巳，以九月辛酉葬于长洲县武丘乡祖兴墩之原矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221801_comment'></div>其子友夔始克状公行实，走书京师曰：「葬当有铭，地远不时请，既埳以俟，非公无以图不朽」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221801_comment'></div>余不佞，束发行四方，所交往往天下善士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221801_comment'></div>今吴有二老，生相从游，死志其墓，其又何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221801_comment'></div>矧所谓发潜德之幽光者，亦余之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221801_comment'></div>公讳懿孺，字彝父，世为建州浦城人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221801_comment'></div>曾祖有證，赠太仆少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221801_comment'></div>祖伉，赠光禄卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221801_comment'></div>父讳，尚书屯田员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221801_comment'></div>屯田始葬常州无锡县，诸孤因家长洲，遂为吴郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221801_comment'></div>公少孤，能自力学，长为进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221801_comment'></div>家素贫，事母尽孝养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221801_comment'></div>言行相顾，疾恶无隐情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221801_comment'></div>宗族有疑，咨而后决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221801_comment'></div>其子弟有过失者，踧踖不敢见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221801_comment'></div>既丧亲，生事益废，朝无夕储。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221801_comment'></div>家人以告，公方读书，哦诗泊如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221801_comment'></div>猝然遇之，神夷气昌，剧谈大笑，未尝有饥寒忧，虽闾里不尽知其贫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221801_comment'></div>凡三预乡贡，五试礼部，卒不第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221801_comment'></div>崇宁二年特奏名，始授简州文学，监杭州富阳县茶场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221801_comment'></div>遇郊恩，以将仕郎权亳州城父县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221801_comment'></div>八宝汎恩，迁登仕郎，调洪州南昌县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221801_comment'></div>居一年，忽载妻子归吴下，且告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221801_comment'></div>今中书侍郎清河公时守洪州，与部使者固留，皆荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221801_comment'></div>公辞，不听，不得已求沿檄浙西，至则复告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221801_comment'></div>奏下，以承奉郎致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221801_comment'></div>又七年，乃卒，年七十有六，属纩不乱如平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221801_comment'></div>公年艾耆始禄仕，平居直心自信，不知世间有倾巧事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221801_comment'></div>见用于州县者或纤利导谀，否则害人以自便，辄眙𥈭却立，退或以言劘切之，以是益不喜为吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221801_comment'></div>自未仕及老于家，不入州县，不事乡里请谒，间一过所亲厚，岁不过数四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221801_comment'></div>客至，相与辨论古今或终日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221801_comment'></div>性简介，见其状貌，知非俯仰人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221801_comment'></div>虽尝出而仕，余犹谓隐者云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221801_comment'></div>娶章氏，甚勤以和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221801_comment'></div>二男，曰友益，先公三十七日卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221801_comment'></div>曰友夔，能文，有志操。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221801_comment'></div>一女，嫁修武郎侍其佃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221801_comment'></div>二孙，曰瞻，曰睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221801_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_41_1221801'>行险狙利，荣犹辱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221801_comment'></div>和光处顺，群犹独也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221801_comment'></div>五试三仕，仕以禄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221801_comment'></div>其隐者存，安且谷也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_44_1221801_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在汴京礼部员外郎任上，驾幸秘书省，特旨召观书阁下，因赐御笔书画，迁朝奉郎。作品：《车驾幸秘书省口号》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span>《宣和御书赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十六。）</span>《宣和御画赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_527293' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527293' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527293?labeling=true' target='_blank'>车驾幸袐书省口号<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首　壬寅）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527293")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527293_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527293'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527293'>端门清跸隐修廊，麟省新开接建章。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527293'>六玉虬飞黄道稳，五芝华耸赪袍光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527293'>风生凡腋天颜近，春入仙洲昼漏长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527293'>拭目训词成饱德，共瞻云日仰陶唐。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527293_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527293'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527293_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527294' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527294' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527294?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527294_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527294'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527294'>清尘膏雨浃人寰，金殿晴开瑞雾间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527294'>帝座腾辉临璧府，飙轮纡景按蓬山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527294'>龙鸾初识昭回迹，麑鹿惊随侍从班。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527294'>再拜逡巡戴君赐，却迎天仗款贤关。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527294_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527294'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527294_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221730' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221730' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221730?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣和御书赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221730")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221730_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221730'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221730'>灵交结空，秘瑛房也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221730_comment'></div>大有在上，俯云章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221730_comment'></div>羲图颉迹，寄明光也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221730_comment'></div>臣俱宝之，泽莫长也<span class='inlineComment2'>（行书。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221730_comment'></div>如龙行天，或游或飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221730_comment'></div>其驰不迫，其静不迟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221730_comment'></div>盖从容八法者，犹严恭而自度；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221730_comment'></div>其超忽万变者，犹应物之神机乎<span class='inlineComment2'>（草书）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221730_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1221730_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221731' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221731' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221731?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宣和御画赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221731")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1221731_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221731'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221731'>太虚混沦，滋象之先。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1221731'>无动而生，万汇出焉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1221731'>巍巍道尊，实主张是。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1221731'>芒乎芴乎，无择巨细。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1221731'>是翾飞者，与彼有筠。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1221731'>如马一毛，如地一尘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1221731'>凡有形相，寄此笔端。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1221731'>造化之妙，毋以尽观。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1221731_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1221731'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1221731_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1122&endYear=1122')">1122年</a>　在汴京礼部员外郎任上，驾幸秘书省，特旨召观书阁下，因赐在汴京礼部员外郎任上，御笔书画，迁朝奉郎。作品：《谢赐御书御画并宣召观书画表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_1221532' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221532' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221532?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谢赐御书御画并宣召观书画表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1122年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221532")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221532_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221532'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221532'>臣某言：今月二日，车驾幸秘书省，先奉圣旨，以臣兼修道史，系提举秘书省官属，合赴省起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221532_comment'></div>是日既与馆阁官观书、赐茶、谢恩毕，退，诏宣三公、宰臣、亲王、使相、执政、侍从官别观书画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221532_comment'></div>臣特蒙圣恩，俾预宣召之数，仍赐御笔行书、草书二纸，御画雀竹一纸者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221532_comment'></div>齿金兰之众俊，已冒殊私；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221532_comment'></div>踵笔橐之后尘，更膺特召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221532_comment'></div>咫尺圭璋之睟表，从容翰墨之荣观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221532_comment'></div>载窥天纵之能，旋拜奎文之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221532_comment'></div>褫心惊宠，浃髓怀恩<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221532_comment'></div>伏念臣疏远下僚，顿顽末学，敢意草茅之名姓，误叨旒扆之闻知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221532_comment'></div>惟是群玉蓬莱之山，实应列宿图书之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221532_comment'></div>六飞来止，七稔于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221532_comment'></div>云构百梁，屹天衢之左界；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221532_comment'></div>龙文八法，揭帝座之中居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221532_comment'></div>及斯轮奂之新，下慰英髦之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221532_comment'></div>爰申阔典，可谓难逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221532_comment'></div>而臣滥吹朝绅，虽玷南宫笺奏之末；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221532_comment'></div>操觚道史，适由东观著作之廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221532_comment'></div>在于提振之司，实与编摩之属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221532_comment'></div>荐迁严旨，俾簉清班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221532_comment'></div>云翼生身，遽翱翔于帝所；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221532_comment'></div>骊珠眩目，获藏去于宸章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221532_comment'></div>事匪常均，荣踰望外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221532_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下为仁由己，以德分人，游心万物之先，高视百王之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221532_comment'></div>譬若堪舆之大，何所弗容；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221532_comment'></div>故虽昭倬之馀，沛然成象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221532_comment'></div>发挥妙蕴，丕广鸿休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221532_comment'></div>灵篆结空，盖禀自然之兆；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221532_comment'></div>神书出洛，夐超副墨之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221532_comment'></div>至肆笔于丹青，盖合符于造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221532_comment'></div>岂伊么么，得被况临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221532_comment'></div>敢不仰服睿慈，时瞻天藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221532_comment'></div>冰霜是蹈，庶无易叶之凋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221532_comment'></div>筋力虽微，傥类衔环之报。</div><div id='poem_sentence_32_1221532_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年3月</a>　在汴京礼部员外郎任上，三月，为表叔王汉之作行状。作品：《延康殿学士中大夫提举杭州洞霄宫信安郡开国侯食邑一千七百户食实封一百户赠正奉大夫王公行状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十四。）</span><div id='poem_1221774' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221774' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221774?labeling=true' target='_blank'>延康殿学士中大夫提举杭州洞霄宫信安郡开国侯食邑一千七百户食实封一百户赠正奉大夫王公行状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1123年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221774")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221774_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221774'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221774'>曾祖敏，故不仕；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221774_comment'></div>曾祖母陈氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221774_comment'></div>祖言，故高邮军判官，赠光禄大夫；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221774_comment'></div>祖母徐氏，长安郡君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221774_comment'></div>父介，故尚书祠部郎中，充秘阁校理，赠少师；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221774_comment'></div>母蒋氏，赠越国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221774_comment'></div>衢州常山县人，年七十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221774_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1221774'>公讳汉之，字彦昭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221774_comment'></div>自曾大父好书服儒，怀器不售，光禄始以进士起家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221774_comment'></div>至少师，遂以贤良方正决殊科，登文馆，出入三朝，以直气谠言闻天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221774_comment'></div>艾耆不衰，老于外徙，教授诸子，身为严师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221774_comment'></div>公幼则不群，学为文词，已有惊人语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221774_comment'></div>神宗皇帝初以经术取士，公年始弱冠，中熙宁六年进士甲科，以秘书省校书郎、秀州司户参军差充汝州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221774_comment'></div>少师以公年尚少，方为人师，当益辅以学，无求速成，因留膝下，研究经史，滋进益勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221774_comment'></div>未行，少师捐馆，公居丧毁瘠，以孝闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221774_comment'></div>服除，为亳州州学教授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221774_comment'></div>郡守南丰曾子固待以国士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221774_comment'></div>迁和州防御推官，知河南府左军巡院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221774_comment'></div>元祐元年，以举者应铨格，改宣德郎，知婺州金华、河南府渑池县事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221774_comment'></div>丁越国太夫人忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221774_comment'></div>绍圣四年，以奉议郎充颍川郡王院吴王宫大小学教授，迁鸿胪寺丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221774_comment'></div>会仲兄卒吴中，公求外补，恤幼孤，治窆事，以承议郎知真州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221774_comment'></div>元符三年，以登极恩，迁朝奉郎，赐五品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221774_comment'></div>仪真当东南要冲，号难治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221774_comment'></div>公发奸举废，人以乂安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221774_comment'></div>建中靖国元年，除提举河东路常平等事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221774_comment'></div>进对称旨，留为开封府推官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221774_comment'></div>以朝散郎迁尚书工部员外郎，寻迁吏部，兼国史编修官，移礼部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221774_comment'></div>不阅月，以太常少卿充讲议司参详官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221774_comment'></div>时方绍修前烈，大起庶政，广学校、行三舍，公之参预为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221774_comment'></div>踰月，迁尚书礼部侍郎、兼修国史、充讲议司详定官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221774_comment'></div>久之，移户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221774_comment'></div>崇宁二年，以显谟阁待制出知瀛州、高阳关路安抚使、马步军都总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221774_comment'></div>公下车，抚绥边氓，申严军律，威声隐然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221774_comment'></div>时朝廷下边郡展楼橹、布埤堄、新守具、除戎器，广袤长短一以元丰法式从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221774_comment'></div>公言：「以高阳旧城较并边诸郡城壁，小大厚薄固已不同，而械具由一律，恐虚费不适用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221774_comment'></div>愿诏诸路参酌元丰法式随宜制备」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221774_comment'></div>从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221774_comment'></div>公又言：「国朝塘泊，东起沧州，西至安肃、广信军之南，凡九节，其所限地里高下、水之深广各有定数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221774_comment'></div>淳化中，知雄州何承矩始制屯田，诏发戍兵万八千人给其役，由是顺安以东濒于海，广袤数百里皆为稻田。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221774_comment'></div>其浚陂塘、筑堤道，则安抚司专制置，边郡遵条式、按图籍以从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221774_comment'></div>其后又诏修保塞等五州堤道为汇水之备，唯跳山以西壅水不能及，则为田设阱，种所宜木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221774_comment'></div>至大中祥符间，榆柳至三百万本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221774_comment'></div>此中国战守之助、万世之利也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221774_comment'></div>自北虏通好，塘泊屯田浸失旧制，并边官司无复案籍可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221774_comment'></div>愿俾河北东西具今废置利害，仍诏有司讨论故事，画一下边郡，守而行之，复祖宗之旧」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221774_comment'></div>又言：「旧制，界河战舡置务，乾宁军造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221774_comment'></div>崇宁初，漕司建徙真定就材木，或窳败不时得，请如旧制便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221774_comment'></div>又总管司旧领义勇乡军，自置保甲以来，更属提举保甲司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221774_comment'></div>愿仿旧制，乡军义勇俾部帅兼领，庶上下服习，缓急有所统一」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221774_comment'></div>所陈略见施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221774_comment'></div>是年，雄州归信、容城旱，两输人户请蠲税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221774_comment'></div>雄州不听，止全蠲南户税。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221774_comment'></div>公密论：「雄州规小利、失大体，非圣朝抚绥意，万有一契丹蠲税振荒，则何以示远」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221774_comment'></div>三年夏，移知江宁府，兼江南东路兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221774_comment'></div>未赴，改知河南府，兼西京留守司公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221774_comment'></div>转朝请郎，移知苏州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221774_comment'></div>以《哲宗实录》成，迁朝奉大夫，改知潭州，兼湖南路安抚使，封保宁县开国男，食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221774_comment'></div>时徭人向、黄二族寇通远峡武阳寨，略省地、杀居人，捕盗官战死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221774_comment'></div>公至，密遣兵据要地，阻其往来，掩获数百，降其酋豪三千馀人，一路安息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221774_comment'></div>移知洪州、充江南西路兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221774_comment'></div>五年春，诏乘驿赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221774_comment'></div>公入对，具言天下利病，如州县纳税租加耗无定法，吏缘侵渔为奸，洪州秋苗十七万石，而耗至二万八千；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221774_comment'></div>又市易岁息千缗，而廪禄杂费至用八百缗，无益公上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221774_comment'></div>大钱利厚，盗铸者不息，当立法为经久计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221774_comment'></div>留为尚书兵部侍郎，转朝散大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1221774_comment'></div>大观元年，成都择守，以显谟阁直学士知成都府、充成都府利州路兵马钤辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1221774_comment'></div>未至，知郑州、充西辅马步军都总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1221774_comment'></div>移知应天府兼南京留守司公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1221774_comment'></div>未至，又改知蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1221774_comment'></div>未几，知青州、充京东东路安抚使，进封开国子，加食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1221774_comment'></div>以受宝恩，迁朝请大夫，移知郓州、充京东西路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1221774_comment'></div>青、郓留皆踰年，政随其俗，皆以治称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1221774_comment'></div>转朝议大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1221774_comment'></div>四年夏，召赴阙，拜尚书工部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1221774_comment'></div>时议北郊仪物配位，公言：「自神宗皇帝正典礼、罢合祭，始诏亲祠北郊，如南郊仪，此成法也，尚何疑」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1221774_comment'></div>后如公议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1221774_comment'></div>八月，充贺北朝生辰国信使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1221774_comment'></div>使回，为《见闻录》以进，且言：「契丹上下游惰，无长虑却顾、为其国为久安计者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1221774_comment'></div>今预密议，唯宰相李俨，俨虽更事，然习久安、无远识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1221774_comment'></div>契丹岁比荒，用度毕取于燕人，凌蹙掊剥，至不堪命，怨嗟日闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1221774_comment'></div>又渤海俗犷悍，契丹尤疑而防之，然待之不以理，其积愤与燕人未尝一日忘契丹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1221774_comment'></div>其亡可待」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1221774_comment'></div>又言河北它利害甚众，上悦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1221774_comment'></div>政和元年，以显谟阁直学士充定州路安抚使、马步军都总管、兼知定州，进封开国伯，加食邑三百户，转中奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1221774_comment'></div>公临边踰年，训练拊循，境内宁肃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1221774_comment'></div>时朝旨下河北路均籴依陕西先得旨，两转运使文檄各下，人自立说，郡县莫知适从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1221774_comment'></div>公具奏请决，使者怒，公因移疾自陈，且乞避使者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1221774_comment'></div>朝廷下本路诘使者当何从，已乃有旨，漕臣及其属皆降官一等，其属仍免所居官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1221774_comment'></div>明年，转运使竟劾公恃故相党与沮籴法，落职，提举杭州洞霄宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1221774_comment'></div>时政和二年三月也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1221774_comment'></div>后三年，复集贤殿修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1221774_comment'></div>明年，复显谟阁直学士、知濠州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1221774_comment'></div>六安贼刘五窃发，邻境皆警。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1221774_comment'></div>公曰：「是何能为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1221774_comment'></div>不足为请兵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1221774_comment'></div>即命巡捕吏阅部曲、斥孱惰、明保伍、籍强勇、识险易、广耳目，至备御所宜，皆亲受方略，居人按堵，贼卒不犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1221774_comment'></div>七年，转中大夫，进封信安郡开国侯，加食邑三百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1221774_comment'></div>八年夏秋，淮水暴涨，城不没者数尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1221774_comment'></div>公止次城上，部勒捍治，城赖以完，濠人德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1221774_comment'></div>顷之，引疾丐归，复提举杭州洞霄宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1221774_comment'></div>重和元年，江东水灾，朝廷择帅安辑振廪之，起公知江宁府事兼江南东路兵马钤辖，加食邑三百户，食实封一百户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1221774_comment'></div>明年十一月，方贼起青溪，踰月，陷睦州，遂陷杭、歙，声摇江东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1221774_comment'></div>承平久，士不知兵，一旦狗鼠辈叫欢陆梁，横溃四出，守将往往茫不知所为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1221774_comment'></div>远近相蒙，初不以实闻上，及事急，则日为遁逃计，至则委城去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1221774_comment'></div>公初闻贼势张甚，即具奏不少隐，且下令曰：「贼来以死守，敢言退避者斩」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1221774_comment'></div>于是练士卒、募丁壮、据走集、远斥候、明赏罚，贼为少却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1221774_comment'></div>就差江南东路安抚使，诏奏事皆径达上前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1221774_comment'></div>正月，贼攻广德，焚宣州之宁国县，事益急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1221774_comment'></div>公日夜训抚，且守且御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1221774_comment'></div>时兵裁数千，贼徒动以数万计，人为公危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1221774_comment'></div>公命当贼冲，除地为场，曰：「贼来力战，共死于此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1221774_comment'></div>吏士皆感泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1221774_comment'></div>外督守将进讨，数获贼将，敕书嘉奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1221774_comment'></div>盖自十一月至二月，会大兵至境，由江东入贼峒，取渠魁以献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1221774_comment'></div>贼平，以功迁龙图阁学士，加食邑三百户，御前遣使赐茶药合、金渡银鞍辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1221774_comment'></div>四年，引年告老，优诏不许，转太中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1221774_comment'></div>九月，以疾力请，进职延康殿学士、提举杭州洞霄宫，金陵之人流涕遮道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1221774_comment'></div>顷之，以守江东日它路粮运留境上，降官一等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1221774_comment'></div>五年正月，上章请老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1221774_comment'></div>命未下，以二月四日卒于镇江居第之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1221774_comment'></div>诏赠正奉大夫，下两浙转运司助襄事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1221774_comment'></div>公夫人曾氏，先卒，赠信安郡侯淑人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1221774_comment'></div>子二人，曰樗，曰栎，皆承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1221774_comment'></div>以某年某月某日葬公于镇江府丹徒县黄杜村马鞍山之原少师墓后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1221774_comment'></div>公以高明之姿，纯正之学，敏达之才，自经术政事、文词字画、养生之妙、方外之理，皆意出人上，自以无前，一时交游，号为第一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1221774_comment'></div>然其高心独见，常糠秕文词，有不足为之意，故应酬落纸，初不留顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1221774_comment'></div>公没，家集其文，才得三十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1221774_comment'></div>至于友爱惇睦，轻财好施，轩豁无隐，又出天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1221774_comment'></div>公既通显，即买田乡里，疏宗群从，均济若一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1221774_comment'></div>凡戚属之贫无告者，赴之如归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1221774_comment'></div>至治命，犹曰妹侄之嫠孤者廪给如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1221774_comment'></div>中年遇方士，授以要诀，常专气葆神，燕坐翛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1221774_comment'></div>然事至不留，不为颓惰苟简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1221774_comment'></div>故出屏藩翰，入赞尚书，知无不言，事无不理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1221774_comment'></div>初得九转丹诀，练养十有五年，晚于大茅峰建洞阳庵，延道士沈若济守之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1221774_comment'></div>丹未成，而公逝矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1221774_comment'></div>然行年七十，须鬓蔚然，自初疾至病，未尝困卧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1221774_comment'></div>属纩之日，呼家人理后事、具遗表，整衣端坐，如假寐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1221774_comment'></div>议者以谓其平生自强，虽大期至，不为变屈，是诚足以过人矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1221774_comment'></div>其遭时事主、出入进退，岁月事实，可考如右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1221774_comment'></div>谨状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1221774_comment'></div>宣和五年三月日，从表侄朝奉郎、尚书礼部员外郎、赐绯鱼袋程状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_142_1221774_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　在汴京礼部员外郎任上，为蒋彝作墓志铭。作品：《朝散郎直秘阁赠徽猷阁待制蒋公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十。）</span><div id='poem_1221780' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221780' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221780?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散郎直秘阁赠徽猷阁待制蒋公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和四年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221780")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221780_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221780'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221780'>公讳彝，字子有，姓蒋氏，常州宜兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221780_comment'></div>汉太尉浚遒侯横者有子九人，其季曰默、曰澄，封维岱𠙶亭乡侯，始家宜兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221780_comment'></div>公则𠙶亭侯之后也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221780_comment'></div>曾祖讳九皋，累赠太傅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221780_comment'></div>祖讳堂，尚书礼部侍郎，为时名臣，国史有传，累赠少师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221780_comment'></div>考讳长源，庄重博雅，不以势利累心，官至朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221780_comment'></div>以公升朝，累赠至中奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221780_comment'></div>自侍郎始居吴，故今为吴郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221780_comment'></div>公幼嗜学，不妄交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221780_comment'></div>弱冠，以大夫遗表恩授太庙斋郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221780_comment'></div>调润州金坛簿，迁开封府陈留丞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221780_comment'></div>未赴，丁祖母仁寿县太君陈氏忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221780_comment'></div>服除，为秀州崇德令，达官部使者才之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221780_comment'></div>政和二年，太师鲁公自钱塘召还，复当国，即以公权提辖陕西坑冶催促铸钱事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221780_comment'></div>选人将使指，前未有此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221780_comment'></div>时荐者已及格，改宣德郎以行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221780_comment'></div>公下车，条析所应废置言上，皆见施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221780_comment'></div>居无几，坑冶鼓铸之利不赀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221780_comment'></div>及代去，计所铸息无虑数百万缗，凡所采金、银、丹砂、汞、铅、铜、铁称是，宝货入中都相属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221780_comment'></div>于是朝廷嘉其能，诏迁通直郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221780_comment'></div>又以复十监五院施置就绪，迁奉议郎，锡朱衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221780_comment'></div>又以岁课迁承议郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221780_comment'></div>六年，权发遣提举两浙路常平事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221780_comment'></div>入对便殿，敷奏详明，皆合上旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221780_comment'></div>上命以惩按奸吏、惠康小人之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221780_comment'></div>公至所治，宣恩举职，一路安之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221780_comment'></div>是年冬，除代赴阙，未行，诏复留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221780_comment'></div>时无锡丞有依势为奸利者赃至钜万，然方以最闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221780_comment'></div>公按捕丞，丞急，道亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221780_comment'></div>或止公曰：「是有挟，弗可败，且反为所中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221780_comment'></div>今丞亡，因末杀，无穷治，亦足以立威矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221780_comment'></div>公不听，曰：「吾受命云何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221780_comment'></div>吾知惩奸明法而已，不知其他」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221780_comment'></div>丞遇赦获免，犹坐废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221780_comment'></div>八年，移永兴军路，未行，诏授直秘阁、权两浙路计度转运副使，兼提举本路神霄、玉清、万寿宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221780_comment'></div>累迁朝散郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221780_comment'></div>二浙户繁，率隐丁口、避更赋，丁簿不得实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221780_comment'></div>前使者钩括釐正，追偿所失丁钱，别储为羡馀，远或至数十年，编户氓鲜获免者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221780_comment'></div>锢系相属，至或破产失业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221780_comment'></div>公至，具奏：「二浙比岁不登，今所追久远不胜治，又多贫下户，急之，必且逃徙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221780_comment'></div>愿一切蠲之，而名籍丁钱断自今始，已追钱归之有司充岁用」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221780_comment'></div>奏闻报可，吴人德之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221780_comment'></div>东南岁歉，御笔下诸路许留上供米四十万石赈饥人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221780_comment'></div>公奉诏唯谨，而廉访使者、提点刑狱司合奏公赈济文具无抚绥意，诏降三官停废。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221780_comment'></div>然犹以为疑，更诏廉访、提刑司，事实即以今诏从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221780_comment'></div>二司径檄公罢，已而诏降两官留任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221780_comment'></div>公力自辩，继降御笔，还所降官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221780_comment'></div>五月，中贵人使二浙，就赐金带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221780_comment'></div>先是，漕输中都数不时足，请以故岁所欠附春运。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221780_comment'></div>既得请矣，发运司方以逋滞劾，诏免所居官，寻落职与筦库。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221780_comment'></div>已而御笔复以公直秘阁、管句亳州明道宫，格前诏不行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221780_comment'></div>累迁朝奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221780_comment'></div>故事，谪宫观遇恩毋得任子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221780_comment'></div>是岁冬祀，诏特听任子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221780_comment'></div>宣和四年，起知明州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221780_comment'></div>公裁决抚循，事得其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221780_comment'></div>居数月，以疾卒于明州州治之正寝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221780_comment'></div>临终，神色不变，易衣坐，命诸子操纸笔付后事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221780_comment'></div>画字纸尾讫，悉遣家人辈出户，独与母诀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221780_comment'></div>三子环泣，即就枕瞑目而逝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221780_comment'></div>实是年六月甲辰，享年四十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221780_comment'></div>母夫人李氏，累封太令人，乐岂寿康。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221780_comment'></div>然再世子不终养而孙是托，何耶！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221780_comment'></div>公娶朝散郎、秘阁校理同郡梅公灏之女，柔顺而有常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221780_comment'></div>自在室至于有家，长于己者畏惕如不胜，与侪等居未尝失色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221780_comment'></div>政和四年六月壬申卒，年三十有七，累赠安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1221780_comment'></div>生三子，曰嗣康，迪功郎，起复秀州仪曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1221780_comment'></div>曰嗣宗，将仕郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1221780_comment'></div>曰嗣昌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1221780_comment'></div>孙男二人，曰谟，曰諲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1221780_comment'></div>孙女一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1221780_comment'></div>公明爽有才气，少治《易》，通大义，荐于有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1221780_comment'></div>然载籍无不观，尤熟唐事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1221780_comment'></div>为诗词婉美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1221780_comment'></div>及为吏，事至能断，不为龊龊小谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1221780_comment'></div>性不容物，而于故旧特笃，干乞借贷，门无虚时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1221780_comment'></div>至或见卖挠其治者，始闻之怒，他日施施复来，振给馆谷之如故，终不忍谢绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1221780_comment'></div>良士友至，不计家有无，为酒具珍馔，陈图书奇玩，剧饮赋诗，相娱乐无厌色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1221780_comment'></div>自未仕及为县令、至使者常然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1221780_comment'></div>初，大夫公捐馆时，上有老亲，孤女满室，食指几数百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1221780_comment'></div>公以一命仰微禄，居数年，所当嗣志卒事者无馀责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1221780_comment'></div>事祖母及母夫人极甘旨之奉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1221780_comment'></div>方是时，家实贫甚，假贷阅日而不见寒饥憔悴态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1221780_comment'></div>及官稍遂，亦不汲汲为生业计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1221780_comment'></div>故奋由小官、将使指，声称日闻，交道弥广，以取宠荣，盖其胸次卓荦，才能绝人远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1221780_comment'></div>公卒之明年，诏特赠公徽猷阁待制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1221780_comment'></div>虽圣主简劳劝功无存亡久新远迩之间而然，抑以见公之才非唯振耀于一时，其规模蕴业所以储荣委祉于身后者又如此其白也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1221780_comment'></div>如端拜而议，如交手相授，施报之道，为不诬矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1221780_comment'></div>其孤将以八月戊申合葬公及安人于平江府吴县至德乡报恩山之原，使来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1221780_comment'></div>余与公游且三十年，知公为详，则叙而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1221780_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_90_1221780'>姬公子龄蒋封始，中微世更国为氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1221780_comment'></div>浚遒九支㡭以继，义兴宗维两侯裔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1221780_comment'></div>作周诒法粲王治，德光流行泽百世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1221780_comment'></div>世多贤能乃其理，孤师端亮世标轨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1221780_comment'></div>培基衍庆施孙子，明州才周质魁伟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1221780_comment'></div>皇皇节舆光族里，发奸绳恶人所徯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1221780_comment'></div>嘉言解纷定流徙，时非不逢用不既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1221780_comment'></div>天高听遐纪瘽瘁，追功陟华告其第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1221780_comment'></div>有嫔维梅柔以惠，无非无仪谨尝馈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1221780_comment'></div>生同甘辛葬同隧，铭无溢词信来祀。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_99_1221780'></div><div id='poem_sentence_99_1221780_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1123&endYear=1123')">1123年</a>　丁母忧，时在汴京。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
杭州（新城）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8177bec30c6a4d97adca921e1fb43637_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8177bec30c6a4d97adca921e1fb43637");'><span id='8177bec30c6a4d97adca921e1fb43637_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1090&endYear=1090')">1090年3月</a>　三月，随外祖邓润甫复至汴京，途经新城。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='8e82f540662a441c8bdf3601b7bd659c_label'><a
