ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>，24岁</div><div id='8e82f540662a441c8bdf3601b7bd659c' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在舒州太湖茶场任上。往余杭，娶继室江氏，同江仲嘉褒、道人陈祖德良孙游洞霄宫，有诗。作品：《同余杭尉江仲嘉褒、道人陈祖德良孙游洞霄宫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_526979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526979?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同馀杭尉江仲嘉褒道人陈祖德良孙游洞霄宫</a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526979")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526979_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526979'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526979'>太湖隐吏迂且顽，手扳柱颊看西山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526979'>笔床茶灶向何许，往来洞庭林屋间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526979'>旧闻西门彻悬霤，故整烟艇寻苕川。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526979'>却惊天柱矗云表，势与太华争擎天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526979'>幅巾跨马及晓鼓，逸思自觉奔春泉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526979'>其谁从者二妙士，金庭老客南昌仙。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526979'>齐驱共语失长道，但见平阪连桑田。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526979'>篮舆后继独不语，鼻息栩栩山耸肩。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526979'>岗回涧曲若无路，万叠老翠漫秋烟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526979'>三山对起锁诘屈，仅容蹄辙通人寰。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526979'>羊肠移险在平地，九疑山色荒联绵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526979'>穿松酌水寻二洞，低隐岩腹高山巅。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526979'>山巅石室如列厦，接肘可置千宾筵。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526979'>最怜西洞隔凡处，凝<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去。）</span>乳络壁留空圆。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526979'>我将拂袖去不返，戏击雷鼓挥神鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526979'>三华宝衣立可致，九赤班符何足传。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526979'>只将尻与驾神马，岂顾家火烧凡铅。<div id='poem_sentence_16_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_526979'>又疑灵物之所宅，卵孕变化蟠蜿蜒。<div id='poem_sentence_17_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_526979'>金龙玉简投不满，恐复下与东溟连。<div id='poem_sentence_18_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_526979'>我嗟何地非圣处，火聚正坐青云軿。<div id='poem_sentence_19_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_526979'>目前阊阖昼自启，电顷已超天地先。<div id='poem_sentence_20_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_526979'>正缘一念重山岳，障碍何啻重城坚。<div id='poem_sentence_21_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_526979'>就令信脚到仙宇，凡骨至死包<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作色）</span>腥膻。<div id='poem_sentence_22_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_526979'>胶胶世网浪自缠，会当去之如蜕蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_23_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_526979'>谁能白衣傍金马，且复锦袍乘钓船。<div id='poem_sentence_24_526979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_526979'>金庭客，南昌仙，他年与我乘八景，举手少别三千<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作十）</span>年。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_526979_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在舒州太湖茶场任上。往余杭，娶继室江氏，有诗。作品：《余杭法喜院荆文公书堂文公康定中读书于此》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527224' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527224' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527224?labeling=true' target='_blank'>馀杭法喜院荆文公书堂文公康定中读书于此</a><span class='authorDate'>（辛巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527224")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527224_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527224'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527224'>钟山太傅起从龙，鼓动风雷<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作云）</span>指顾中。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527224'>未见图形求傅野，岂知徒步客新丰<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527224'>青鞋曾访餐芝老，白首惟馀捣药童<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527224'>藏壁故应留断简，至今山鬼恸悲风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527224'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527224_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527224'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527224_0'>⑴ 自注：许远游登岩茹芝，乃馀杭山中也。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_527224_0'>⑵ 自注：寺僧言文公多养疾此堂，当时给侍童子，今八十一岁矣。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527224_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8aab14d951fb468e985a575b182b3036_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8aab14d951fb468e985a575b182b3036");'><span id='8aab14d951fb468e985a575b182b3036_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，52岁</div><div id='8aab14d951fb468e985a575b182b3036' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月14日</a>　二月十四日，至杭州，上劄子议事，时任礼部员外郎。作品：《乞许六参官赴二十六日起居》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221587' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221587' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221587?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞许六参官赴二十六日起居状<span class='inlineComment2'>（建炎三年二月随驾初到杭州。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年2月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221587")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221587_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221587'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221587'>某窃闻已降指挥，二十六日朝殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221587_comment'></div>契勘当日不系六参日分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221587_comment'></div>切缘六参官及望参官自此月已来，车驾戒行在道，久阙常仪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221587_comment'></div>况艰危之后，驻跸之初，始御朝殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221587_comment'></div>不胜臣子之情，欲乞特降指挥，六参官及望参官并赴二十六日起居。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1221587_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月24日</a>　在杭州礼部员外郎任上，二月二十四日，再上劄子议事。作品：《省官》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十五。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月</a>　在杭州礼部员外郎任上，三月初，上劄子乞外任或宫观。作品：《三年三月初乞郡或宫观劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十六。）</span><div id='poem_1221592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221592?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三年三月初乞郡或宫观劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221592")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221592_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221592'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221592'>某昨以罪戾之馀，寓居镇江，屏迹丘园，自知无用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221592_comment'></div>伏自车驾驻跸扬州，将及一年，某虽累经寇攘之后，衣食不给，然一水之间，终不敢出干禄仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221592_comment'></div>于去年八月，忽蒙误恩，复除著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221592_comment'></div>某皇恐具状，备述多病不才与朝廷方当总核名实，以图中兴之举，非疵贱小臣尸禄养痾之时，申尚书省，乞赐罢免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221592_comment'></div>寻又蒙尚书省劄子，催促就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221592_comment'></div>遂再具劄子申丞相府，具述如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221592_comment'></div>久不闻罢，渐至冬深，疆埸未宁，恐涉避事，以十月二十三日赴行阙朝见供职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221592_comment'></div>每见宰执，具陈诚恳，略如前意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221592_comment'></div>且言方冬，未敢乞罢，只候开春丐归林下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221592_comment'></div>今仆射相公、门下侍郎及尚书右丞时领中司，每蒙与见，皆曾具布此诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221592_comment'></div>而正月已来，边报日急，未敢复申前恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221592_comment'></div>又蒙恩命，还置礼曹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221592_comment'></div>入谢之初，即复狼狈渡江，缘路遭劫，几至裸露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221592_comment'></div>即与妻孥徒步趼足，奔赴行阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221592_comment'></div>于时从官尚有未到，庶官到者才十数人，留家杭州者不过一二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221592_comment'></div>人之常情，理势应尔，但疵贱惷愚，人所不贷，深自惩创，不敢迟留，区区之私，亦足矜察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221592_comment'></div>今天气渐暖，既无外虞，厚禄清曹，别无规避，乃敢复申前恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221592_comment'></div>伏望钧慈陶铸宫庙一次，俾遂首丘，不负本志，则虽死之日，犹生之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221592_comment'></div>下情无任激切俟罪之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1221592_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月14日</a>　在杭州礼部员外郎任上，三月十四日，徒步山间，失脚倒地受伤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年3月16日</a>　在杭州，三月十六日，除太常少卿，以“疾痛日加，有妨行步”等原因再三上劄子辞免。作品：《辞免太常少卿申尚书省状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十六。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月1日</a>　在杭州，四月一日，以直秘阁秀州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='63a1491b68ba4d05af36bbc85ed6f787_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("63a1491b68ba4d05af36bbc85ed6f787");'><span id='63a1491b68ba4d05af36bbc85ed6f787_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年</a>，55岁</div><div id='63a1491b68ba4d05af36bbc85ed6f787' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月14日</a>　在临安中书舍人任上，正月十四日，随高宗至临安。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月16日</a>　在临安中书舍人任上。武功大夫、荣州团练使苏易乞以奉化县界把截所转一官于阶官，上许之。正月十六日，程俱上书力论其不可。作品：《缴苏易转行横行奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷四十。）</span><div id='poem_1221573' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221573' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221573?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴苏易转行横行奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年1月16日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221573")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221573_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221573'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221573'>准中书门下省兵房送到词头一道，为武功大夫、荣州团练使苏易把截奉化县界，已蒙转一官回授，乞于今官上收使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221573_comment'></div>奉圣旨，苏易将所得转一官特于阶官上转行，其已降回授指挥更不施行，令臣命词行下者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221573_comment'></div>右，臣窃见自顷以来，武臣转官皆自武功大夫转入横行，寖以冗滥，顿失祖宗之法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221573_comment'></div>得者既众，则官益以轻，使人人皆怀欲得之心，无有纪极，在于厉世劝功之时，其为弊害尤大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221573_comment'></div>今苏易止是把隘奉化，不经斗敌，便转一官，回授有服亲，已是优恩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221573_comment'></div>既降成命，今来乃于阶官上转行，即合转右武大夫，乃是昔时西上閤门使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221573_comment'></div>而朝廷即从其请，收还回授指挥，其于祖宗之法、号令之宜，皆非所应得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221573_comment'></div>臣契勘祖宗之法，文臣自守将作监主簿至尚书左仆射，武臣自三班奉职至节度使，即是以次迁转之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221573_comment'></div>而武臣閤门副使至客省使为横行，不系磨勘迁转之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221573_comment'></div>既不系磨勘，即非皇城使所得转入之官，其除授皆须特旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221573_comment'></div>故元丰肇新官制之时，以承务郎至特进为寄禄官，以易监主簿至仆射之名，而武臣独依旧，不以寄禄官易之者，盖有深意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221573_comment'></div>自政和，不唯轻改武臣官称为郎、大夫，遂并与横行易之，而为转官之等级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221573_comment'></div>此皆当时有司不习典故，不思祖宗之深旨，率意改更，以开侥倖之门，大抵如此，故流弊日深也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221573_comment'></div>祖宗时如曹玮屡更边帅，功名杰出，乃以閤门使知秦州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221573_comment'></div>张亢扬历最久，官止于客省使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221573_comment'></div>且以元丰三年言之，是时官仪人物最盛且多之时，而閤门使止有十四员，引进使一员，四方馆使二员，副使五员而已，诸将之为横行者皆在数中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221573_comment'></div>如种谔、韩存宝、李浩、李昌祚、姚麟之流是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221573_comment'></div>谔以崇仪副使知岷州，擒宗哥首领，败鬼章而得引进副使，后以擒山后生羌冷鸡朴而得东上閤门使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221573_comment'></div>当时横行既少，官职贵重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221573_comment'></div>官职贵重，则人以为荣，人主庆赏之柄亦重，不然则反是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221573_comment'></div>且文臣之所谓庶官者，转不得过中大夫，而武臣乃得过皇城使，此何理也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221573_comment'></div>横行职事亲近人主，恩数多类从官，故祖宗时官至皇城使者尚少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221573_comment'></div>其有至皇城使而合转官者，多是只与遥郡刺吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221573_comment'></div>今乃于武功大夫上一例转行，其为冗滥甚矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221573_comment'></div>自改使为大夫已来，经靖康、建炎覃沛之后，常调之官，下至皂使仆厮之馀，转而为横行者不可胜数，而运战之物不以功之高下一例转入者又不可胜数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221573_comment'></div>自古名器不慎，官职太轻，变易旧章、紊乱体制，未有如十馀年以来者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221573_comment'></div>今横行之官无虑数百千员，其弊可谓极矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221573_comment'></div>夫官职重轻，在朝廷所以用之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221573_comment'></div>朝廷爱重官职，不妄与之，则官职重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221573_comment'></div>若朝廷轻以与人，得者冗滥，则官职轻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221573_comment'></div>官职轻则得者不以为恩，未得者常怀觖望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221573_comment'></div>何谓得者不以为恩？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221573_comment'></div>异时横行至少，得者即为异恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221573_comment'></div>今则人人可以循次转行，则彼才器超绝之人，军职立功之士，与常进碌碌之流，官称一同，了无差别，所在之处，百千为曹，则亦何足贵者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221573_comment'></div>使彼挈短量长、计功比类，则所谓得之不以为恩者有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221573_comment'></div>何谓未得者常怀觖望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221573_comment'></div>盖与之既轻，得之容易，则其流必滥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221573_comment'></div>既滥则冗，理之必然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221573_comment'></div>则彼未得者将曰，某人之才，我岂不如；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221573_comment'></div>某人之迁，岂以功伐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221573_comment'></div>然彼为横行，而我独平进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221573_comment'></div>则所谓未得者常怀觖望者有矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221573_comment'></div>岂唯不以为恩与常怀觖望而已，而安危治乱之萌实存其中，盖不可不慎所与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221573_comment'></div>关、张官为将军，则虽以黄忠之才之功，先主亦欲为将军，而诸葛武侯以为不可遽与关、张等，如此则官职安得不重？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221573_comment'></div>唐德宗时，勋官冗滥，于是有以开府骠骑告身易一醉者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221573_comment'></div>然则官职重轻无它，唯朝廷所以用之如何耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221573_comment'></div>臣不胜愚惷拳拳虑国之诚，忘其么么，敢因苏易之请，曲折布陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221573_comment'></div>亦冀陛下深思熟计，有以救其弊而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221573_comment'></div>其苏易所转一官，伏望圣慈只令依前降回授指挥施行，庶使有功而得之者皆知为异恩，而非可以循致者也，则官职重而劝激深矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221573_comment'></div>所有词头缴纳中书门下省外，谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_49_1221573'></div><div id='poem_sentence_49_1221573_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月20日</a>　在临安中书舍人任上，二月二十日，上书指斥徐俯与中官唱和，并言除其为谏议大夫不妥，上不听。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年2月22日</a>　在临安，二月二十二日，右司谏方孟卿论程俱谄附蔡攸、弃秀州而遁事，因此罢官归乡，时提举江州太平观。作品：《二月二十日实封奏》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷四十。）</span><div id='poem_1221578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>二月二十日实封奏<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1132年2月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221578")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221578_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1221578_0'>① 二十二日承省劄备坐白劄子上言云云，奉圣旨罢中书舍人、提举江州太平观。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221578'>右，臣准中书门下省吏房送到词头一道，徐俯除右谏议大夫，令臣命词行下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221578_comment'></div>臣伏见自顷以来，陛下图治之切，往往急于用人，德意诚厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221578_comment'></div>然窃考古今之宜与祖宗之制，其进用人才，自非隐遁丘园、道义才器卓然杰出，如阳城、种放之流，未有阔略资望，不循次而进者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221578_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221578_comment'></div>名器不可不重，人情当使厌服故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221578_comment'></div>俯之少时，诚有俊声，气亦豪迈，以禧之子，尝见用于崇宁、政和之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221578_comment'></div>然以黄庭坚甥，又上书入邪等，且连任宫观，故流落于群枉当路之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221578_comment'></div>靖康之初，召为省郎，其后未有所历也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221578_comment'></div>陛下即位以来，初未之识，令乃遽自前任省郎骤除谏议大夫，自元丰五年更定官制来，五十馀年未之有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221578_comment'></div>上皇用人，虽号为兼收骤用，然亦未有所谓亲擢之士阔略资历如此者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221578_comment'></div>传曰：「如有所誉，其有所试矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221578_comment'></div>又曰：「左右皆曰贤，未可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221578_comment'></div>诸大夫皆曰贤，未可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221578_comment'></div>国人皆曰贤，然后察之，见贤焉，然后用之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221578_comment'></div>此古圣人之言，用人之法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221578_comment'></div>今陛下亦既有所试而见其贤矣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221578_comment'></div>况谏议大夫以弥缝衮阙、佑佐上德为职，昔者端厚如王觌，博通如孔文仲，刚果如刘安世，忠清如丰稷，尝为之矣，然觌、文仲、安世，皆自谏官次迁，稷自前侍郎、待制迁，皆望实俱高，人主熟其议论趣向以充选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221578_comment'></div>今俯虽气豪才俊，然陛下何从便得之而骤用若此？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221578_comment'></div>臣恐天下怪惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221578_comment'></div>汉鲍宣尝言：「古刑人尚服，今爵人反惑，无乃与人美官，未足以劝，而反令天下惑乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221578_comment'></div>陛下诚知徐俯，可惜岁月，召至行在，所谓视其所以，观其所由，察其所安，使其望实已孚于人，然后进而用之，盖无不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221578_comment'></div>宁使士论以得之为后时，而无使相顾骇视，腹非而窃叹也，非君父所以成就爱惜臣子之心也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221578_comment'></div>不然，则似恐其不来，以高位诱之，要其必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221578_comment'></div>如此，则不唯非所以待士，亦不足以得士矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221578_comment'></div>何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221578_comment'></div>盖上之人期之以利，而彼亦怀利而来，苟怀利也，亦何士之可得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221578_comment'></div>臣愿陛下但下召命，须其至也，姑以所应得者命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221578_comment'></div>陛下它日欲置之左右，循涂而进，亦何为不可哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221578_comment'></div>臣诚为朝廷惜此举措而爱俯人才，窃思有以弥缝成就之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221578_comment'></div>臣承词头，窃用惶惑，伏念旬日，不敢措词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221578_comment'></div>已而再思，蒙陛下厚恩，俾待罪论思之地，傥使朝廷举措未厌人心，或致疑谤，而乃惜身怀利，不能长虑却顾，尽忠献言，是臣仰负圣恩，苟贪荣宠，人尤鬼瞰，将无所逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221578_comment'></div>所以触死忘生，妄贡愚瞽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221578_comment'></div>伏望陛下深思愚言，更赐裁处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221578_comment'></div>臣闻汉武帝时读《子虚赋》而善之，有「恨不与朕同时」之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221578_comment'></div>狗监杨得意侍旁，进言「乃臣里人司马相如所作」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221578_comment'></div>及召相如至，但以为郎，久之，为文园令而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221578_comment'></div>使相如不因狗监，不由华丽之文以闻，则汉武必有以处之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221578_comment'></div>史称汉武雄才大略，岂此类耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221578_comment'></div>今俯之素行无相如之累，陛下育材从善、爱惜臣子之心又远过前古，但不须匆匆如此，无故使上下皆受疑谤于清议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221578_comment'></div>只如唐之元稹，其才器文章既为名御史矣，在长庆时命知制诰，以至翰林，真不忝矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221578_comment'></div>止缘自荆南判司中，忽命从中出，召为省郎，便知制诰，遂喧朝听，穆宗与稹皆得谤议，以谓荆南监军崔潭峻之所引也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221578_comment'></div>致使元稹才能一皆埋没，为正人面辱，比之青蝇，是进之适所以毁之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221578_comment'></div>以此观之，不可不慎，不可不惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221578_comment'></div>此臣所以拳拳恳恳上渎圣聪者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221578_comment'></div>所有告命，臣未敢命词行下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221578_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221578_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1221578'>臣两日来，闻外传俯与中官唱和，有「鱼须」之句，号为警策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221578_comment'></div>臣恐外人不知陛下所以得俯之由，妄以此为疑议，仰累圣德之聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221578_comment'></div>愚所以不敢缄默，终具缴论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221578_comment'></div>然臣未敢具申中书门下省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221578_comment'></div>如臣所陈或蒙采纳，只乞圣旨从中处分，别降指挥，收还前命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221578_comment'></div>臣无任惶惧忧灼俟罪之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221578_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_52_1221578'>〔贴黄〕奏为徐俯差除词头，欲乞圣慈更加裁省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221578_comment'></div>如臣所陈或蒙采纳，只乞从中处分，别降指挥，收还前命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221578_comment'></div>候敕旨事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221578_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1221578'>臣手写奏状，如蒙圣慈开可，别作施行，即乞不须降出。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_55_1221578'></div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1221578_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

建德

-----title
苏州（吴县）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='d4b355755db84c82a829f9c17c8084dd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d4b355755db84c82a829f9c17c8084dd");'><span id='d4b355755db84c82a829f9c17c8084dd_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年</a>　仲姊归朱长文长子耜，得乐圃先生朱长文赏识，目为奇童，程俱或在吴县，从之学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年</a>　或在吴县，从学乐圃先生朱长文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1093')">1093年6月</a>　或在吴县，从学乐圃先生朱长文，六月，朱长文赴太学，有诗送之。作品：《送朱伯原博士赴太学》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷八。）</span><div id='poem_527215' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527215' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527215?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送朱伯原博士赴太学</a><span class='authorDate'>（癸酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527215")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527215_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527215'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527215'>朱公将赴成均时，炎炎六月云峰奇。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527215'>阊门鼓声催画鹢，陂塘菡萏方华滋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527215'>朝云回首暮云合，汗青嵬磊扃岩扉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527215'>先生顾此重惜去，片帆未肯乘风飞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527215'>贱子乃前致以词，诚知去鲁心迟迟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527215'>丈夫出处会有时，从来猿鹤焉能知。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527215'>醇儒况复生盛世，终老岩穴将何为。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527215'>公其去矣莫回首，君王仄席思贤久。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527215'>公怀慷慨善哉言，挽舟便出枫桥口。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527215_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527215'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_527215_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　客居吴县，尝过林虙居所大云坊，结识富延年。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1094&endYear=1094')">1094年</a>　客居吴县，外祖邓润甫是年卒，此文大约作于此年。作品：《邓安惠公赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_1221732' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221732' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221732?labeling=true' target='_blank'>邓安惠公赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1094年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221732")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221732_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221732'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221732'>翼翼邓公，外粹中刚，德人之容。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1221732'>有蕴若虚，叩之则出，如响发钟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1221732'>有文不彪，用之则宜，温厚显融。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1221732'>白首事亲，洞洞属属，如相肃雍。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1221732'>移之事君，牧丘之慎，文终之恭。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1221732'>然执法宪府，謇謇不挠，审克厥中。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1221732'>有赫军容，祸乱之机，见微纳忠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1221732'>晚登庙堂，泊无怨怀，游心大公。<div id='poem_sentence_7_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1221732'>盖清而畏知，仁而有勇，和而不同。<div id='poem_sentence_8_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1221732'>不色不言，不有其贤，名莫之从。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1221732'>知人则哲，帝鉴孔昭，温良在躬。<div id='poem_sentence_10_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1221732'>老成日徂，世不之才，机警疏通。<div id='poem_sentence_11_1221732_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_1221732'>爱而不见，再拜遗像，隐如岱嵩。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1221732_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='3a34a99144ad400f86bf067c637e3921_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3a34a99144ad400f86bf067c637e3921");'><span id='3a34a99144ad400f86bf067c637e3921_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>，18岁</div><div id='3a34a99144ad400f86bf067c637e3921' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1095&endYear=1095')">1095年</a>　客居吴县。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='08b19883bd2f425db17f5ae676248fc7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("08b19883bd2f425db17f5ae676248fc7");'><span id='08b19883bd2f425db17f5ae676248fc7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年</a>，25岁</div><div id='08b19883bd2f425db17f5ae676248fc7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>于苏州吴县拜见吴中二老杨懿孺、方子通，有诗。作品：《过方子通惟深》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷一。）</span><div id='poem_526875' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526875' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526875?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过方子通惟深</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526875")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526875_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526875'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526875'>白日苦易晚，我怀多隐忧。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526875'>忧思剧春浸，浩漫不可收。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526875'>出门欲有适，举步且复休。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526875'>尘中等胶扰，念此将焉投。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526875'>驾言城东北，阎闾即岩丘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526875'>是中有幽人，厉志凌霜秋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526875'>寸田荆棘尽，不假斤斧脩。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526875'>门无杂车马，一饭乃见留。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526875'>虚堂芝朮香，下有百尺虬。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526875'>苍阴匝平地，老干森下樛。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526875'>堂中罗酒浆，耿耿灯烛幽。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526875'>四天黮无光，万籁肃以揫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526875'>炯然坐相向，更仆语益遒。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526875'>我身动乖迕，梦寐乔松游。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526875'>常恐在泥滓，永为天所囚。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526875'>会当从之子，濯足万里流。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526875_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526875'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_526875_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>于苏州吴县拜见吴中二老杨懿孺、方子通，有和杨懿孺诗。作品：《和杨彝甫静妙轩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_527048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和杨彝甫静妙轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", id='poem_sentence_0_527048'>君家执戟郎，寂寞坠天禄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527048'>萧然刘董外，那用相窘束。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527048'>居无甔石储，但有书满屋。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527048'>君今老衡茅，出处异兰菊。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527048'>静中独观妙，四达开惠目。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527048'>中园郁黄华，庭下森翠竹。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527048'>饥来索盘餐，小极须睡足。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527048'>时当叩君门，为问梅子熟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527048'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527048_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb6336bc5e29468e8cbe2dea8bba3be3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb6336bc5e29468e8cbe2dea8bba3be3");'><span id='bb6336bc5e29468e8cbe2dea8bba3be3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>，36岁</div><div id='bb6336bc5e29468e8cbe2dea8bba3be3' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>以崇宁上书罢职，不久，主管兖州岱岳观，时为通直郎，卜居苏州蜗庐。作品：《迁居蜗庐诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷三。蜗庐在长洲县（今江苏苏州）城北，中有常寂光室、胜义斋等。另据程俱《北山小集》卷十九《衢州开化县新学记》“通直郎管勾岱岳观程某记”，主管兖州岱岳观时为通直郎，年谱中无，今补上。）</span>《蜗庐有隙地三两席稍种树竹已有可观戏作七篇》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_527007' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527007' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527007?labeling=true' "poem_title_527007")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527007_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527007'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527007'>有舍仅容膝，有门不容车。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527007'>寰中孰非寄，是岂真吾庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527007'>不作大耳儿，闭关种园蔬。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527007'>茅薝接环堵，无地可灌锄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527007'>不作下榻翁，一室谢扫除。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527007'>平生四海志，投老河鱼枯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527007'>坐视蛮触战，兼忘糟粕书。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527007'>聊呼赤松子，伴我龟肠虚<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《北山小集》卷三）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527007_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527046?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>水青</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527046'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527046'>水青虽楚楚，不复中栋梁。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527046'>黄封入雕槛，亦足被宠光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527046'>朝离粪壤区，暮上君子堂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527046_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527046_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>苏州蜗庐有胜林堂、妙高堂、常寂光庵等，当为陆续所建之物，有诗咏之，时间不详，姑系于此。作品：《山居》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷六。）</span><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>卜居苏州蜗庐期间，结识叶梦得，两人唱酬颇多。作品：《同叶内翰游南峰，窃观壬辰旧题诗，谨次严韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷二。）</span>《葺蜗庐吴下，用叶翰林见寄诗韵作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span>《和叶翰林阻雨枫桥》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷一。）</span>《同叶翰林游虎丘分韵得丘字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_527003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同叶内翰游南峰窃观壬辰旧题诗谨次严韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527003")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527003'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527003'>道林弥天辩，妙誉倾斗南。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527003'>山阴有馀赏，禹穴或已探。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527003'>晚岁折<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：舌。）</span>筇杖，兹焉寄伽蓝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527003'>呼鹰阅神骏，对客手自谈。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527003'>却顾夸夺子，心兵战方酣。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527003'>当时蹇驴辈，蹴踏岂所堪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527003'>斯人不可见，荒径昔已谙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527003'>青鞋踏松月，幽灯照禅龛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527003'>尔来十五年，身世犹朝三。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527003'>羁游了无蒂，飞蓬转毗岚。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527003'>愧此石窟人，坚持證那含<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：石庵间有道者坐禅。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527003'>如公世所挽，明堂要樟楠。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527003'>徘徊弭玉节，聊酌需泉甘。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527003'>老乃涧底松，霜枝郁毵毵。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527003'>尚有蠹书癖，囊中密如蚕。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527003'>中年锢泉石，此外无馀耽。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527003'>从公恣幽讨，形疲意犹贪。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527003'>安得五亩园，旁营二空庵。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527003'>心游万物表，旷若巨海涵。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527003'>恨无买山具，抚境思髯参<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_19_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_527003'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_527003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527003'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_527003_0'>⑴ 自注：郗超每闻高隐者，辄倾财资之。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527003_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527362' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527362' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527362?labeling=true' target='_blank'>葺蜗庐吴下用叶翰林见寄诗韵作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527362")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527362_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527362'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527362'>四海无庐置此翁，故营松竹尽囊空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527362'>明知计出<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_527362", 527362, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>柏马</span>下，正拟身全木雁中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527362'>东郭易成生草舍，南村先怯卷茅风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527362'>向来豪气今如此，敢与元龙比长雄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527362'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527362_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527362'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_527362_0'>⑴ 自注：张志和结庐东郭，茨以生草。余结庐皆竹椽松柱，故有松竹之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527362_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_526921' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526921' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526921?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和叶翰林阻雨枫桥</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526921")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526921_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526921'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526921'>白雨下车轴，江湖与天邻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526921'>浑流已横溃，川陆无行人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526921'>荡荡淮楚舟，篙樯动萧晨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526921'>淹留寒山寺，河湾俯清沦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526921'>虚堂梦春草，落纸佳句新。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526921'>长啸寄遐想，深谈破无因<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：外道无因论。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526921'>泊无轩裳累，但觉山林亲。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526921'>迟迟去鲁意，欲驾还逡巡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526921'>阴霖固无限，所念商农迍。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526921'>乃知君子怀，绝出世俗尘。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526921_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526921'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_526921_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527002' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527002' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527002?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同叶翰林游虎丘分韵得丘字</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527002")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527002_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527002'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527002'>四顾渺平野，孤撑见林丘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527002'>常疑涌地出，傥复海所浮。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527002'>上有千人台，灵踪想前脩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527002'>无情肯深义，顽石亦点头。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527002'>下有百尺渊，神光干斗牛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527002'>阴崖不见日，草木皆先秋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527002'>两晋多达士，东亭抑其流。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527002'>结庐远车马，寄此山之幽。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527002'>一朝施白足，弃去如毛輶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527002'>矧伊桑下宿，肯作贾胡留。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527002_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527002'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_527002_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='d20d57bd3c6541a5b52ca7f9c20e102e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("d20d57bd3c6541a5b52ca7f9c20e102e");'><span id='d20d57bd3c6541a5b52ca7f9c20e102e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>，36岁</div><div id='d20d57bd3c6541a5b52ca7f9c20e102e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年9月1日</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，九月一日，为张有《复古编》作序。作品：《复古编后序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221646' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221646' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221646?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复古编序</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和三年九月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221646")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221646_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221646'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221646'>程子曰，学之不可以不专也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221646_comment'></div>涉其流者未有能极其原，游其藩者未有能睹其奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221646_comment'></div>不极其原，不睹其奥，求其是且精焉无有也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221646_comment'></div>夫支左诎右，夫人而射也称养叔；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221646_comment'></div>钧弦柱指，夫人而琴也称子野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221646_comment'></div>上下千百载间，学是者亦众矣，而二子擅焉，岂不以其专以精乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221646_comment'></div>吴兴张有，弱冠以小篆名，自古文奇字与夫许氏之书，了然如烛照而数计也，它书馀艺一不入于胸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221646_comment'></div>盖其专如此，故四十而学成，六十而其书成，《复古之编》是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221646_comment'></div>余尝论其书曰：小篆之作，自峄山真刻不传，至唐，字学虽盛，而以篆法盖一时、名后世者，惟李阳冰为称首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221646_comment'></div>徐铉后出，笔力劲古，遂出阳冰上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221646_comment'></div>近世名笔固多，其分间布白、规圜绳直不工，而笔力劲古，少复铉比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221646_comment'></div>今有自振于数千载后，独悟周秦石刻用笔意，落纸便觉岐阳峄山去人不远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221646_comment'></div>二卷三千言，据古《说文》以为正，其点画之微，转侧从衡、高下曲直，毫发有差，则形声顿异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221646_comment'></div>自阳冰前后名人，格以古文，往往而失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221646_comment'></div>其精且博又如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221646_comment'></div>然其寄妙技于言意之表，守古学于寂寞之滨，固非浅俗之所能识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221646_comment'></div>且汉之诸儒比肩立，而扬子云以识字称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221646_comment'></div>韩文公言语妙天下，而犹自谓略须识字，字亦岂易识哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221646_comment'></div>观《复古之编》，则其于识字几矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221646_comment'></div>使人之于学也，皆能致其专而求其是，既得之，又能守其所学，而不与时上下，则学虽有小大，其有不至者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221646_comment'></div>不得于今，必得于后世矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221646_comment'></div>张翁求余文以信其传，因叙次如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221646_comment'></div>政和三年九月朔，信安程俱叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_22_1221646_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年10月1日</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，十月一日，为贺铸诗集作序。作品：《贺方回诗集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221647' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221647' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221647?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺方回诗集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和三年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221647")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221647_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221647'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221647'>鉴湖遗老诗凡四百七十二篇，其五字八句诗，鍜练出入古今，为集中第一，其馀大抵名家作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221647_comment'></div>余少读《唐实录》与会稽石刻，见贺季真弃官本末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221647_comment'></div>方开元、天宝之交，天下号无事，文学士见贵重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221647_comment'></div>季真出入禁省，冠道山，友储副，极当世华宠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221647_comment'></div>然一旦不顾，去为千秋观道士，使人望之超然如云汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221647_comment'></div>过秦望，行剡川，未尝不悠然遐想也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221647_comment'></div>季真去后四百二十载，建中辛巳岁，始识其孙方回五湖上，盖鉴湖遗老也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221647_comment'></div>方回落落有才具，观其诗可以知其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221647_comment'></div>中间罢钱官及通守两郡，辄谢病去，为祠岳吏，又一旦挂衣冠，客吴下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221647_comment'></div>穷达虽不同，其勇退乐闲，故有鉴湖馀味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221647_comment'></div>然余谓方回之为人，盖有不可解者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221647_comment'></div>方回少时，侠气盖一座，驰马走狗，饮酒如长鲸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221647_comment'></div>然遇空无有时，俛首北窗下，作牛毛小楷，雌黄不去手，反如寒苦一书生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221647_comment'></div>方回仪观甚伟，如羽人剑客；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221647_comment'></div>然戏为长短句，皆雍容妙丽，极幽闲思怨之情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221647_comment'></div>方回忼慨多感激，其言理财治剧之方，亹亹有绪，似非无意于世者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221647_comment'></div>然遇轩裳角逐之会，常如怯夫处女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221647_comment'></div>余以谓不可解者，此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221647_comment'></div>余奇穷，抗脏可憎，方回多交游，乃独以集副授余曰：「子好直，美恶无溢言，为我评而叙之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221647_comment'></div>此亦岂其不可解之一端耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221647_comment'></div>政和三年癸巳岁十月朔，信安程俱叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_20_1221647_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1113&endYear=1113')">1113年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，除夕作诗。作品：《癸巳岁除夜，诵孟浩然归终南旧隐诗有感，戏效沈休文八咏体作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527257' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527257' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527257?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸巳岁除夜诵孟浩然归终南旧隐诗有感戏效沈休文八咏体作<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>北阙休上书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527257")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527257_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527257'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527257'>说将且<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作日）</span>不暇，于时真自疏。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527257_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527257'>深惭叔孙子，未办茂陵书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527257_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527257'>正自饥欲死，敢言忠有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527257_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527257'>平生畎亩志，本不羡严除。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527257_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527257'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527257_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527258' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527258' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527258?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>南山归敝庐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527258_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527258'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527258'>故庐今茂草，新构羡茅茨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527258'>久慕泉石约，空令猿鹤悲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527258'>一廛端可共，三径复谁期。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527258'>会结忘年友，归云茹紫芝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527258_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527258'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527258_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527259' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527259' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527259?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>不才明主弃</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527259_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527259'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527259'>沃壤有多稼，良工无废材。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527259'>固知时不弃，正坐老无媒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527259'>病骥终难驾，寒花不易开。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527259'>古来天下士，取次没蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527259_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527259'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527259_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527260' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527260' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527260?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>多病故人疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1113年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527260_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527260'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527260'>雁足慵难寄，鸡栖出厌频。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527260'>路长时有梦，人远遽如新。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527260'>胶漆唯穷士，云泥隔要津。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527260'>嚣嚣亦何病，懒放任天真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527260_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527261'>先秋同柳弱，早白误山高。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527261_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527263'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527263'>腷膊南枝鹊，铿宏半夜钟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527263_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_527035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>空相僧舍书事</a><span class='authorDate'>（癸巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527035")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527035'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527035'>午景入疏竹，堂阴筠粉香。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527035'>疏帘扑空翠，无风自微凉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527035'>棋声破禅寂，日转幡影长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527035'>霏烟触垂瓜，泛乳搜枯肠。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527035'>投局起寻胜，徘徊雨花堂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527035'>巢莲见灵龟，信有千岁祥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527035'>徐观乃跛鳖，圉圉循菰蒋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527035'>笑罢得叹息，是非可兼忘。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527035'>却坐对谈麈，冰松想千章。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527035_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527035'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_527035_0'>⑴ 自注：杜甫为功曹，云“束带发狂欲大叫，簿书何急来相仍。”是日江、赵、潘以幕职事去。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527035_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='995e0fee7ca34479b654849b3838f333_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("995e0fee7ca34479b654849b3838f333");'><span id='995e0fee7ca34479b654849b3838f333' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　回苏州，叶梦得有信至，作诗。作品：《卞山信至三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_527013' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527013' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527013?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡州叶翰林寄示近诗次韵八首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>卞山信至三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527013'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527013'>公昔奉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>阡陇，二毛不胜簪。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527013'>扶杖事耘植，咿唔<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>杂呻吟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527013'>耿耿霜露感，遑遑蓼莪心。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527013'>浮云为愁容，鸟兽亦哀音。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527013'>徘徊动行路，下比元与任。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527013'>宿草今已长，新松郁森森。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527013'>尚有五芝秀，荧荧烂如金。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527013'>为公赋南陔，凯风吹我襟<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527013'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527013_comment'></div></div><div 原作鸣，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_527013_0'>⑶ 自注：公庐墓芝生墓（三字原作之生庐，据四库本改）次道旁，故有五芝之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527013_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527014' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527014' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527014?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>卞山信至三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527014_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527014'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527014'>行云本无心，虚舟但乘流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527014'>主人非逋客，不使芳杜羞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527014'>鸣驺入山谷，黾勉赴所求。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527014'>明知廊庙具，岂为猿鹤留。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527014'>朝来尺素书，联翩自岩丘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527014'>平安喜筠柏，宁论橘千头。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527014'>岂无木石居，吾非若人俦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527014'>既与世同乐，那容不同忧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527014_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527014'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527014_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527015' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527015' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527015?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>卞山信至三首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527015_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527015'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527015'>往客霅溪上，舒娥几亏盈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527015'>深穷卞<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_2_527015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527015'>夜投<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>阿兰若，松窗待朝明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527015'>济胜剧许掾，评诗陋钟嵘。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527015_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_527015_0'>⑶ 自注：金石，见杜子美寄声事苏大侍御书诗。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527015_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，秋夜抒怀，呈寄友人。作品：《秋夜写怀，呈常所往来诸公，兼寄吴兴江仲嘉八首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_526959' class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526959")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526959_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526959'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526959'>秋声不关人，倦客偏入耳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526959'>萧萧舞黄叶，策策振疏苇。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526959'>明知壮则老，摇落固其理。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526959'>如何石心人，慨叹中夜起。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526959'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_526959_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526960' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526960' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526960?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526960'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526960'>蓬藋没三径，藤蔂上瓜庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526960'>时闻步屧声，款关问何如。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526960'>定坐无杂语，文章较精粗。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526960'>马融辞东观，抗脏与世疏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526960'>顾此穷巷士，华颠空著书<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：属王元规防。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526960_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_526961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526961'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526961'>外监嗟已远，吾犹识其孙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526961'>森然见孤韵，辨作悬河翻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526961'>颇携未见书，过我樵无烟<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：属贺方回铸。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526962'>青青千丈松，不改冰雪容。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526962'>坐阅蒲与柳，飘萧随雨风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526962'>寒松老益高，蒲柳老益衰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526962'>流萍况无蒂，复与飞蓬期。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526962'>却扫计不早，出门欲何之<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526962'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_526962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526962'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_526962_0'>⑴ 自注：属方子通惟深。余壬午岁常过子通，赋诗有云是中有幽人，厉志凌秋霜。又云会当从之子，濯足万里流。俯仰十二年矣，愧此高人。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526962_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_526963' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526963' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526963_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526963'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526963'>剥啄惊牛枕，轩昂见长身。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526963'>苍髯如脩竹，定非俯仰人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526963'>德公卧襄阳，不踏官府尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526963'>此老颇似之，酒酣见天真。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526963'>结庐甚幽独，已办老圃邻。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526963'>披榛时一来，数面久益亲<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：属杨彝父懿孺。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526963_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_title_526964_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526964'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526964'>二士出吴下，诸生有杨王。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526964'>纵横三千字，坐可致玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526964'>词章乃糠秕，不直粟一囊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526964'>穷居似韩子，草树亦荒凉。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526964_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526964'>时能出佳句，慰我秋夜长<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526965'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526965'>物色一如此，凄风薄人衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526965'>忽使梨枣间，缠绵生茧丝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526965_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526966'>方春万物遂，苑籞及冰谷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526966'>奇穷坐迂疏，此事计已熟。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526966'>如何半世间，生理常刺促<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526966_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
