自注：二篇属江仲嘉。仲嘉有气节，多难，比有伉俪之戚，故云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526966_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1114&endYear=1114')">1114年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，与蒋有道交游，赋诗。作品：《与蒋子有道丁丑相从吴下之适，感而赋诗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。蒋有道事迹不详。）</span><div id='poem_527271' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527271' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527271?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与蒋子有道丁田相从吴下之适感而赋诗</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲午）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527271")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527271_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527271'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527271'>三径旁临招隐溪，子真池馆叩林扉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527271'>拿舟雪夜多乘兴，步屧春风每醉归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527271'>居舍相望一牛吼，官途常作二凫飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527271'>试寻邀月持杯地，共觉劳生四十非。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527271_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527271'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527271_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年10月1日</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，李侯给衢州开化县新学书与图，十月一日，为衢州开化县新学作记。作品：《衢州开化县新学记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1221710' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221710' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221710?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州开化县新学记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和八年十月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221710")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221710_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221710'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221710'>开化县学故在县治之西，其址不能五亩，旁无壖地，右倚山足，因高接庑，以布讲席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221710_comment'></div>大成之殿，顾在平地，斋宇趣完，未中程度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221710_comment'></div>自初构迄今，更十数令，顾地势不可复广，莫能易而大之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221710_comment'></div>今县令李侯旬视学区退，则大惧，以谓自大观学法行天下，西被氐羌，南踰牂牁，岭海万里之外，荒漠不毛之地，皆为郡县置学官，师弟子弦诵之声相闻，三尺之童不谈天人之道，咏颂功德以志荣名、取显仕者，舆台樵牧知笑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221710_comment'></div>今开化虽小邑，僻在山谷间，当句越之穷处，然在舆图，尚为次近地，奉诏令、蒙教养犹毂下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221710_comment'></div>县之造士秀人，岁不绝于贤能之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221710_comment'></div>又今天下宾兴士群至于王廷，与备官使于中外者，必自县学始，则学法之行，繄乡县为根本，顾不重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221710_comment'></div>而县学舍乃不称，县令安所逃责？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221710_comment'></div>则相方绳址，得县南临溪爽垲之地而营之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221710_comment'></div>乃状其事请于郡，郡言上使者，得钱四十万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221710_comment'></div>取人屋之籍于官者十四间，益以故学之材与亭观之废无用者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221710_comment'></div>厥既蒇事，工徒赴功，如治私舍，邑豪里氓亦底其力，盖不三旬而众工释用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221710_comment'></div>高门有严，面埶端邃，庙象宏显，巍然有临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221710_comment'></div>命教之堂，师长之舍，周庐广庑，若承若翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221710_comment'></div>基坚材良，皆倍于故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221710_comment'></div>士气舒豫，雍雍洋洋，行道之人，过者衽轼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221710_comment'></div>于是李侯走书与图至吴下以抵俱曰：「开化，子之乡邑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221710_comment'></div>新学成，宜有文以记岁月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221710_comment'></div>固愿以请，而众亦以为子宜」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221710_comment'></div>俱生晚，不及熙宁、元丰之初以与诸生齿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221710_comment'></div>今兹壮且老，顾以饥寒走四方，而学校益隆，又不得预养士数，以相与燕间揖逊于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221710_comment'></div>今得托词新学以纪侯之绩，其又何辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221710_comment'></div>若夫道学之序，饬励之端，所以开示于方来者，则学法粲然，皆圣上所建立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221710_comment'></div>又辟雍奖谕之书、八行之碑，与凡诏札具在，俱不敏，勉记新学之成云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221710_comment'></div>李侯名光，会稽人，好古强志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221710_comment'></div>起诸生为吏，而所立皆不苟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221710_comment'></div>奉法爱人，文檄不妄下，庐里怀之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221710_comment'></div>新学之成，实政和五年八月甲子十月丁酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221710_comment'></div>通直郎、管勾岱岳观程某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1221710_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，叶梦得知蔡州，作诗赠行。作品：《叶内翰赴淮西》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527252' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527252' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527252?labeling=true' target='_blank'>叶内相<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作史）</span>赴淮西</a><span class='authorDate'>（1115年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527252")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527252_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527252'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527252'>向来英妙压鳌头，去国三年白鬓秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527252'>萧傅岂烦更吏治，贾生元自赞皇猷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527252'>高文已得江山助，远业宁为管晏留。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527252'>闻说云亭已除地，正须椽笔纪鸿休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527252_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527252'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527252_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1115&endYear=1115')">1115年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，叶梦得寄诗，和之。作品：《次韵叶翰林见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527244' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527244' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527244?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叶翰林见寄<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（乙未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527244")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527244_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527244'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527244'>雅望清班亦醉翁，暂令槐阁曳铃空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527244'>更评他日归贤守，画诺何人称治中<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527244'>便合追锋来就日，已知投刃有成风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527244'>贻书千里兼金意，俎豆常怜断尾雄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527244'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527244_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527244'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527244_0'>⑴ 自注：蔡州今为汝南郡，故得用汝南故事。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527244_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527245' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527245' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527245?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（乙未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527245_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527245'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527245'>相望千古一涪翁，还向江湖四壁空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527245'>病目自甘桃李后，野麋难着凤麟中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527245'>未成下泽还乡里，且寄穷阎蔽雨风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527245'>举世知音常契阔，空悲沉抑为谁雄。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527245_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527245'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527245_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='426595efdcd3418483b3e9f44fd6ae5b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("426595efdcd3418483b3e9f44fd6ae5b");'><span id='426595efdcd3418483b3e9f44fd6ae5b_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1117')">1116-1117年</a>，39-40岁</div><div id='426595efdcd3418483b3e9f44fd6ae5b' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年4月1日</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，常平司新移公宇，四月一日为之作记。作品：《京西北路提举常平司新移公宇记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1221711' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221711' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221711?labeling=true' target='_blank'>京西北路提举常平司新移公宇记</a><span class='authorDate'>（政和六年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221711")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221711_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221711'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221711'>政和四年冬，诏复置四辅郡，颍昌府领南辅都总管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221711_comment'></div>于是京西北路常平使者言，常平司故治颍昌，今颍昌隶畿内，当徙治所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221711_comment'></div>部州惟蔡大州，处一路中，道里径，易于督察，报应便，且近徙省劳费。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221711_comment'></div>敢以请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221711_comment'></div>奏可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221711_comment'></div>时朝奉郎、信安余侯实提举常平事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221711_comment'></div>明年，奏下，则于蔡城东南隅得官地若干亩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221711_comment'></div>夏六月兴土功，冬十月毕涂雘，为屋二百八十六间，吏舍居十三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221711_comment'></div>又明年，余侯以书属某记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221711_comment'></div>某惟余侯信厚敏明，自试吏至为御史、部使者，其为政循理而行，奉法度惟谨，不为赫赫名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221711_comment'></div>然所历有实绩可纪，无事于斯记也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221711_comment'></div>辞不听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221711_comment'></div>某惟古建官列为公、卿大夫、士，其栋宇、车服、器用之文皆有等衰存焉，贵与贱亦各安其所当得，而无怍怨于其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221711_comment'></div>故虽大启尔宇，山川土田，而不为泰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221711_comment'></div>一堂五亩，还庐以桑，而不为偪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221711_comment'></div>彼诚知建官所以待天下之贤能，非以私天下之贤能也，凡以为国与人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221711_comment'></div>所谓公、卿、大夫、士，其职非惠人，则乂人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221711_comment'></div>其克有禄位，非有功于国，则有劳于国者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221711_comment'></div>其任大，其享大亦宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221711_comment'></div>惟外使者，常平专以惠人为本，人为重，使者因以重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221711_comment'></div>盖常平之职，掌常平免役之政令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221711_comment'></div>谨视岁之早晚丰俭，以颁敛出纳，而赒万人之艰阨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221711_comment'></div>周咨川原山泽之利害，以阜人财、任土事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221711_comment'></div>通泉府之货贿，以平节贾；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221711_comment'></div>禄庶人之在官者，以纾人力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221711_comment'></div>凡鳏寡孤独废疾之人受食焉，共其养生送终之具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221711_comment'></div>其凡有二，曰常平之法，取于人者以予人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221711_comment'></div>免役之法，取于人者以治人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221711_comment'></div>是法也，更元丰、绍圣至于今，兹盖三圣人而后备，一以惠人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221711_comment'></div>其维持衍绎，繄使者是赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221711_comment'></div>其守金谷如制阃外，其称丰荒如持权衡，其急民隐如救焚溺，是能守我三圣人之良法，以宣上泽于一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221711_comment'></div>则所谓惠乂人与劳于国者，使者有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221711_comment'></div>夫如是，居则广厦跨闾里，出则车马光原隰，以奔走八州五十县之人，盖亦未为泰已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221711_comment'></div>然则经度之勤，栋宇之壮，无足为余侯记，而独喜余侯之有以称也，又安得不书？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221711_comment'></div>政和六年夏四月甲子，具位程俱记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1221711_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，从江大方学《内丹诀》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1116&endYear=1116')">1116年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，有次韵张祠部诗。作品：《次韵张祠部见示》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。张祠部事迹不详。）</span><div id='poem_527238' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527238' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527238?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵张祠部见示</a><span class='authorDate'>（丙申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527238")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527238_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527238'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527238'>大涤先生不讳贫，鬓髯虽白脸长春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527238'>三江鱼美东曹后，二柳泉甘慧晓邻<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527238'>怀组归来无长物，挂冠谁复并清尘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527238'>自怜出处俱违性，旋结衡茅寄此身。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527238'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527238_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527238'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527238_0'>⑴ 自注：《南史》张融与陆慧晓并宅云云。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527238_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，与叶梦得酬唱尤多。诗最迟应作于1116年或次年元夕（正月十五日），姑系于此。作品：《元夕块坐，用叶翰林去年见寄元夕诗韵写怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_527017' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527017' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527017?labeling=true' target='_blank'>元夕块坐因用叶翰林去年见寄元夕诗韵写怀<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527017")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527017_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527017'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527017'>儿童逐遨戏，先春祷春晴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527017'>心如飘风快，目若冰壶明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527017'>宁为惜日计<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作许，据四库本改）</span>，所愿佳节并。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527017'>老来见纷丽，如乾闼婆城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527017'>流光不可挽，譬彼空中声。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527017'>那知节物佳，翛然谢将迎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527017'>幽灯对简编，历历记所更。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527017'>斯须闭关卧，鼻息惊雷鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527017'>寤念<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作言）</span>北山北，田家已催耕。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527017'>胡为异乡久，空寒猿鹤盟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527017_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527017'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_527017_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527018' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527018' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527018?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527018_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527018'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527018'>短日良易暗，凝阴有时晴。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527018'>何人劝之照，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_527018", 527018, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>烛燎</span>皆争明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527018'>今年春苦寒，寒威剧幽并。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527018'>连绵积三白，云埋阖庐城。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527018'>深泥浃新雨，行路无人声。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527018'>藜灯不来下，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_527018", 527018, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>箕卜</span>岂复迎。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527018'>朝来日照梁，天气忽已更。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527018'>稍闻桥市间，箫鼓远近鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527018'>吴人尚游乐，急如赴春耕。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527018'>唯有穷巷士，守穷如守盟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527018_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527018'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_527018_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，与叶梦得酬唱尤多。诗最迟应作于1117年或次年元夕（正月十五日），姑系于此。作品：《蔡州叶翰林寄示近诗次韵八首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_527009' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527009' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡州叶翰林寄示近诗次韵八首 诸葛莱</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527009")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527009_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527009'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527009'>三<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>雄未辨谁朱紫，祇有群狙聊作使。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527009'>卧龙偃蹇正躬耕，一饱但知藜藿美。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527009'>平生习气故难尽，品藻芜菁传锦里。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527009'>投醪饮河真有味，置薤留根何足比。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527009'>要知茹草可终身，肯作染羹摇食指。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527009'>公今啸<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作笑）</span>诺坐堂上，方丈盈前宁少此。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527009'>戏持微草调诸伧，笔势滔滔下南纪。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527009'>云亭漫吏食不足，几欲送穷烦郁垒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527009'>拔毛蒸瓠当家鹜，漱石枕流徒厉齿。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527009'>因公始识武侯鲭，盖地何当似芣苢<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527009'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_527009_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527009'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_527009_0'>⑴ 原作二，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_9_527009_0'>⑵ 自注：芣苢，车前也。退之诗榆荚车前盖地皮。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527009_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　卜居苏州蜗庐期间，与叶梦得酬唱尤多。诗最迟应作于1118年或次年元夕（正月十五日），姑系于此。作品：《复次韵酬叶翰林见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷七。）</span><div id='poem_527175' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527175' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527175?labeling=true' target='_blank'>复次韵酬叶翰林见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527175")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527175_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527175'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527175'>渭川十顷青，上谷千灶墨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527175'>县河供拂石，濡笔应未足。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527175'>公初入承明，神采映冰玉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527175'>孤芳信难群，廉士故可辱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527175'>虚怀得逢蒙，泛爱近藉福。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527175'>终然翟公题，正堕杨朱哭。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527175'>于今十年后，犹作一麾出。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527175'>何当还宣温，不用求钓筑。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527175'>遥知西湖柳，蔽芾谁敢秃。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527175'>应馀金石文，会使天雨粟。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527175'>留连借三辅，夏木今再绿。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527175'>斯文咏公归，怅望非我独。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527175'>羁怀老无堪，览卷百忧触。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527175_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527175'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_527175_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1117&endYear=1117')">1117年</a>　春，蔡州作临芳观于牙城之上，太守为叶梦得，为之赋，时卜居苏州蜗庐。作品：《临芳观赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1221283' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221283' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221283?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临芳观赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　政和七年春）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1117年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221283")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221283_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221283'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221283'>政和七年春，蔡州作临芳观于牙城之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221283_comment'></div>太守，翰林叶公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221283_comment'></div>俱为之赋云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1221283'>览飞霞兮鳌丘，翩乘风兮下游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221283_comment'></div>观豫俗兮安舒，弭霓旌兮少留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221283_comment'></div>衷天孙之锦裳，戏毫端兮组绣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221283_comment'></div>驱陈前兮万象，付心宰兮锤钩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221283_comment'></div>抚曾城兮坐啸，眷山川之旷修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221283_comment'></div>矗连云乎蜚观，奂翚檐兮上浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221283_comment'></div>席沈息兮南荣，带汝颍兮双流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221283_comment'></div>仰晨宵兮闛阖，寄心驰兮北眸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221283_comment'></div>俯动植兮欣荣，繄童耋兮休休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221283_comment'></div>眇桑麻兮牟稷，蔼平皋兮广畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221283_comment'></div>嗛臣力之何有，归鸿庬乎帝猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221283_comment'></div>方青春兮浩荡，落斯成以旨羞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221283_comment'></div>揭临芳之高颜，聊托物兮优繇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221283_comment'></div>面柴潭之滈衍，被璀错兮华洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221283_comment'></div>森号风之僵木，曶丰艳兮敷柔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221283_comment'></div>知造化之神骏，宁与物兮为谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221283_comment'></div>等孤荄与丛蔓，何此恩兮彼仇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221283_comment'></div>纷游鳞与翔羽，亦乘和而出幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221283_comment'></div>蹇鷤䳏兮将鸣，见有生之王囚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221283_comment'></div>阅芸芸于过目，澹无心乎献酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221283_comment'></div>念千古兮一眴，经向来之乐忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221283_comment'></div>笑东门兮黄犬，异晋国之青油。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221283_comment'></div>吷奇功兮剑首，谢酣寝于矛头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221283_comment'></div>想平舆之二龙，匪罦置兮可蒐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221283_comment'></div>岂嵁岩兮无伏，羌莫挽兮谁侜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221283_comment'></div>要曳涂之灵介，胜泣河之鲍䐹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221283_comment'></div>缅句吴之旅人，守冰墟兮海陬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221283_comment'></div>闻凌虚之杰观，恍梦寐兮将求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221283_comment'></div>憖赢粮而即之，嗟道岨其奚由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221283_comment'></div>傥从公乎嵺廓，挹浮丘之长衰<span class='inlineComment2'>（恊）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221283_comment'></div>览熙熙兮无外，同春台兮九州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221283_comment'></div>写登高之遐素，斯可以补由庾而赋何尤也<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山小集》卷一二。）</span>。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_33_1221283'></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1221283_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='7c707f4400254f359c6619789838a7f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7c707f4400254f359c6619789838a7f4");'><span id='7c707f4400254f359c6619789838a7f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，53岁</div><div id='7c707f4400254f359c6619789838a7f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年2月24日</a>　在秀州知州任上。二月二十四日，因弃秀州保华亭事被捕至平江，将斩以徇，既复释之。<br /></div>
-----end

徐州（彭城）

-----title
吴江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a994b893c3f94fdeaa160a908d680b79_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a994b893c3f94fdeaa160a908d680b79");'><span id='a994b893c3f94fdeaa160a908d680b79_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1100')">1097-1100年</a>，20-23岁</div><div id='a994b893c3f94fdeaa160a908d680b79' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　任苏州吴江县主簿。时徽宗即位，肆赦放免秋苗。本县复行催，理吏持文书通签，公即申县请准赦蠲放，而转运司牒准省符讲求遗利。公申状，见者惊叹，亦或指以为狂。作品：《吴江县申乞准赦放秋苗议状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十五。）</span>《吴江回申讲求遗利状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文《北山小集》卷三十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221584' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221584' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221584?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴江县申乞准赦放秋苗议状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221584")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221584_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221584'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221584'>今月某日，户案手分将到文引通签，准使符，准转运衙牒，催索去年苗米事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221584_comment'></div>右，某伏见圣主初临宝位，思布惠泽于天下，故赦文内将应干积欠并行蠲放，以至去年秋苗亦行放免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221584_comment'></div>宣赦之日，百姓闻之皆稽首感抃，驩颂之声如出一口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221584_comment'></div>寻已翻黄张挂，及行下乡村，晓示人户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221584_comment'></div>今来旬日，乃复催索，不唯使皇泽不下于民，亦何忍使圣主即位之初失大信于天下，非小故也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221584_comment'></div>况去秋苗米，富家上户必已于上中限内送纳入官，今来已入末限，欠苗米未纳之人多是残零或贫氓下户，力未能及者，此尤仁政所当先及者，乃不被覃霈之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221584_comment'></div>又况所得无几，徒格上恩，且伤国体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221584_comment'></div>某窃以谓准赦蠲放，乃为得宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221584_comment'></div>所有文引，难以书押行出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221584_comment'></div>谨具议状申县，伏乞备申使府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221584_comment'></div>伏候裁旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1221584_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221585' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221585' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221585?labeling=true' target='_blank'>吴江回申讲求遗利状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1097年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221585")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221585_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221585'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221585'>准县牒，备准使府准转运衙牒，准省符<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云。）</span>右，某窃谓财用之在天下，譬之众州之水潴之万顷之陂，决漏既多，乾涸可待，乃欲崎岖回远，引线脉之流以益之，不如塞其陂之决漏而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221585_comment'></div>今诸路赋入，则众川是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221585_comment'></div>万顷之陂，则总计是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221585_comment'></div>决漏如江，则无艺之费是也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221585_comment'></div>崎岖回远，引线脉之流以益之，则讲求遗利是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221585_comment'></div>所谓无艺之费，某疏远小吏，不能尽知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221585_comment'></div>徒见顷年以来，纲运自杭而西以过县境者，有曰明金生活，有曰佛道帐殿，有曰花石者，挽舟之卒所支口券米岁无虑若干千石，计工无虑若干万夫，家粮借请之数不与焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221585_comment'></div>然比造作之费，曾何足道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221585_comment'></div>窃以谓天下无艺之费如此类者傥一切罢之，则神宗皇帝息民裕国之政具在，守而勿失，可以有馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221585_comment'></div>某愚无知，妄陈管见，谨具申县衙，伏乞备申使州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221585_comment'></div>伏候裁旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221585_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1221585_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年</a>　在苏州吴江县主簿任上，其文初被叶梦得所识。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年</a>　在苏州吴江县主簿任上。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1099&endYear=1099')">1099年</a>　在苏州吴江立三高祠。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在苏州吴江县主簿任上，早春，值江上颇有春色，偶成绝句遣兴。作品：《数日江上颇有春色偶成绝句遣兴五首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>数日江上颇有春色偶成绝句遣兴五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527536")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527536'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527536'>柳怯馀寒未展眉，嫩黄轻绿渐依依。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527536'>春郊正好闲行处，不及游蜂自在飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527536'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527536_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527537' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527537' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527537?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚辰）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527537_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527537'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527537'>错莫江梅春信迟，晴熏寒蕊雪团枝。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527537'>年来顿失寻春意，一任高楼玉笛吹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527537_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527537'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527537_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527538?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚辰）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527538'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527538'>远树参差数点烟，目穷天际水黏天。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527538'>背人叶叶风帆去，应有鸱夷万里船。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527538_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527538'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527538_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527539?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚辰）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527539'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527539'>不奈江头春色何，暖光摇日涨晴波。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527539'>凭栏何处牵幽兴，杨柳沙洲一钓蓑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527539_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527539'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527539_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527540?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚辰）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527540_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527540'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527540'>露压浓烟染远山，垂虹真在画图间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527540'>平湖渺渺思无限，何日浮云伴我闲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527540'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527540_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年3月</a>　在苏州吴江县主簿任上，三月，与僚佐拜奠范蠡、张翰、陆龟蒙，有文。作品：《三高堂诗序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_1221655' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221655' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221655?labeling=true' target='_blank'>三高堂诗序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221655")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221655_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221655'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221655'>蠡位越相、禄万钟，去之如涕唾，则后世角毛铢之得，冒坎擭而不省者可以少沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221655_comment'></div>翰进退无必，随时而保身，则出处之意得托菰鲈以示好，又何深哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221655_comment'></div>龟蒙江湖一匹夫，然于其不合，视执位无如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221655_comment'></div>其交如皮日休，终见污于贼巢，彼独挺然玉峙，无一衅可指擿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221655_comment'></div>与夫攫金挟炭之夫，盖万万矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221655_comment'></div>夫左手据图籍，右刃掠其吭，虽冥惷不为也，揣是而求之，轻重得矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221655_comment'></div>然世固有抱利权，逐势燄，死不反顾，为天下僇笑者，几何人哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221655_comment'></div>其于轻重之思，是又出冥惷者之下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221655_comment'></div>然则是三子者祠而旌之，固可以训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221655_comment'></div>元符二年，吴江既立三子者像，明年三月甲子，安于祠堂，令与僚佐拜而奠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221655_comment'></div>某谓俗奔竞久矣，冀得守道自重，确乎不可拔，足以风百世而驱天下者，将矫浮俗而归之，庶几清节之为贵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221655_comment'></div>然望之而未见，抑有之而未闻耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221655_comment'></div>今居是邑，特仰三子之志，意其知时而退，不迷于出处之道，盖君子之所悦闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221655_comment'></div>凡我同志，其系之以诗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1221655_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在苏州吴江县主簿任上作《松江》二赋，远近腾颂之。时间不可确考，姑系于此。作品：《松江赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（赋见《北山小集》卷十二。）</span>《后松江赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（赋见《北山小集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1221278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>松江赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221278")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221278'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221278'>鸱夷子皮既弃越相，乘扁舟、携西子、溯东流，方将家五湖以长迈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221278_comment'></div>屣万钟而不留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221278_comment'></div>放若巨鱼纵大壑，脱若六骥驰坦道而挟轻辀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221278_comment'></div>时则八荒收云，千里一碧，狂澜不兴，远岫凝色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221278_comment'></div>目尽意往，云天出没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221278_comment'></div>引风樯以悲啸，趣烟波而不极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221278_comment'></div>于是遇亡是叟而问津焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221278_comment'></div>曰：「三江之凑，实为五湖，地脉四远，衍为松江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221278_comment'></div>汹汹浑浑，溶溶洋洋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221278_comment'></div>孤岑连嶂，七十有二，眇若散螺黛于微茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221278_comment'></div>五湖之中，大曰包山，风穴昼暝，霜林夏寒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221278_comment'></div>暮烟屯其叠翠，冬实累其错丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221278_comment'></div>麟鹤之所憩，蛟鼍之所渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221278_comment'></div>山中之人，忘世与年，条桑缥缈之下，采石明月之湾<span class='inlineComment2'>（包山有缥缈峰、明月湾。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221278_comment'></div>草衣木茹，泊若追羲盘而与还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221278_comment'></div>江流之穷，是则归墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221278_comment'></div>王百谷于一吸，环齐州于一区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221278_comment'></div>大鹏奋翅于泱漭，烛龙洗光于咸虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221278_comment'></div>由江而下，二百馀里，布帆无恙，尚可以朝海门而暮方壶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221278_comment'></div>虽然，善贾者据其会，善搏者扼其吭，方趣南则遗北，既画圆而失方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221278_comment'></div>今子将揽众物之会，莫若遐观乎中央。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221278_comment'></div>惟是江湖之接，二州相望，散荒墟于垤块，识断岸于毫芒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221278_comment'></div>尝试与子至中流而四顾，阴霾郁兴，不辨云水，天高日出，万顷在目者，五湖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221278_comment'></div>冈岫相属，如走如伏，溟濛突兀，乍见乍失者，包山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221278_comment'></div>拥松江之上流，穷海道于一苇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221278_comment'></div>时矫首而斯尽，固可以访渔樵而种鲂鲤，亦优游而卒岁矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221278_comment'></div>吾子以谓何如」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221278_comment'></div>子皮曰：「然务外游者有待，乐内观者无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221278_comment'></div>吾方以日月为烛，六合为宫，参天地以为友，从四海之诸公，乘云气、御飞龙，指包山于遗砾，视五湖于一钟，松江之胜，又安能芥蒂于胸中乎」！</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1221278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221278'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北山小集》卷一二。又见《吴都文粹》卷五，绍定《吴郡志》卷一八，《历代赋汇》卷二五，《古今图书集成》山川典卷二七八、职方典卷七○三。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221278_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1221279' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221279' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221279?labeling=true' target='_blank'>后松江赋</a><span class='authorDate'>（1100年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221279")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221279_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221279'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221279'>程子既为《松江赋》，假鸱夷子皮、设亡是叟以为词，是夜，梦有夫颀然而长，黧色而修髯，叩舷而称曰：「松江之胜，吾子之词侈矣，然子亦闻吴越之遗事乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221279_comment'></div>唯而答曰：「长桥卧波，截江之冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221279_comment'></div>飞栏叠架，排雾行空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221279_comment'></div>万景所会，而垂虹屹立乎其中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221279_comment'></div>吾尝登垂虹、顾二渚，尚想夫霸国之争雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221279_comment'></div>方其践忍鸟喙，差耕石田，祸起腋下，谋钳悟先，则吴阵江北，越军江南，杀气朝合，军声夜严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221279_comment'></div>衔枚北渡，奋为两翼，方风驰而雾障，顿雷轰而电击。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221279_comment'></div>吴卒麇溃，江流赭赤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221279_comment'></div>毕夫椒之世仇，偿会稽之胆食。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221279_comment'></div>于此，盖夫子之雄绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221279_comment'></div>乃自太湖、过横山，乱越来之溪，登姑胥之台，吊亡国于游鹿，指血化于黄埃，挽艅艎以凌江，卷旌旗而南归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221279_comment'></div>则夫子于此退身行意，揖勾践而长辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221279_comment'></div>盖与夫咎犯之贪天，子推之独贤，歌龙蛇而激愤，块然与槁木而偕燔者，不可同日而言矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221279_comment'></div>閒者五季棼乱，钱镠崛兴，苏据都会，乃淮浙之必争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221279_comment'></div>徐约先拔，孙儒继焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221279_comment'></div>彼得之不能以岁月守，我守之不能以岁月宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221279_comment'></div>则江之两厓，相为二城，镇威武之右境，遏淮南之寇兵，实用武者之所凭<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221279_comment'></div>版图入朝，置为县治，画井疆、设群吏，皋亩棋别，居庐鳞次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221279_comment'></div>带以千尺之桥，捍以百里之塘，舟舆所通，楼观相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221279_comment'></div>曾城邑之几时，翳乔木之苍苍矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221279_comment'></div>吾尝叹曰，一江方东，虽逝不流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221279_comment'></div>阅世事之万变，去莫知其所遁，而来莫知其所由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221279_comment'></div>今之松江，其昔之松江耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221279_comment'></div>抑夜半之藏舟，失万世于俯仰，尽贤愚于一丘？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221279_comment'></div>夫子亦尝吊抉眼之忠魂，而访伏剑者之灵游不乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221279_comment'></div>子皮不对，顾谓西子，援琴而歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221279_comment'></div>歌曰：「霰雪纷兮云霏霏，带长铗而佩宝璐兮，子安适而不归？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221279_comment'></div>岁晼晚而将暮兮，路既壅而中迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221279_comment'></div>嗟二子之不返，折疏麻而搴杜若，羌摇摇其遗谁」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221279_comment'></div>馀音未息，󰚋然而觉，棹头载歌，付千古于一笑。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1221279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221279'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221279_0'>⑴ 吴江，钱氏时谓之南北两城防遏所。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1221279_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏州吴江县主簿任满，作诗抒怀。作品：《数诗述怀》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_526971' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526971' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526971?labeling=true' target='_blank'>数诗述怀</a><span class='authorDate'>（庚辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526971")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526971_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526971'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526971'>一生共悠悠，今者曷不乐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526971'>二十起东山，误为微官缚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526971'>三年瞬眸耳，邮传那久托。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526971'>四壁自萧然，青编束高阁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526971'>五更霜钟动，起视星错落。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526971'>六律聿其周，忽忽更岁籥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526971'>七哀哦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>幽韵，感念惊独鹤。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526971'>八极岂不广，衰怀了无托。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526971'>九原叹多贤，死者那可作。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526971'>十里望烟村，天随去寥廓<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作廊，据四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526971'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_526971_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526971'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_526971_0'>⑴ 原作我，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526971_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　苏州吴江县主簿任间颇有宦绩，后主簿高文虎作曾程堂，以寓景仰，李处全与范成大俱有记。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
太湖
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='dd23f0de9574433891177dcce0cf4955_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dd23f0de9574433891177dcce0cf4955");'><span id='dd23f0de9574433891177dcce0cf4955_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1101')">1100-1101年</a>，23-24岁</div><div id='dd23f0de9574433891177dcce0cf4955' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年8月</a>　辟差舒州太湖茶场，八月，编《侑坐元龟》并作序。作品：《侑坐元龟序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221645' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221645' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221645?labeling=true' target='_blank'>侑坐元龟序</a><span class='authorDate'>（元符三年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221645")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221645_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221645'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221645'>治乱之端，率常隐于寻常忽眇之间，初若不足畏向者，积而致之，至于不可御。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221645_comment'></div>善恶皆然，治乱因之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221645_comment'></div>观秦汉以来，享国历世唯唐最长，而中绝于孽后，败乱于艳妃，陵夷于宦官，衰弱于藩镇，所经之变不一，未有不生于所忽而积于至微，以至于大坏而不可复振者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221645_comment'></div>使祸福之来常如山摧川溃，霆震而至，则虽至愚，孰不知所避就？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221645_comment'></div>唯其隐于寻常忽眇之间，初若不足畏向者，故蹈覆辙而不知常相踵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221645_comment'></div>方天下初定，魏徵劝太宗以行仁义、以致太平者，如封伦辈往往笑而排之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221645_comment'></div>唯太宗能用其言，行于寝食起居、造次颠沛之间，卒以致贞观之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221645_comment'></div>然求其若为仁、若为义者，则未易彰彰论之，岂非其积微，故其成速耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221645_comment'></div>及明皇在位久，当盈成丰豫之时，春秋既高，方且宠一妇人，进一小人，退一正士，逍遥游宴，姑以乐其当年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221645_comment'></div>意必以谓是岂足以伤生害治，又况乱天下者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221645_comment'></div>卒之百敝随生，抢攘悖缪，至于逆胡称兵，陷两京，焚九庙，四海横溃，而卒至于衰微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221645_comment'></div>此何故也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221645_comment'></div>岂非生于所忽而积于至微，以底于是哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221645_comment'></div>唐之治乱善恶之大致，较然明白者，前哲论之备矣，余独取其治乱善恶之萌，而祸乱之所由生，足以为世戒者，裒而为书，名之曰《侑坐元龟》云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221645_comment'></div>元符庚辰秋八月，信安程俱谨序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1221645_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1100&endYear=1100')">1100年</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上作。作品：《移竹》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527220' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527220' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527220?labeling=true' "poem_title_527220")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_527220_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527220'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527220'>寓目无清致，兴怀要此君。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527220'>影移千亩月，枝散五湖云。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527220'>凤实和筠得，龙苞带箨分。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527220'>伤根同柏大，剪叶异芝焚。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527220'>拔筱衣沾粉，连鞭藓破纹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527220'>虚心宁择地，直节任离群。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527220_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年3月3日</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上，三月三日作。作品：《寓斋记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1221712' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221712' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221712?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寓斋记<span class='inlineComment2'>（建中靖国元年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年3月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221712")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221712_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221712'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221712'>客有至寓斋而叹曰：「夫以介然之形，措之天地之间，不百年寓耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221712_comment'></div>于一寓中，而暂寓于东南西北之游者又几何耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221712_comment'></div>是斋之士，其又寓暂寓于其间者乎」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221712_comment'></div>程子曰：「何特此耳！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221712_comment'></div>天，气之积者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221712_comment'></div>地，块之积者，寓于空而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221712_comment'></div>日月星辰，山河草木，又寓于二物而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221712_comment'></div>请观子之一形，寓视于目，寓听于耳，寓声于口，寓神于此百骸五藏之间，是则子之所谓介然之形者，盖有寓之者焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221712_comment'></div>不有寓之者，是则粪壤濡沫而已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221712_comment'></div>子于此而求之，又有不寓者存而天地万物之所以寓者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221712_comment'></div>晋陵钱定国显道尉吴江，予名其燕处曰寓斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221712_comment'></div>定国盖尝闻道云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221712_comment'></div>建中靖国元年三月甲子，信安程某记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1221712_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上，结识贺铸。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='aa15032c3044478f912cd78d4f82efb5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aa15032c3044478f912cd78d4f82efb5");'><span id='aa15032c3044478f912cd78d4f82efb5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上作。作品：《日日》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span>《看镜》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527353' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527353' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527353?labeling=true' target='_blank'>日日</a><span class='authorDate'>（辛巳）</span><span class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527353_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527353'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527353'>日日长川去，行行万化新。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527353'>回思几年事，已似隔生人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527353'>章甫宁资越，连城漫入秦。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527353'>应知衣内宝，肯浑隙中尘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527353_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527353'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527353_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527355' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527355' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527355?labeling=true' target='_blank'>看镜</a><span class='authorDate'>（辛巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_527355_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527355'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527355'>看镜恍如梦，今余犹昔余。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527355'>身经几堕甑，迹寄一蘧庐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527355'>仙客有遐怨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，孔兄无近书。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527355'>尘缨与蕙帐，两事欲何居。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527355'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527355_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527355'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_527355_0'>⑴ 自注：昔人以鹤为仙客，鸭为闲客。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527355_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1101&endYear=1101')">1101年</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上。时见吴郡包山采太湖石，作赋。作品：《采石赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1221277' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221277' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221277?labeling=true' target='_blank'>采石赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（并序　建中靖国元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1101年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221277")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221277_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221277'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221277'>建中靖国元年，以修奉景灵西宫，下吴兴、吴郡采太湖石四千六百枚，而吴郡实采于包山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221277_comment'></div>某获目此瑰奇之产，谨为赋云：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1221277'>吴吏采石于包山也，洞庭乡三老趋而进、揖而言曰：「惟古浑浑，物全其天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221277_comment'></div>金藏于穴，珠安于渊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221277_comment'></div>机械既发，剖蚌椎矿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221277_comment'></div>不翼而飞，无胫而骋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221277_comment'></div>刳山探海，阶世之竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221277_comment'></div>乃若富媪赘瘤，则为山岳，茂草木于毛肤，包崭岩于骨骼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221277_comment'></div>与瓦甓其无间，何于焉而是索<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221277_comment'></div>今使者窥复穴、荡沉沙，搜奇礓于洞脚，劂巧势于丘阿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221277_comment'></div>呼灵匠以运斤，指阳侯使息波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221277_comment'></div>竖江山之崿崿，积剑阁之峨峨<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221277_comment'></div>莫不剔山骨、拔云根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221277_comment'></div>贞女屹立，伏虎昼奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221277_comment'></div>督邮攘袂以相睨，令史临江而抗尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221277_comment'></div>虽不遭于醯沃，岂有恨于苔痕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221277_comment'></div>嗟主人之不见，信羊牧之犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221277_comment'></div>何一拳之足取，笑九仞之徒勤<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221277_comment'></div>既而山户蚁集，篙师云屯，输万金之重载，走千里于通津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221277_comment'></div>使山以为骨，则土将圮；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221277_comment'></div>使玉以为璞，则山将贫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221277_comment'></div>煮粮之客，叹终年之无饱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221277_comment'></div>谈玄之老，持一法其谁论<span class='inlineComment2'>（《神仙传》：白石生煮为粮。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221277_comment'></div>尝闻不为无益，则用之所以足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221277_comment'></div>惟土物爱，则民之所以淳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221277_comment'></div>怪斯取之安用，非野夫之得闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221277_comment'></div>敢请使者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221277_comment'></div>吏呼而语曰：「醯鸡不可与语天，蟪蛄不可与论岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221277_comment'></div>矧齐侯之读书，岂轮人之得议」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221277_comment'></div>三老曰：「极治之世，樵夫笑不谈王道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221277_comment'></div>至圣之门，鄙夫问而竭两端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221277_comment'></div>野人固愿知之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221277_comment'></div>对曰：「上德光大，孝通神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221277_comment'></div>阐原庙之制，妥在天之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221277_comment'></div>以谓物不盛则礼不备，意不尽则享不精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221277_comment'></div>故金瑰珠琲，天不秘其宝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221277_comment'></div>樟楠楩梓，地不爱其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221277_comment'></div>而青州之怪，犹未足于充庭，故于此乎取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221277_comment'></div>且太行之石英，采谷城之文石，以起景阳于芳林者，魏明之侈陋也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221277_comment'></div>菲衣恶食，卑宫室以致美乎祭祀者，夏禹之勤俭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221277_comment'></div>上方罢后苑之作，缓文思之程，示敦朴以正始，尽情文而事神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221277_comment'></div>此固上德之难名者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221277_comment'></div>抑尝闻之，西有未夷之羌，北有久骄之虏，顾蹀血之未艾，乍游魂而送死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221277_comment'></div>方将不顿一戈，不驰一羽，殄丑类于烟埃，瞰幽荒于掌股，庶黄石之斯在，傥素书之可遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221277_comment'></div>抑又闻之，三德虽修，不去指佞之草；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221277_comment'></div>万国虽和，犹豢触邪之兽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221277_comment'></div>盖邪佞之蛊心，犹膏肓之自腠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221277_comment'></div>惟属镂之无知，顾尚方之奚救？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221277_comment'></div>故将铸采石以为剑，凛竖毛于佞首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221277_comment'></div>若是，则在边无汗马之劳，在廷无履霜之咎也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221277_comment'></div>抑又闻之，尧不能无九年之灾，汤不能无七年之旱，虽阴阳之或盭，岂闲纵之可缓？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221277_comment'></div>故将放鞭石于宜都，回雨旸于咳眄<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221277_comment'></div>抑又闻之，扶耒之子，有土不毛；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221277_comment'></div>抱瓮之老，有茅不薅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221277_comment'></div>富者侈而贫者惰，游者逸而居者劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221277_comment'></div>虽齐导之有素，奈狡焉而是逃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221277_comment'></div>故将取嘉石以列坐，平罢民于外朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221277_comment'></div>抑又闻之，日不蔽则明，川不阏则清，听之广者视必远，基之固者构不倾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221277_comment'></div>方披旒而出黈，俾伐鼓而扬旌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221277_comment'></div>盖萧墙之戒，坐远于千里；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221277_comment'></div>朽索之驭，益危于薄冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221277_comment'></div>矧四者之无告，尤圣人之所矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221277_comment'></div>故将尽九山之赤石，达万县之穷民」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221277_comment'></div>三老悚然而兴曰：「圣治盖至此乎」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221277_comment'></div>吏曰：「此犹未也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221277_comment'></div>若其造化掌中，宇宙胸次，弥纶两仪而执天之行，燮理二气而袭气之母，此包牺之妇所以引日星之针缕，方将鍊五色以补天，育万生于一府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221277_comment'></div>既无谢于襄城之师，又何惊于藐姑之处？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1221277_comment'></div>吾亦与汝饮阴阳之和而游万物之祖矣，又何帝力之知哉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑹</sup>」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1221277_comment'></div>三老稽首再拜曰：「鄙朴之人，聋瞽其知，鹿豕其游，窃亿妄议，乃今知之」。</div><div id='poem_sentence_67_1221277_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221277'><span class='label'>按：</span>《北山小集》卷一二。又见《吴都文粹》卷六，绍定《吴郡志》卷二九，正德《姑苏志》卷一四，《历代赋汇》卷二三，《古今图书集成》坤舆典卷一六，山川典卷二八一。<br /><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_1221277_0'>⑴ 《晏子春秋》：灵山以石为身，以草木为毛发。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_10_1221277_0'>⑵ 江淹《江上之山赋》曰：「百里兮崿崿。」张载《剑阁铭》：「岩岩梁山，积石峨峨。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221277_0'>⑶ 王韶之《始兴记》：「中宿县有贞女峡，水际有石，似女子。」《幽明录》：「宜都建平界有倚石，如二人。俗谓一郡督邮，争界于此。」《南康记》：「湘源有长濑，其旁石或像人二，人名为令史。」卢仝《赠石诗》：「主人虽不归，长见生人面。」又：「自惭埋没久，满面苍苔痕。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_48_1221277_0'>⑷ 《穆天子传》：「天子升于采石之山，取采石焉，铸以成器于黑水之上。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_50_1221277_0'>⑸ 《荆州图副》：「宜都有石穴，穴有二石，俗云其一为阳，其一为阴。旱鞭阳石则雨，雨鞭阴石则晴。」</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_66_1221277_1'>⑹ 卢仝诗：「女娲伏羲妇，引日月之针、五星缕。」</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1221277_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年8月1日</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上，八月一日，撰《韩文公历官记》并作序。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《北山小集》未收《韩文公历官记》及序，文见粤雅堂丛书本。）</span><div id='poem_1221657' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221657' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221657?labeling=true' target='_blank'>韩文公历官记序</a><span class='authorDate'>（1102年8月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221657")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221657_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221657'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221657'>予友彭城陈传道师仲，少时尝藁具韩文公历官出处之概，凡传不载而见于他书者，将一二以记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221657_comment'></div>比出旧藁示予，予疑未广，因补次其遗，十增七八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221657_comment'></div>其所考订微言小节，纤悉毕具，盖得于文公之文者为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221657_comment'></div>至其论辨是非，与夫坎𡒄之致，则著之尤详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221657_comment'></div>盖古之贤士，信道坚笃，其出身从仕，下不为卑贱之所诎塞，既贵，不为高官厚禄之所诱制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221657_comment'></div>而唯辨不苟已，事不苟随，虽关摧节沮而终不挠者，如文公可得见耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221657_comment'></div>故乐记其事而传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221657_comment'></div>若本传所载，此则略云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221657_comment'></div>崇宁元年八月一日，信安程俱致道叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1221657_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221657'><span class='label'>按：</span>《韩文公历官记》卷首，粤雅堂丛书本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221657_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1102&endYear=1102')">1102年9月</a>　在舒州太湖茶场任上，以上书论时政被斥为邪等，罢归。时间当在本年九月十八日庚子以后。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
高邮
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='38cb58baa7e6481c9547f8c7edf1043b_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("38cb58baa7e6481c9547f8c7edf1043b");'><span id='38cb58baa7e6481c9547f8c7edf1043b_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　罢官游历高邮，书怀。作品：《高邮旅泊书怀寄淮东提举蔡成甫观兼呈郑使君弇三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527228' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527228' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527228?labeling=true' target='_blank'>高邮旅泊书怀寄淮东提举蔡成甫观兼呈郑使君弇三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（癸未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527228")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527228_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527228'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527228'>久客颇自厌，长歌胡不归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527228'>束书方有适，捧檄定焉依。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527228'>尘里音容改，山中信息稀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527228'>十年长漫浪，深觉负荷衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527228_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527228'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527228_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527229' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527229' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527229?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（癸未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527229_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527229'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527229'>命矣周南滞，时哉冀北空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527229'>居无刮目视，动有转喉穷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527229'>泛宅如蛮蜑，淫书伴蠹虫。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527229'>飘蓬故人念，赖有绣衣公。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527229_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527229'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527229_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527230' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527230' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527230?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（癸未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527230_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527230'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527230'>长夏热欲死，迎秋气已清。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527230'>蚊蝇任来往，螟螣尚纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527230'>行止厌人问，栖迟真自惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527230'>使君高义在，解榻见深情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527230_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527230'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527230_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
南京（上元）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='874f3215e31a47f4a89062675d6055cd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("874f3215e31a47f4a89062675d6055cd");'><span id='874f3215e31a47f4a89062675d6055cd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>，26岁</div><div id='874f3215e31a47f4a89062675d6055cd' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1103&endYear=1103')">1103年</a>　罢官游历金陵，秋天作怀古诗。作品：《癸未秋金陵怀古三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527542' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527542' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527542?labeling=true' target='_blank'>癸未秋金陵怀古三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527542")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527542_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527542'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527542'>壮士狂歌击唾壶，追风老骥望长驱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527542'>山川形势端如此，当日宁无一伯符。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527542_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527542'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527542_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527543?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1103年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527543'><div class='poemSentence' -----title
富阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='93d076093d9542adaac2802dd960e65a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("93d076093d9542adaac2802dd960e65a");'><span id='93d076093d9542adaac2802dd960e65a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年</a>，27岁</div><div id='93d076093d9542adaac2802dd960e65a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年1月7日</a>　是年人日有诗寄友，地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《人日书怀兼寄吴中三二友》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九，人日，即正月初七。）</span><div id='poem_527232' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527232' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527232?labeling=true' target='_blank'>人日书怀兼呈吴中二三友</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527232")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527232_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527232'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527232'>东西南北走红尘，又见江淮草木薰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527232'>小谢篇章成画饼，卧龙功略付浮云<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527232'>栖迟枳棘今如许，啸傲冰<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作笑傲风）</span>霜赖此君<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527232'>俛俯折腰成底事，故交千里漫离群。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527232'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527232_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527232'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_527232_0'>⑴ 自注：孔明为孙权画赤壁之策，及谢惠连为司徒府法曹时，与予今年齿正同。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_527232_1'>⑵ 自注：太湖多竹，所居有修篁千个。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527232_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1104&endYear=1104')">1104年2月</a>　罢官，春游富阳观山亭，赋诗。作品：《登富阳观山亭三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527377' class='_poem'><div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527379' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527379?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span
