-----title
常州（武进）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='bc8b0bfe967141fd8130297be87d1912_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc8b0bfe967141fd8130297be87d1912");'><span id='bc8b0bfe967141fd8130297be87d1912_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>，30岁</div><div id='bc8b0bfe967141fd8130297be87d1912' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1107&endYear=1107')">1107年</a>　大观初，监常州市易务。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2e1bf3ee788f4602a78c86496d05c832_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2e1bf3ee788f4602a78c86496d05c832");'><span id='2e1bf3ee788f4602a78c86496d05c832_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1110')">1108-1110年</a>，31-33岁</div><div id='2e1bf3ee788f4602a78c86496d05c832' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年8月15日</a>　在监常州市易务任上，常州新修市易务，八月落成，有文记之。作品：《常州新修市易务壁记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1221708' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221708' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221708?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州新修市易务壁记<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观二年八月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年8月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221708")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221708_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221708'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221708'>熙宁中，始置市易务于通邑要郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221708_comment'></div>常州以编氓居十数间，粗更门户墙壁，榜为市易务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221708_comment'></div>及今垂四十年，不知先为编氓居又几何年，中间再废，益不治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221708_comment'></div>栋宇故庳隘，岁加摧腐，每大风雨，岌岌将遂颠压。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221708_comment'></div>规制又甚浅劣，平旦侧肩庭中，无所旋足；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221708_comment'></div>吏坐两壁间，与之争席；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221708_comment'></div>按察时至，门不容车盖，率步以入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221708_comment'></div>余初至，谋撤其甚者而新之，则会凡匠事之材用上郡，为钱十二万有畸，凡再裁损，乃上使者，使檄下郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221708_comment'></div>又再裁损，亶为钱八万六千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221708_comment'></div>时久阙常平使者，又八月，会提点刑狱盛公兼行常平事，则具状走其府，又以记道不可已之故，即日檄下予钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221708_comment'></div>先是，以书与所会之材抵张渚镇官田，渚与江南接，多山木大竹，幸为我期于市取足焉，钱至则取之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221708_comment'></div>又以告埏埴者，毕具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221708_comment'></div>又移晋陵、武进鸠众工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221708_comment'></div>盖檄下十日而庀工即事，二十五日而完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221708_comment'></div>木之工二百八十，竹之工百有九，瓴甓之工百三十，涂饰之工百五十，凡为工六百六十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221708_comment'></div>募于市者十之一，晋陵之所集者十之九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221708_comment'></div>其畚除运负之工又四百五十有畸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221708_comment'></div>以负重出纳食其力于务者七夫，与警守之卒供其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221708_comment'></div>警守故十卒，前十日，兵马司取其三，其所留大抵军营小儿，占尺籍而名廪帛耳，其为力不足以半一夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221708_comment'></div>是三十日间，率寅入酉出，公察其勤惰，时其难易而均督之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221708_comment'></div>暮休，面赋其直，不容吏下隐刻，故其赴功也力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221708_comment'></div>材审其良窳，因其旧新而材用之，下至竹头木附无弃物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221708_comment'></div>凡为屋十五间，堂三楹，极高故屋五尺，挟以二舍，引以二庑，惟称庑舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221708_comment'></div>为库六，其题曰懋、迁、有、无、化、居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221708_comment'></div>门高三仞，庭倍前日，其为址尽，是无馀隙矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221708_comment'></div>深不能八丈，前官道，后人居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221708_comment'></div>广不能十丈，左右皆人居，故技止于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221708_comment'></div>它日使尝见故区者视之，则固以为广厦为难能矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221708_comment'></div>如其不然，以为陋可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221708_comment'></div>昔叔孙婼羁于晋，其所馆虽一日必葺，去之如始至，君子纪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221708_comment'></div>况任其事、食其禄而为三年淹者，其可鄙其居而苟于事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221708_comment'></div>且乘田委吏，圣人之所不忍，余何敢苟？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221708_comment'></div>然余贱有司也，出纳贸迁之为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221708_comment'></div>若其市材供事，鸠工董役，则故有任其事者，非吾任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221708_comment'></div>余不忍坐视越尊俎而代庖，是亦泰多事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221708_comment'></div>厥既讫工，则志本末刻诸石，而材用工役之事加详焉，盖使来者知余之勤且艰如此，而其所建立止如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221708_comment'></div>余不负市吏，而市吏负余，亦足叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221708_comment'></div>大观二年八月十五日，信安程俱书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_37_1221708_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，八月以后，迁通仕郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1108&endYear=1108')">1108年</a>　在监常州市易务任上。冬，在常州题奖谕敕碑。是年会试，常州得士最多，得到皇帝嘉奖，故立碑。作品：《常州州学奖谕敕碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1221777' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221777' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221777?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州州学奖谕敕碑<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1108年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221777")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221777_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221777'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221777'>皇帝临御之七年，实大观元年，诏班学令于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221777_comment'></div>教养之数，劝沮之方，有目有凡，毕协理义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221777_comment'></div>简大如江汉，明信如四时，灏灏恢恢，咸出天翰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221777_comment'></div>于是郡县百吏奔走厥职，宣达圣志，小大丕应，荒陬绝徼，一变邹鲁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221777_comment'></div>二年，辟廱会试，郡国贡士无虑数千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221777_comment'></div>其升诸司马、命于天子者百四十人，而常州得士之多为天下最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221777_comment'></div>皇帝嘉之，诏三省亟论功加赏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221777_comment'></div>十月，制下，知州事若蒙进官朝请大夫，州学教授虙以宣德郎充职如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221777_comment'></div>于是诸生侈上之赐，相与言曰：「进贤之诏，载在令甲，播之天下，岂惟一邦宠休，凡士与荣焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221777_comment'></div>若具石表刻明诏，列词其下，祗颂上德之万一，与夫劝学报功之意，惟明有孚，郡国诸侯徯承不怠，师儒之官训率有叙，惟允惟公，迄有成绩，以饬稚昧于无穷，岂不益显」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221777_comment'></div>咸曰唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221777_comment'></div>则系以词曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1221777'>惟古有学，惟治之原，何以先之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221777_comment'></div>德教是宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221777_comment'></div>《泮水》之诗，有据有游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221777_comment'></div>六艺具焉，以文厥修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221777_comment'></div>秦汉以来，倚吏为治，本之不图，绳其已至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221777_comment'></div>天肇神考，见道之赜，斡神之机，鼓舞群物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221777_comment'></div>作我多士，一开其天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221777_comment'></div>以澡以摩，今三十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221777_comment'></div>于穆皇帝，遹广圣猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221777_comment'></div>渊跃鲔鲂，山有杞枢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221777_comment'></div>声教溥渐，穷日所照。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221777_comment'></div>目睨指摽，万邦是效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221777_comment'></div>惟邦有常，士子之区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221777_comment'></div>雷风所覃，不约而趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221777_comment'></div>都试辟雍，俊造是罗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221777_comment'></div>论定而官，莫与常多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221777_comment'></div>皇帝曰都，承宣有劳，实惟师儒，乂我俊髦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221777_comment'></div>是达是化，以礼以文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221777_comment'></div>奉我新书，以迄有成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221777_comment'></div>惟守暨师，既受上赏，天语有嘉，四方是仰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221777_comment'></div>倬彼宸翰，虽在四方，揭之龟趺，俾人不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221777_comment'></div>士之不忘，惟上之赐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221777_comment'></div>潭潭学区，大烹以饫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221777_comment'></div>岂惟养之，择师以教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221777_comment'></div>车服稍徒，以酬有造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221777_comment'></div>岂惟官之，于以旌之，显示万邦，以劝厥来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221777_comment'></div>上德之怀，惟称厥求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221777_comment'></div>惟克有为，有守有猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221777_comment'></div>多士之修，有邦之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221777_comment'></div>洋洋德音，万世由之。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1221777_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年10月1日</a>　在监常州市易务任上，十月初一，为林虙《西汉诏令》作序。作品：《西汉诏令序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221653' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221653' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221653?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西汉诏令序<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观三年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年10月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221653")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221653_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221653'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221653'>右《西汉诏令》四百一章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221653_comment'></div>旧传《西汉文类》所载尚多阔略，吴郡林德祖虙实始采括传志，参之本纪，凡断章析简，掇之无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221653_comment'></div>方荟蕞在纸，未遑诠录，间以示余，余因取其具稿，以世次先后，自高祖至平帝，人别为篇，又差考岁月，纂而成书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221653_comment'></div>且叙次其末曰：古之盛王与道为一，故其酬酢之间，理言遗事皆足以为万世法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221653_comment'></div>是以事为《春秋》，言为《尚书》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221653_comment'></div>而《书》之所传，自唐虞、夏、商、周，上下千数百载间，而其存则今之五十八篇而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221653_comment'></div>由秦汉以来，置学官弟子诵说研究，至有白首没身莫能诣其极者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221653_comment'></div>大哉王言！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221653_comment'></div>盖圣人之防表也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221653_comment'></div>自五十八篇而后，起衰周至五代之末，又千数百载间，其为诏令温醇简尽，而犹时有三代之遗法者，唯西汉为然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221653_comment'></div>其进退美恶，不以溢言没其实，其申饬训戒皆至诚明白，节缓而思深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221653_comment'></div>至丛脞大坏之馀，其施置虽已不合古道、当人心，然犹陈义恳到，雍容而不迫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221653_comment'></div>此其一代之文流风未泯，顾犹不可及，又况文实兼盛哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221653_comment'></div>昔者文中子以圣人之重自任，乃始断自七制之主，列为四范，以续典、谟、训、诰、誓、命之文，然其书世不传，莫得而述，故备载如彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221653_comment'></div>德祖以学行名搢绅，方将以文词为时用，方今昭回之章、丝纶之美固已轹绝中古，陋汉唐而莫称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221653_comment'></div>是书也，虽未能比唐虞、夏、商、周之隆，庶其或者亦足为王言之斧藻、《尚书》之鼓吹云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221653_comment'></div>大观三年岁次己丑十月壬申朔，信安程俱叙。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221653_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，与林虙时有唱和，时间应在是年前后，姑系于此。作品：《和林德祖惠山诗一首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷三。程俱大观四年（1110）庚寅有《用德祖韵送毛彦时二首》，则得知是年前后程俱与林虙定有唱和。）</span><div id='poem_526984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和林德祖惠山诗一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1109年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526984")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526984'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526984'>好山如幽士，胜绝不可攀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526984'>往者天姥梦，长谣愁谪仙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526984'>兹山出平野，秀特无株连。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526984'>招提倚云锦，森然见林峦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526984'>幽寻无十里，正处闲忙间<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作涧，据四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526984'>入门心目静，世累若可捐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526984'>灵泉出土脉，汩汩无流难。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526984'>茶神瀹浮乳，方士沉馀丹。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526984'>我生猿鹤姿，颇有山水缘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526984'>何时共清赏，杖屦穷崖巅。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_526984_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1109&endYear=1109')">1109年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，有和柳宗元诗。作品：《和柳子厚读书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_526936' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526936' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526936?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和柳子厚读书</a><span class='authorDate'>（己丑）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526936")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526936_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526936'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526936'>事贱反<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>多暇，居卑适无虞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526936'>人间不争地，聊此谢畏途。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526936'>岂无营营子，熟视付一吁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526936'>廛中亦何有，坐听日月逾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526936'>展卷阅千古，置书忘万殊。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526936'>不妨权子母，亦复商有无。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526936'>平生仅识字，乃与忧患俱。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526936'>持此游学海，层台渐积苏。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526936'>年来但遮眼，颇觉心恬愉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526936'>囊钱<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作粟）</span>足自饱，肯怖驺朱儒<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作讵肯羡侏儒）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526936'>起卧一榻间，兀如橛株拘。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526936'>凉风北窗下，不减愚溪愚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526936'>谁能三万卷，悬头苦劬劬。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526936'>小极正当寐，睡魔不须驱。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526936'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_526936_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526936'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_526936_0'>⑴ 原舌及，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526936_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年4月14日</a>　在监常州市易务任上，四月十四日，为江褒祖墓作记。作品：《江氏小山祖墓记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十九。）</span><div id='poem_1221707' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221707' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221707?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江氏小山祖墓记<span class='inlineComment2'>（大观四年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年4月14日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221707")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221707_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221707'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221707'>开化县治开元乡，故常山县地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221707_comment'></div>县宇之北，有丘墟隐然，域以垣堑，族葬其中，望之松槚蔚然者，江氏之祖岁郳之墓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221707_comment'></div>按江氏家谱，系出济阳，统之八世孙曰世源官信安，留家不去，实始为信安人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221707_comment'></div>又五世孙岁郳等五丧葬常山县开化乡之万岁里小山村，其地四十亩，则此墓是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221707_comment'></div>繇始葬及今十六世，子孙益蕃，属益远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221707_comment'></div>又散处郊邑，或仕或游，藉令归且处，岁时祭扫，上不过四世而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221707_comment'></div>小山墓地既广，近族之贫者往往寓着其间，岁且久，因以为己产，稍斥卖之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221707_comment'></div>又四域之外，耕艺者相接，岁攘日蹙，莫之谁何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221707_comment'></div>大观三年，乡豪汪氏遂欲葬墓域中，县又取西北隅地构丞舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221707_comment'></div>会诸孙之官学者皆在里中，大骇且惧，则相与愬于县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221707_comment'></div>未得直，乃出康定、皇祐二牒以为證。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221707_comment'></div>其一太常少卿钧任两浙转运使日，具墓地界，俾宗子乃等主之，岁一补治垣墙，则宗司白宗长凡宗人共其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221707_comment'></div>其一尚书郎钺以邻人之侵其地也，言于县，县按所侵地归之，俾宗人祐主之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221707_comment'></div>既出二牒，争者语塞，县即日徙丞舍，凡违法之契尽毁之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221707_comment'></div>于是子孙乃始周域其地为垣墙，稍树松槚，揭其阡曰「江氏皇祖之墓」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221707_comment'></div>然不能四十亩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221707_comment'></div>余友仲嘉褒既与其族父兄子弟事其事，它日，一二语余，且曰：「余惧来日之无穷也，事寖远而寖忘，则其不为前日之𢦤败者几希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221707_comment'></div>余将列其事于石，揭之墓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221707_comment'></div>然非文不传也，莫如子能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221707_comment'></div>余曰：「古人以谓君子之泽不过五世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221707_comment'></div>先王制礼，必以远近戚疏为之节，凡祖子孙上下不能十世，而服则五等而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221707_comment'></div>盖先王所以教天下之中，其制不得不然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221707_comment'></div>先王之制则有节，而人之恩性顾岂有量哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221707_comment'></div>今而以世观之，则虽近而已疏，即吾身以推之，则虽远而益恩，是何言也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221707_comment'></div>且吾之生者为子，子之孙为曾孙，曾孙之曾孙则已不能名矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221707_comment'></div>夫吾之委蜕适数世耳，而遂至于不知何人，岂非虽近而已疏乎，夫安得不悲？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221707_comment'></div>然今吾视听食息于是者，父母之遗体也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221707_comment'></div>求生之所自生，则由祖而上百世可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221707_comment'></div>使人而无祖，则乃今安得视听食息于是者哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221707_comment'></div>以是推之，岂非虽远而益恩乎，夫安得不思？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221707_comment'></div>思且悲，则其惙惙不忘于心者岂有穷耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221707_comment'></div>然则制虽有远近戚疏，而恩性则有至于不能忘者，何可夺也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221707_comment'></div>且江氏小山之祖至太常府君十三世，至仲嘉又四世矣，而其族父兄子弟不忍其墓地之不除，而途人皆得以攘蹙锄刈也，相与出力而营之，以为庶几神灵之复安，而后世知所本也，岂非所谓中有不能忘者故耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221707_comment'></div>今子碣于是，俾后之人过是者知敬戒，岂唯江氏之子孙？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221707_comment'></div>人孰不生且死也，思所以奉祖先、训子孙、保坟墓者，人情均也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221707_comment'></div>繇是而思之，则虽已暴之骨、无名之丘，有不忍易而𢦤之者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221707_comment'></div>其为利顾不博哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221707_comment'></div>然则余其敢爱荒陋之文而无以成子之善也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221707_comment'></div>四年四月壬午，北原程俱记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1221707_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，有诗送毛随。作品：《用德祖韵送毛彦时二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷三。）</span><div id='poem_526985' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526985' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526985?labeling=true' target='_blank'>用德祖韵送毛彦时二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚寅）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526985")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526985_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526985'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526985'>往者玉楼客，栖迟感秋蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526985'>龙钟江海士，屑屑悲穷冬<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526985'>今我亦羁旅，号寒思祝融。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526985'>故乡邈千里，胡马长嘶<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526985'>平生饮最少，亦复贤圣中。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526985'>其谁共谈笑，无乃志所同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526985'>泮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>宫备文质，楩楠饰雕栊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526985'>毛子亦好古，摛辞丽春工。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526985'>飘然适我愿，一舸来自东。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526985'>明时猎英奇，备问罗皋龙。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526985'>逢辰若公等，附凤云从龙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526985'>遥知赋伐木，相望有梁鸿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526985'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_526985_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526985'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_526985_0'>⑴ 自注：孟郊有暮天寒风悲屑屑之句。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_526985_0'>⑵ 原作斯，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_6_526985_0'>⑶ 原作伴，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_11_526985_0'>⑷ 自注：梁鸿东游，思其友高恢，作诗曰鸟嘤嘤兮友之期。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526985_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_526986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526986?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（庚寅）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526986'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526986'>断港冰未泮，海风起蓬蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526986'>君行亦良苦，浮家秋复冬。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526986'>故人一相遇，醉觉心形融。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526986'>道旧有深乐，班荆馀古风。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526986'>何<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>当度杨子，起视东井中。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526986'>未应迫期会，促步佐一同。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526986'>况当万灯燃，流光煖疏栊。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526986'>胡为即言别，系书凭鸟工。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526986'>空令千里月，团团出天东。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526986'>解舟动栖禽，破晓啼匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526986'>酒阑城西道，已失衔烛龙。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526986'>振衣一回首，瞥去如惊鸿。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526986'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_526986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526986'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_526986_0'>⑴ 原作可，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526986_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，有诗。作品：《适轩》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527236' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527236' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527236?labeling=true' target='_blank'>适轩<span class='inlineComment2'>（庚寅岁郭慎求见邀同作）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527236")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527236_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527236'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527236'>厌苦常从乐未央，不如要足两俱忘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527236'>当饥粝食遗三鼎，便<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：一平。）</span>体绨袍胜五章。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527236'>夜雪扁舟千嶂净，午风高枕一窗凉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527236'>飘然自适非人适，肯受辕驹六尺缰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527236_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527236'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527236_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，替表叔王涣之为江褒母作墓志铭。作品：《宋故德兴县君宋氏墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1221786' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221786' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221786?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故德兴县君宋氏墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（为王侍郎彦舟作。　政和元年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221786")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221786_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221786'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221786'>夫人宋氏，郑州管城人，故吏部尚书、赠太尉、谥文安公讳白之曾孙，奉宁军节度副使、检校尚书水部员外郎讳良臣之孙，尚书比部员外郎讳保孙之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221786_comment'></div>母崇德君吕氏，早丧，夫人哀慕如成人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221786_comment'></div>及长，端嫕通敏，事至迎解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221786_comment'></div>奉继母建昌君赵氏得礼之宜，比部每奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221786_comment'></div>择所从，年十八以归信安江氏，为尚书职方员外郎讳楫之冢妇，故朝散郎讳汝明之妻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221786_comment'></div>宋氏世望族，内外姻大抵将相通显家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221786_comment'></div>夫人少长贵富闻，而江氏世儒，被服寒素，土着山谷中，聚食数千指。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221786_comment'></div>夫人无毫发骄气，承上抚下，尽得其驩心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221786_comment'></div>至烹饪蚕桑，若素习者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221786_comment'></div>诸子胜衣，则口授以《孝经》、《论语》。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221786_comment'></div>群儿敖戏处，辄屏不使近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221786_comment'></div>望众中衣服端洁、词貌循衎者，则知其为德兴儿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221786_comment'></div>自朝散君丧，事其姑寿安君周夫人益谨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221786_comment'></div>周夫人治家严整，鲜可其意者，独以夫人为能，饮膳药剂不经手不以进，至属纩犹咨其勤孝云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221786_comment'></div>既就养诸子，处门内事明白简直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221786_comment'></div>朝夕坐堂上，子妇从侍，孙息走前，怡怡如也，僮使䜣䜣如也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221786_comment'></div>大观四年闰月四日，以疾卒于其家，享年六十七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221786_comment'></div>夫人常曰：「吾自念平生无贪嚚𢦤暴一可悔事，期于死生之际如觉寐者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221786_comment'></div>既疾，屏荤味弥月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221786_comment'></div>少间，起居如平时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221786_comment'></div>一日夙兴，复就寝，若将寐者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221786_comment'></div>候之，形神离矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221786_comment'></div>将敛，饰无珠玉，箧无新衣，其于乐施予、尚纯素，又过人远甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221786_comment'></div>盖为江氏妇垂五十年，见其夫以进士决科，繇州县吏至二千石，身被命书，为德兴君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221786_comment'></div>诸子皆好学有立，又相继登第、与乡举，族人钦慕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221786_comment'></div>卒之日，来会哭，皆尽哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221786_comment'></div>夫人生五男六女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221786_comment'></div>曰裒，宣德郎、勾当在京都茶库；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221786_comment'></div>曰褎，宣德郎、知越州馀姚县事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221786_comment'></div>曰袤，曰表，曰褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221786_comment'></div>袤举进士，表幼卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221786_comment'></div>女长适朝散大夫、知蔡州军州事陆偕，次已嫁而归，皆前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221786_comment'></div>次适从事郎、知潭州湘潭县事王居仁，次适宣德郎、知睦州建德县丞毛宽，次适宣德郎、知泗州临淮县事程俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221786_comment'></div>其幼在室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221786_comment'></div>孙男四人，女二人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221786_comment'></div>其孤将以明年正月乙酉葬夫人于常山县定阳乡菱湖之原，前期，以其族人状来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221786_comment'></div>余惟朝散君居乡为笃行君子，仕为清白吏，繄必有内助，故能遂其志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221786_comment'></div>尝闻乡人云然，考状益信，乃为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221786_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1221786'>女子之正，惟辅惟从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221786_comment'></div>其覆则仁，其承则恭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221786_comment'></div>有如德兴，能妇能母。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221786_comment'></div>不汰不嬉，绩我桑杼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221786_comment'></div>卒相夫子，既遂既成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221786_comment'></div>生靡忮行，没有荣名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221786_comment'></div>内德则懋，不显其仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221786_comment'></div>我铭昭之，彤史之资。</div><div id='poem_sentence_45_1221786_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，为华严教院作上梁文，时间不可确考，姑系于此。作品：《常州华严教院上梁文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州华严教院上梁文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221812")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221812'>兰陵胜境，兴国名蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221812_comment'></div>拟开华藏之道场，既画祗洹之界相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221812_comment'></div>仰二天之外护，魔事冰销；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221812_comment'></div>洎四众之知归，檀那云集。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221812_comment'></div>金沙宝网，顿除荒梗之区；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221812_comment'></div>悦柏寒松，共演苦空之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221812_comment'></div>爰伸善颂，用举修梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1221812'>儿郎伟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221812_comment'></div>抛梁东，法水无边不滞空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221812_comment'></div>慧日永将尧日晓，河沙尝在普光中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1221812'>儿郎伟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221812_comment'></div>抛梁西，宝网金沙路不迷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221812_comment'></div>五浊海中成般若，妙华香洁出深泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1221812'>儿郎伟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221812_comment'></div>抛梁南，无胜光明正剧谈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221812_comment'></div>若见只今华藏海，不须辛苦百城参。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1221812'>儿郎伟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221812_comment'></div>抛梁北，不动虚空非智力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221812_comment'></div>大伽蓝后少年场，一一回光销六贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_1221812'>儿郎伟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221812_comment'></div>抛梁上，法界微尘如指掌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221812_comment'></div>普贤楼阁镇长开，目前举足超非想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1221812'>儿郎伟！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221812_comment'></div>抛梁下，无间光明长不夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221812_comment'></div>九幽沉苦證无生，八极含灵安圣化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221812_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1221812'>右，伏愿上梁之后，胜幢永建，苦海蒙庥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221812_comment'></div>咸裂贪嗔之网，共夷人我之丘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221812_comment'></div>广大得毗庐之境，精勤如童子之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221812_comment'></div>仰尧仁之广被，泳周泽之常流。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1221812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1110&endYear=1110')">1110年</a>　在监常州市易务任上，会从官，有文记之，时间不可确考，姑系于此。作品：《常州会三从官致语》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221814' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221814' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221814?labeling=true' target='_blank'>常州会三从官致语<span class='inlineComment2'>（胡、邹、陈。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1110年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221814")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221814_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221814'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221814'>青山绿野，尝传洛下之英词；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221814_comment'></div>金马玉堂，近播汝阴之故事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221814_comment'></div>况复瑶台之彦，相从琳馆之闲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221814_comment'></div>西省南宫，行奉赐环之召；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221814_comment'></div>东阡北陌，时追连璧之游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221814_comment'></div>迨此胜辰，并临高会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221814_comment'></div>恭惟宫使密学、待制侍郎、宫使侍郎，才推人杰，文粲时英。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221814_comment'></div>烨若星辉，适应台躔之象；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221814_comment'></div>屹然山立，共堪鼎足之承。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221814_comment'></div>从容献纳之馀，萧散轩裳之表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221814_comment'></div>知府典乐属棠阴之多暇，及葭管之迎长，式谐既见之心，爰谨加笾之享。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221814_comment'></div>金章照座，回淮海之青春；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221814_comment'></div>玉麈生风，动豫章之白日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221814_comment'></div>宜尽百川之饮，无庸驷马之归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221814_comment'></div>长使此邦，共传嘉话。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221814_comment'></div>但某叨居乐部，获奉宾筵，上悦台颜，敢陈口号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221814_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1221814'>诗书礼乐旧将军，献纳论思两侍臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221814_comment'></div>暂比挥金同宴衎，即看鸣玉侍严宸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221814_comment'></div>风流珠璧辉班著，名节冰霜耸搢绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221814_comment'></div>好与兰陵传盛事，德星应复聚江滨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1221814_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='cfee3aaa87484740bb14eb2bed8f31ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("cfee3aaa87484740bb14eb2bed8f31ce");'><span id='cfee3aaa87484740bb14eb2bed8f31ce_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1125&endYear=1125')">1125年</a>，48岁</div><div id='cfee3aaa87484740bb14eb2bed8f31ce' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春居毗陵，贺铸来访，病甚，以墓志铭托之。<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>居毗陵，服除，复除礼部员外郎，以病告老，不俟报而归。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洪泽（临淮）

id='poem_sentence_1_527269'>芝兰有馀化<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作臭）</span>，桃李竟无言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527269'>远日来千两，他年叹九原。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527269'>死生如可作，安用百身存。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527269_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527269'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527269_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527270' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527270' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527270?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（辛卯）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527270_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527270'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527270'>夷蹠虽殊趣，彭殇共一归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527270'>投荒万里再，乘化百年非。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527270'>细行皆无憾，常言亦造微。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527270'>祇应存信史，千古有沾衣。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527270_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527270'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527270_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在泗州临淮知州任上，春，与江纬、江褒交游，有诗。作品：《寄江彦文纬》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷六。）</span>《和江仲嘉见寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷九。）</span><div id='poem_527500' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527500' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527500?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄彦文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_527500'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527500'>踵息庵前草又青，庵中禅客养黄庭。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527500'>起来何物共吟啸，照眼云山锦翠屏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527500_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527500'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527500_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527278' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527278' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527278?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和江仲嘉见寄<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首　壬辰）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1112年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527278")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527278_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527278'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527278'>荜门蓬舍不知春，车似鸡栖甑有尘。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527278'>千里传情望双鲤，一杯和影祇三人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527278'>交亲离合同巢燕，身世羁危独茧纶。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527278'>四体不勤心扰扰，拟将玄旨问吴筠<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：江修练，故有此句。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527278_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527278'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527279'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527279'>寒谷应殊尺五天，盐车无复望腾骞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527279'>至人未免填沟壑，大隐不如居市廛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527279'>长笑呼鹰思上蔡，独令留石在平泉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527279'>茅茨欲作终焉计，未有沧浪四万钱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527279_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527279'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527279_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1112&endYear=1112')">1112年</a>　在泗州临淮知州任上，秋，有感赋诗。作品：《秋将获水行田中不复留因窾胜通沟引水过堂下小儿以茫苇作车其上昼夜决决不休戏书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷二。）</span><div id='poem_526947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526947?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秋将穫水行田中不复留因窾塍通沟引水过堂下小儿以芒苇作车其上昼夜决决不休戏书</a><span class='authorDate'>（壬辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_526947")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526947_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526947'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526947'>水行山原溉平畴，时当断壶穫且收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526947'>功成则退逝不留，去彼畎遂来清沟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526947'>测之深咫浅可杯，循除㶁㶁环一丘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526947'>堆沙累石隘厥流，势激滟滪吞黄牛。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526947'>谁持机缄设中洲，折芒<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>断苇驾两辀。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526947'>置之不汨亦不浮，六辐眩转无时休。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526947'>推行作止莫可诹，孰居无事供其求。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526947'>迫而后动真无尤，眩转自彼非吾谋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526947'>屈伸臂<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作俄）</span>顷一万周，我无欣厌何名忧。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526947'>孰能观身与此侔，众假合集成坚柔。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526947'>沈轻燥湿交相仇，逝川洄洑更春秋。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526947'>滔滔南北东西游，死生壮老休王囚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526947'>形骸流运我则不，物境万变何其幽。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526947'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_526947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_526947'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_526947_0'>⑴ 原作芸，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_526947_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
湖州（乌程）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2de6ad988d4e4a71b895d2fbf743ef6d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2de6ad988d4e4a71b895d2fbf743ef6d");'><span id='2de6ad988d4e4a71b895d2fbf743ef6d_link' id='poem_sentence_1_526992_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526992'>牢愁不可排，磊块如高冈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526992_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526992'>烦君着酒浇，身世得暂忘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526992_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526992'>举觞漱明月，似觉幽桂香。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526992_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526992'>拟吹三江水，浣此九转肠。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526992_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526996'>中营五亩宅，何必封石窌<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：朱公死，其妻与诸子守之。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526996'>桑麻无外求，茶果供日富。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526996'>夭条列僮奴，花草更黼绣。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526996'>生生所应有，取足谢奔走。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526996'>嗟余四方志<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作忠，据四库本改）</span>，老大无一就。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526996'>对此寸心惊，无因托圭窦。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526996_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526996'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_526996_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_526997' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526997' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526997?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>西庵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526997_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526997'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526997'>是公固麟凤，入兽不乱群。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526997'>吴侬欲争席，但见一幅巾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526997'>篮舆从<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去）</span>逋客，上下寂寞滨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526997'>却行共谈笑，愧此礼意亲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526997'>行行得西庵，杉竹含清薰。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526997'>解衣静盘礴，虚窗蕙烟纷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526997'>濡毫散珠玑，咳唾不自珍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_526997'>曳屣转山足，长林蔽浮云。<div id='poem_sentence_7_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_526997'>旁连众迤逦，上有高嶙峋。<div id='poem_sentence_8_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_526997'>穹窿见深洞，划如敞重闉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_526997'>往者玉京子，翔空驾飙轮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_526997'>于今蜕骨在，坚重踰苍珉。<div id='poem_sentence_11_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_526997'>颇欲穷其源，燃犀问蛇神。<div id='poem_sentence_12_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_526997'>钩穿忽无间，信有仙凡分。<div id='poem_sentence_13_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_526997'>却寻招提路，松风亦随人。<div id='poem_sentence_14_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_526997'>潺潺石桥水，洗尽荆吴尘。<div id='poem_sentence_15_526997_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_526997'>胡床兴不浅，已觉千山曛。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_526998' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/526998?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>夜归</a><span class='authorDate'>（1114年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526998_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526998'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_526998'>日入三籁息，群山郁苍苍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_526998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_526998'>巾裾湿烟雾，宛转度涧冈。<div id='poem_sentence_1_526998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_526998'>涓涓暗泉鸣，冉冉松筠香。<div id='poem_sentence_2_526998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_526998'>林梢吐纤月，露叶琐碎光。<div id='poem_sentence_3_526998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_526998'>归来叩禅扉，幽灯对绳床。<div id='poem_sentence_4_526998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_526998'>相羊有馀适，笑咏白雪章<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：翰林是日有诗数首。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_526998_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_526998'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_526998_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷二。诗题，《程俱年谱》系节录，今据四部丛刊续编《北山小集》补全。）</span>《次韵江司兵寄示所和赵司录相从饮解嘲之句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span>《戏赠江仲嘉司兵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷五。诗题，《程俱年谱》系节录，今据四部丛刊续编《北山小集》补全。）</span>《同赵叔问、江仲嘉游法华之胜为曲水会有客先焉还饮舟中分韵赋诗得山字一首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷五。）</span><div id='poem_527038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527038?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527038'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527038'>纷华眩人剧朱碧，子独好书如好色。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527038'>王孙被服甚寒生，射策君门先破的。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527038'>荣州书窟三万卷，锦囊付此庞眉客。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527038'>南游句吴北大魏，亦复徒劳问刀笔。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527038'>不唯唇齿腐经史，正自云山锁胸臆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527038'>老来息交思简事，为子忘劬废晨昔。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527038'>春风满帆送归舸，回首清游如昨日。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527038'>知君名骏定千里，不待朝庭访幽侧。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527038_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527038'>有书时寄雁南飞，顾我渔樵正争席。<div /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527039'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527039'>云亭老人穷不死，故园茅屋荒苍苔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527039'>阖庐城中一亩地，已辨瓮牖锄蒿莱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527039'>吴兴上佐吾党士，十年纵赏西王台。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527039'>要须酩酊酬此别，不离万顷添金杯。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527039_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527039'>明朝相望即湖海，纵有美酒何为哉。<div /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_526967_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_526967'><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527034' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527034?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵江司兵寄示所和赵司录相从饮解嘲之句</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527034")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527034_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527034'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527034'>卜居林塘静，禽鱼乐融融。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527034'>阳和一披拂，照烂黼绣工。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527034'>柔条罥繁枝，幽香来晚风。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527034'>谁谓武陵远，临清千树红。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527034'>俯仰村郭间，从容圣贤中。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527034'>暮见月圆缺，馀光入疏栊。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527034'>朝乘日车作，坐守四壁空。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527034'>遥想赵与江，屈身薄书丛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527034'>正类鹳雀碧，未为覆盆烘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527034'>禄隐寄簪笏，神游在方蓬。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527034'>时时望西山，把酒一笑同。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527034'>茗碗倾石鼎，山蔬出筠笼。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527034'>不妨问中圣，何暇赋恼公。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527034'>赵子五车腹，春秋富终童。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527034'>居然出其类，俨如黄发翁。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527034'>江子事超旷，町畦漫无封。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527034'>但见磊砢姿，温温若春浓。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527034'>人生迭相笑，伧父嘲吴侬。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527034'>鸱夷与井瓶，忧乐殊初终。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527034'>且当从所好，迂辔若为容。<div id='poem_sentence_19_527034_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_527034'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_527034_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527036' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527036' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527036?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戏赠江仲嘉司兵</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527036")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527036_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527036'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527036'>君不见谢公栖迟乐东土，起作司马征西府。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527036'>莫年谈笑有穰孙，鹤唳风声走强虏。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527036'>又不见子猷剡川高兴阑，肯随鹤书落人间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527036'>不知骑曹底官职，朝来拄颊看西山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527036'>平生清真翠岩老，泉石膏肓偶同调。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527036'>岁寒落落见孤松，不忍低眉宁枯槁。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527036'>年来无米继朝炊，闻说吴兴富鱼稻。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527036'>不妨来作古司<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>兵，士卒投醪止凫藻。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527036_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_527077_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527080' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527080' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527080?labeling=true' target='_blank'>南窗夜集叔问戏取樟木脑然雪为灯因与仲嘉叔问联句一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527080'>性空本无方，水火不留碍<span class='inlineComment2'>（致）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527080'>阳生至阴中，此理固有在<span class='inlineComment2'>（问）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527080'>初疑水焚槐，忽若镜加艾<span class='inlineComment2'>（致）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527080'>又如大海中，神龙出光怪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527080'>冰姿映烈焰，势恐不两大。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527080'>原燎正焮腾，汤沃忽崩败<span class='inlineComment2'>（嘉）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527080'>涓涓煖泉涌，熠熠寒光碎<span class='inlineComment2'>（问）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527080'>伟哉六合间，恢诡不胜载。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527080'>阴风结飞雨，来自<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作日，据四库本改）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527080'>九天外。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527080'>苍樟出芳液，根节依大块。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527080'>初非气相求，又岂天所配。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527080_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527080'>如何冰炭仇，乃作坎离会。<div target='_blank'>闻仲嘉叔问继以职事行县道游茶山及诸胜境作寄一首</a><span class='authorDate'>（1116年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, id='poem_sentence_3_527075'>阴崖气亦暖，瑞草先春敷<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：小杜诗茶称瑞草魁。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527075'>飞流吐明月，转壑千雷车。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527075'>大中乾元字，入木蛟鸾俱。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527075'>薰风想佳句，奇踪典刑馀。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527075'>林间伯劳飞，茶篚春事初。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527075'>尚有北枝秀，明空雪千株。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527075'>幽香发清夜，肝胆生冰壶。<div
