class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作亦）</span>禄隐，居然卧蜗庐。<div id='poem_sentence_22_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_527075'>画墁固无役，反<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>如著辕驹。<div id='poem_sentence_23_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_527075'>亦拟浮扁舟，乘春经五湖。<div id='poem_sentence_24_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_527075'>收帆白蘋下，令子见潜夫<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_25_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_527075'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_527075_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527075'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_527075_0'>⑴ 自注：方子通言，顷有好事人刻意仙术，闻施翁遗迹，故往访之。临归，但闻妙香不绝，云沉榆之香。事见《王子年拾遗记》。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_23_527075_0'>⑵ 原作及，据四库本改</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_25_527075_0'>⑶ 自注：二子数以书见招为扁舟之游，故有此句。老杜几回书札待潜夫。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527075_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>春，至吴兴，见江仲举、仲嘉兄弟。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
镇江（丹徒）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='a2bfd41ab721414ea98e56c8f03a140f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a2bfd41ab721414ea98e56c8f03a140f");'><span id='a2bfd41ab721414ea98e56c8f03a140f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>，47岁</div><div id='a2bfd41ab721414ea98e56c8f03a140f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年1月</a>　正月，葬母于镇江府丹徒县，叶梦得作墓志铭。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年7月11日</a>　表叔王涣之卒，七月十一日，祭奠之，作祭文，创作地点或在镇江府丹徒县。作品：《王八侍郎祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>王八侍郎祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（宣和六年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221807")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221807'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221807'>维宣和六年岁次甲辰七月丙子朔十一日丙戌，从表侄程某谨以茶果素馔清酌之奠，致祭于表叔宝文学士、太原郡侯之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221807_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221807_comment'></div>天有间气，是生公侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221807_comment'></div>刚柔愿栗，赋委异侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221807_comment'></div>公之所钟，和厚纯静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221807_comment'></div>大雅恢闳，德人之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221807_comment'></div>虽则和厚，不可疏亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221807_comment'></div>静而不固，既纯且明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221807_comment'></div>风度凝远，绝世垢尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221807_comment'></div>论议英发，出言成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221807_comment'></div>视此标鉴，神仙中人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221807_comment'></div>惟初未冠，发策帝庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221807_comment'></div>拔出人上，誉走四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221807_comment'></div>为郡文学，博士先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221807_comment'></div>齑盐八年，泊若无营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221807_comment'></div>栖迟三馆，出佐一州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221807_comment'></div>入未几时，遂侍前旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221807_comment'></div>譬彼瑰异，为世所求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221807_comment'></div>不疾而驰，顾岂我谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221807_comment'></div>蔼蔼其华，秩秩其音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221807_comment'></div>圣主所器，宰府所钦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221807_comment'></div>名位之来，走避不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221807_comment'></div>公在天朝，宝璐明珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221807_comment'></div>照十二乘，和鸾九衢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221807_comment'></div>亦犹灵囿，孔翠鸾鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221807_comment'></div>羽仪绚粲，光动草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221807_comment'></div>公治省曹，通达政体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221807_comment'></div>公司诰命，温厚纯美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221807_comment'></div>舆言所期，必相天子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221807_comment'></div>何以占之，惟德与器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221807_comment'></div>庶几前人，休养康济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221807_comment'></div>入则讽议，将美赞猷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221807_comment'></div>出把将符，坐啸轻裘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221807_comment'></div>聊以华国，亦以镇浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221807_comment'></div>窃尝有言，物有定价，人有品俦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221807_comment'></div>金玉之利，不如戈矛，驺麟之用，不如马牛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221807_comment'></div>较第等差，孰处其尤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221807_comment'></div>世有如公，实第一流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221807_comment'></div>某也不肖，顽顿朱愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221807_comment'></div>始以童子，拜公南徐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221807_comment'></div>及官太湖，公镇龙舒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221807_comment'></div>顾睐叹惜，刻画吹嘘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221807_comment'></div>借重培塿，比之衡庐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221807_comment'></div>肝肺开示，底蕴无馀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221807_comment'></div>华首游倦，愿言卜居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221807_comment'></div>庶几亲仁，环堵是图。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221807_comment'></div>公闻此言，载色载愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221807_comment'></div>辱置怀抱，期通有无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221807_comment'></div>孤穷不孝，寻遭祸罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221807_comment'></div>葬亲五州，居计益决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221807_comment'></div>承颜接词，一日三月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221807_comment'></div>如何不憖，不至耄耋？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221807_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221807_comment'></div>吾乡多士，继出更奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221807_comment'></div>公一辈人，凋丧遂尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221807_comment'></div>公沙五龙，松折山殒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221807_comment'></div>风流酝藉，无复耆隽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221807_comment'></div>昔者曾子，身被齐衰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221807_comment'></div>子张氏没，往哭之哀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221807_comment'></div>贤哲是痛，吊也欤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221807_comment'></div>惟俱不天，怙恃永已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221807_comment'></div>得见父执，如痿暂起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221807_comment'></div>于父执中，厚莫公比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221807_comment'></div>从容话言，历历在耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221807_comment'></div>如何一朝，于此已矣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221807_comment'></div>荒摧之言，颠沛丛委。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1221807_comment'></div>登堂一恸，有泪如洗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1221807_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1221807_comment'></div>尚飨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_68_1221807_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1124&endYear=1124')">1124年</a>　叶梦得居卞山，秋游西余山有诗，程俱和之，创作地点或在镇江府丹徒县。作品：《次韵叶内翰游西余山用袁奉议韵》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷四。）</span><div id='poem_527033' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527033' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527033?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵叶内翰游西余山用袁奉议韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（甲辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527033")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527033_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527033'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527033'>平子愧明略，长卿真倦游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527033'>笭箵傥可佩，瑶玉岂复舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527033'>旧闻西余老，猖狂白蘋洲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527033'>毫端宝刹见，尘起大地收。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527033'>奋迅师子王，蚓蛙视蛟虬。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527033'>向来大涤翁，晚节万户侯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527033'>襄阳一转语，富贵真云浮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527033'>此道久已微，珷玞混琳球。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527033'>念昔过苕霅，寻溪亦经丘。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527033'>同游今安在，十载一瞬眸<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：尝与江仲嘉至西余。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527033'>几欲挂长剑，刻舟笑延州。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527033'>焉知瓮中人，寂默无春秋。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527033'>香炉着古庙，一念万劫休。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527033'>安得五亩园，良苗接平畴。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_527033'>脱身饥寒外，结友<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>高胜流。<div id='poem_sentence_14_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_527033'>二边无馀习，六贼可尽刘。<div id='poem_sentence_15_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_527033'>谁能使危肠，一日一万周。<div id='poem_sentence_16_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_527033'>须公谢三旌，故事追羊求。<div id='poem_sentence_17_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_527033'>青鞋一幅巾，往来山之幽。<div id='poem_sentence_18_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_527033'>且复载明月，深潭戏垂钩。<div id='poem_sentence_19_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_527033'></div><div id='poem_sentence_20_527033_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527033'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_14_527033_0'>⑴ 原作及，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527033_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='2e63bd46ba51427186959e4a97ad3d76_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2e63bd46ba51427186959e4a97ad3d76");'><span id='2e63bd46ba51427186959e4a97ad3d76_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1128')">1126-1128年</a>，49-51岁</div><div id='2e63bd46ba51427186959e4a97ad3d76' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　被斥为蔡攸党人，罢官，寓居镇江。有书信问候蔡攸，但应作于此前，具体时间不明，姑系于此。作品：《蔡少师问候》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_1221634' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221634' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221634?labeling=true' target='_blank'>蔡少师问候启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1126年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221634")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221634_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221634'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221634'>日者某官抗节抚边，祖车戒道，获走违于郊舍，徒群簉于宾阶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221634_comment'></div>瞻行色以增怀，曾立谈之弗及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221634_comment'></div>顾难将母，莫敢请从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221634_comment'></div>矧才略不足以赞咨诹，筋力不足以先士伍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221634_comment'></div>空承素眷，何异众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221634_comment'></div>违德以来，驰诚滋剧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221634_comment'></div>近请见令似，审比收家问，已次赵州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221634_comment'></div>仰惟绥御之馀，懋膺神物之相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221634_comment'></div>少保相公九官称首，一德承君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221634_comment'></div>美常武于徐方，召公是似；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221634_comment'></div>授恩言于帝所，相度来宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221634_comment'></div>谅坚体国之忠，益广周询之实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221634_comment'></div>不测不克，以修我戎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221634_comment'></div>嘉谋嘉猷，入告乃后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221634_comment'></div>上以安社稷，下以庇生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221634_comment'></div>永为黔首之依，以尽赤心之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221634_comment'></div>是则子孙奕世，将庆泽以无穷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221634_comment'></div>岂止功德兼隆，与皇基而同固矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221634_comment'></div>伏见五月晦日御笔，颇勤旰食，切责宪臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221634_comment'></div>盖闻德博之郊，似有潢池之聚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221634_comment'></div>虽鼠窃狗盗，随即诛夷；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221634_comment'></div>然鸟与兽穷，或能啄搏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221634_comment'></div>愿循其本，益戒弗虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221634_comment'></div>当令无外之春台，欢谣击壤；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221634_comment'></div>肯使好生之赤子，流血成川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221634_comment'></div>某昨在江湖，每窥诏札，观丁宁于睿旨，深恻怛于斯民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221634_comment'></div>固知尧舜之仁，盖出生成之性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221634_comment'></div>父老或至于感泣，神祇因是以介休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221634_comment'></div>仰宽北顾之忧，实赖中权之重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221634_comment'></div>惟时溽暑，愿体眷怀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221634_comment'></div>计多吐握之劳，无爽应酬之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221634_comment'></div>少保相公弼谐侍极，德望冠朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221634_comment'></div>英才皆入于彀中，风采想闻于天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221634_comment'></div>窃料远方之吏属，皆思自达于门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221634_comment'></div>凤凰高翔，争先睹之为快；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221634_comment'></div>江海善下，固不辞于细流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221634_comment'></div>岂惟阴察隽异之材，抑以博询攻守之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221634_comment'></div>固无损于威重，但益隆于具瞻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221634_comment'></div>当复隐如长城，还师衽席之上；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221634_comment'></div>固已沛若时雨，折冲尊俎之间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221634_comment'></div>阐声教于遐陬，同华夷于寿域。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221634_comment'></div>即趋严节，遂秉鸿钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221634_comment'></div>益殚素业之施，大慰苍生之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221634_comment'></div>顾兹孤蹇，永托帡幪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1221634_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1126&endYear=1126')">1126年</a>　此年前后，自编文集若干卷，欲托叶梦得为序，不果。时寓居镇江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年5月</a>　五月，转朝请郎，时寓居镇江。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　寓居镇江，有书寄李纲丞相议事。程俱所论有六：行在、百司与供奉等物要当简易；朝廷应事先筹划，防备金人南攻；泗州等地虽为控扼之地，然淮河南岸也不可忽视；应选侍讲、侍读；虽在艰难草创之时，朝廷纪纲不可不振；慎选诸路帅臣。时寓居镇江。作品：《寄李丞相劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十六。）</span><div id='poem_1221601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄李丞相劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1127年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221601")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221601'>某罪废之馀，驽懦狂瞽，近者不胜惓惓圳亩之诚，敢以蠡管之见，仰裨听采之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221601_comment'></div>伏蒙答以教字，下情感戢，不知所云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221601_comment'></div>藿食馀生，隐忧多虑，忘其浅鄙，继欲有陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221601_comment'></div>顾自屏丘园，誓无闻达之念，不敢上书阙下，怀不能已，用渎钧听，庶几少助启沃之际，馀议所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221601_comment'></div>僭冒皇恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221601_comment'></div>谨条具如左：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1221601'>一、窃闻车驾尚且驻跸梁宋，此得计也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221601_comment'></div>不唯变故之后，以系西北之心，兼奏报往来，指踪制画，不至辽远，或失事机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221601_comment'></div>昔者黄帝居无常处，以兵车为卫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221601_comment'></div>今虽与古不同，然亦经纶草昧，圣人焦劳勤俭、不遑宁处之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221601_comment'></div>若驻跸梁宋，以据天下之冲，缮治建康，以为时巡之所，备御有素，顺动以时，亦一时之策也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221601_comment'></div>然行在百司与供奉等物要当简易，稍略繁文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221601_comment'></div>多备车乘，以当营卫，其馀冗从，或俾舟行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221601_comment'></div>权时之宜，窃以为便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_1221601'>一、窃有愚虑，妄意万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221601_comment'></div>自来虏人入寇，率是因我之粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221601_comment'></div>两年以来，皆自河北、河东而来，劫掠残破，谅已无馀，千里萧条，必无供亿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221601_comment'></div>兼彼既图割据，则于此两路理必少宽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221601_comment'></div>窃虑今秋万一南牧，却恐或自山东以趋内地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221601_comment'></div>不唯前此未到城邑聚落可以剽攘，兼亦冲我衿喉，出于不意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221601_comment'></div>某虽不晓山东道路，但去冬传闻虏人辎重有自单州去者，又闻向日山东群盗有海州招安者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221601_comment'></div>若金人以一军自单州出来，直捣南京，一军自海州出来，或自徐趋泗，截断淮楚，则为患益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221601_comment'></div>更乞朝廷先事防虑，控扼之地，密为经画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1221601'>一、窃闻泗州建府，实为控扼之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221601_comment'></div>然泗州城在淮北，切恐淮之南岸不可无城，以置仓场库务、军营官府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221601_comment'></div>所有北城，谅须亦有措置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221601_comment'></div>况今已是深夏，不日秋凉，愿惜分阴，如救焚溺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1221601'>一、伏以新天子聪明圣武，出于天纵，然古所谓「念终始典于学」与夫「监于先王成宪」者，固不可略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221601_comment'></div>高宗所以为商中兴王者，用是道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221601_comment'></div>使大学之道成于胸中，则其于听言应物、出入起居、发号施令，岂不恢恢然有馀地而唯理之从哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221601_comment'></div>此古之贤佐所以未尝不以学为言者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221601_comment'></div>愿选端亮敦厚、通知古今大体之人，专以侍讲读为职，使之日侍天子左右，以备顾问，不必俟开经筵也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221601_comment'></div>要令出入禁闼，常在上前，如汉侍中尚书郎之比，清间之宴，为圣主陈说治道与古之正心诚意、修身爱物，任贤御事之宜，古今成败之事，亦所以资缉熙光明之万一，非小补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221601_comment'></div>况上方焦劳，念国步之艰难，怀二圣之北狩，天下之大，不足解忧，谅无燕豫便嬖之娱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221601_comment'></div>傥使儒生日奉简编于前，讲论古今，不唯仰裨海岳，亦足少宽圣怀，以度永日，岂不贤于馀事哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221601_comment'></div>若夫使沾沾自喜，截截谝言，倾险浅躁、利口嗜进之人为之，又不若无之为愈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221601_comment'></div>此盖当今急务之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1221601'>一、古者虽在艰难草创之时，纪纲亦不可不振，献替尤不可不闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221601_comment'></div>盖一事失宜，不比平时，立能致患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221601_comment'></div>肃宗方在凤翔，李勉为御史大夫，老将乘马阙门，弹劾不置。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221601_comment'></div>德宗虽在奉天，欲以试衔官与人，陆贽论列再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221601_comment'></div>今者行在台谏之官，谅须得人，端厚诚实，维持至公，通达国体，足以开广聪明、献替可否，则朝廷黜陟之间，政事弛张之际，莫不适于事理，当于人心矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221601_comment'></div>夫日亲讲读，以资圣学，妙选台谏，以正朝廷，此事之本源也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221601_comment'></div>岂有源清而流浊，表正而景邪者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221601_comment'></div>则天下无不立之事矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221601_comment'></div>狂瞽，仰幸采择。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_45_1221601'>一、方今宰执、侍从固是安危所系，休戚实同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221601_comment'></div>然诸路帅臣比之平时尤当慎选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221601_comment'></div>若诸路抚绥无事，不唯屏卫王家，抑亦兵食所出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221601_comment'></div>兼不贻朝廷之忧，得以一意并力，备御燮和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221601_comment'></div>如其不然，小有蠢动，兵旅既难抽发，馈饷或致阙供，扰溃之虞，不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221601_comment'></div>且以迩日浙西利害观之可见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221601_comment'></div>二浙自经方贼陆梁，人往往喜乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221601_comment'></div>倪贼比作，一路振骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221601_comment'></div>赖安抚司绥驭措画有方，卒以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221601_comment'></div>盖贼徒初欲出而肆掠，径捣钱塘，则官兵已集；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221601_comment'></div>欲胁诱乡氓以广徒众，则保伍素严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221601_comment'></div>是以数月之间，不离巢穴，卒以穷迫，乞就招安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221601_comment'></div>何方贼于承平之时，旬月之内，能致数十万人，掉臂横行，围陷州府；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221601_comment'></div>而倪贼当艰危之际，以勤王之馀，半年之久，不能近一严州者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221601_comment'></div>此帅臣得人与否之异也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221601_comment'></div>然则诸路帅臣不当轻付，盖利害如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221601_comment'></div>惟朝廷加意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221601_comment'></div>僭越死罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_62_1221601_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1127&endYear=1127')">1127年</a>　寓居镇江，得小圃城南，有诗。作品：《得小圃城南，用渊明归田园居韵六首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_527088' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527088' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527088?labeling=true' target='_blank'>得小圃城南用渊明归田园居韵六首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丁未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527088")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527088_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527088'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527088'>城南美林壑，城上皆青山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527088'>山光照庭户，于此可尽年。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527088'>穰穰千古区，化作鱼蒲渊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527088'>秋蕖渺无际，红鲜间田田。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527088'>邂逅得小隐，连山在其前。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527088'>流泉带其左，松篁接风烟。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527088'>它年营把茅，不待雪满颠。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527088'>宁图五鼎食，坐失十载闲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527088'>愿比小人腹，一餐期果然。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527088_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527088'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_527088_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527089' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527089' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527089?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丁未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527089'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527089'>说难死韩非，法蔽叹商鞅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527089'>当时轩冕计，肯作刀锯想。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527089'>辰来阴影集，事过流电往。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527089'>胡为意无穷，机械日争长。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527089'>俗中多局促，正觉斯道广。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527089'>斯道不可迷，荒涂辟榛莽。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527089_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527089'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_527089_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527090' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527090' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527090?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丁未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527090_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527090'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527090'>年大百无味，区中故人稀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527090'>京江一都会，卜筑行当归。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527090'>傥回故人车，云关访荷衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527090'>时来吐情话，未觉世相违。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527090_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527090'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527090_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527091' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527091' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527091?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丁未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527091_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527091'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527091'>馀生甚穷独，四海谁与娱。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527091'>故乡道脩阻，宛在太末墟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527091'>向来亲仁意，正拟城南居。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527091'>乌衣丈人行，玉树珊瑚株。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527091'>所冀邻里间，徜徉从所如。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527091'>如何漳滨卧，使我恨有馀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527091'>会当悟杯蛇，灵府静以虚。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527091'>且复陪杖屦，敢言通有无。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527091_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527091'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527091_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527092' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527092' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527092?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丁未）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527092_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527092'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527092'>缅怀斜川人，胜日追邻曲。<div class='authorDate'>（戊申）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527458")'>程俱</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_1_527458_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527458'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527458_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527459' class='authorDate'>（戊申）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527459_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527459'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527459'>一壑回环十二峰，茅茨送老白云封。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527459'>如今尘里看图画，却愧当年邴曼容。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527459_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527459'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527459_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年8月11日</a>　寓居镇江，八月十一日，复除著作佐郎。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1128&endYear=1128')">1128年</a>　寓居镇江，两次上书乞罢著作佐郎，不准。时间当在是年八月十一日至十月二十三日之间。作品：《乞罢著作佐郎恩命申尚书省状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221586' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221586' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221586?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞罢著作佐郎恩命申尚书省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1128年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221586")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221586_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221586'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221586'>右，某今月十五日准尚书省劄子节文，八月十一日，三省同奉圣旨，除某著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221586_comment'></div>某疏远小官，罪戾之馀，久伏农圃，涵泳皇泽，期毕此生，敢图圣朝弃瑕录用，非某糜陨所能报塞，固当竭蹶奔命，以效犬马之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221586_comment'></div>然伏自惟念，某愚钝迂惷，一无所长，忧愤以来，心志耗落，穷独贫病，因以早衰，收置朝廷，何所裨益？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221586_comment'></div>而况著作品秩虽卑，实古太史氏之职，所修日历言动兼载，细大毕书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221586_comment'></div>是以选择必精，职任亦重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221586_comment'></div>又况某昔年备员东观，更历岁月，纂次无几，尸旷已多，岂容冒荣，更尘史属？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221586_comment'></div>方圣主焦劳侧席，懋建中兴之业，群能著职，总核名实之时，而某以疵谬之迹，无用之才，加以衰瘁，玷兹盛选，义不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221586_comment'></div>所有新除著作佐郎恩命，伏望钧慈察其恳诚，特行敷奏，许赐寝罢，除某一宫观差遣，以安愚分。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1221586_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='f171f33126dd4812be4cf6a888c2ecf6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("f171f33126dd4812be4cf6a888c2ecf6");'><span id='f171f33126dd4812be4cf6a888c2ecf6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，52岁</div><div id='f171f33126dd4812be4cf6a888c2ecf6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月4日</a>　二月四日，随车驾渡江南下，至镇江，时任礼部员外郎。<br /></div>
-----end

商丘（宋城）

class='authorDate'>（宣和七年八月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221743")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>四言诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_1221743_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221743'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221743'>大道之行，人无斁怀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_1221743'>泊焉相忘，莫往莫来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1221743'>逮德下衰，亲誉畏侮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1221743'>迩之不能，繄远是务。<div id='poem_sentence_3_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_1221743'>招徕不足，求以兵旅。<div id='poem_sentence_4_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1221743'>有服斯叛，无得何亡。<div id='poem_sentence_5_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1221743'>我观此图，掩卷慨慷。<div id='poem_sentence_6_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1221743'></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1221743_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221743'><span class='label'>按：</span>宣和乙巳八月，舟行道睢阳，赵叔问携此图过河亭共阅，为题此赞。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221743_comment'></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
丹阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ef6b62e533c34bef9804c6c598e5d4bf_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ef6b62e533c34bef9804c6c598e5d4bf");'><span id='ef6b62e533c34bef9804c6c598e5d4bf_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，52岁</div><div id='ef6b62e533c34bef9804c6c598e5d4bf' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年2月4日</a>　二月四日中午，离镇江，夜宿吕城，时任礼部员外郎。有诗。作品：《己酉二月二日车驾渡杨子江四日匆遽离镇江余与妻孥徒步趼足饥走至吕城道中口占》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527457' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527457' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527457?labeling=true' target='_blank'>己酉二月二日车驾渡扬子江四日匆遽离镇江余与妻孥徒步趼足饥走至吕城道中口占</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年2月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527457")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527457_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527457'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527457'>白日无光捲地风，扶携趼足去匆匆。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527457'>安知白首干戈里，身寄淮南老小中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527457_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527457'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527457_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
嘉兴（嘉兴府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0ebed5d08a56439fa544745f31d745ce_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0ebed5d08a56439fa544745f31d745ce");'><span id='0ebed5d08a56439fa544745f31d745ce_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，52岁</div><div id='0ebed5d08a56439fa544745f31d745ce' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月15日</a>　在秀州知州任上，四月十五日到任，上表谢恩。作品：《秀州谢上表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。秀州州治即南宋嘉兴府府治。）</span><div id='poem_1221533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀州谢上表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221533")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221533'>臣某言：臣昨任礼部郎官，自三月初即以病告卧家，乞外任或宫庙差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221533_comment'></div>间蒙除太常少卿，臣三具状申都省，辞不就职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221533_comment'></div>寻准敕，除臣直秘阁、权发遣秀州军州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221533_comment'></div>臣已于今月十五日到任上讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221533_comment'></div>初布条纲，具宣德意，所忧绵薄，莫副使令。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221533_comment'></div>臣<span class='inlineComment2'>（中谢。）</span>伏念臣幼而奇孤，长益顽钝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221533_comment'></div>上书论事，空怀忧国之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221533_comment'></div>窃禄代耕，每尽守官之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221533_comment'></div>挂名邪籍，为世僇人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221533_comment'></div>晚陪英俊之躔，浸冒典章之选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221533_comment'></div>再游东观，愧刘郎之复来；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221533_comment'></div>三至南宫，知冯公之已老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221533_comment'></div>遭时之变，振古未闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221533_comment'></div>穷独馀生，忧愤不死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221533_comment'></div>卧家请急，投劾丐归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221533_comment'></div>敢于臲𡰈不安之时，而当绵蕞草创之事，既遂颛愚之守，复瞻天日之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221533_comment'></div>喜不自胜，死无所恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221533_comment'></div>顾惟敝邑，实介大邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221533_comment'></div>征赋之入有经，而不时之须沓至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221533_comment'></div>盗贼之忧方炽，而即戎之备未修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221533_comment'></div>念偾骄凋敝之馀，则莫若利其衔勒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221533_comment'></div>而匮竭疮痍之后，又当事于抚摩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221533_comment'></div>靖言以思，宁免于咎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221533_comment'></div>收此桑榆之景，终繄覆载之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221533_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尝胆济时，厉精图治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221533_comment'></div>辟至公之路，方因任于群材；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221533_comment'></div>念无竞维人，故兼收于片善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221533_comment'></div>致兹疵贱，亦不弃遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221533_comment'></div>臣敢不行其所知，施于有政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221533_comment'></div>使公绰为赵魏之老，于用或优；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221533_comment'></div>而阳城躬抚字之劳，自知甚拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221533_comment'></div>唯当竭力，少谢素餐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221533_comment'></div>臣无任瞻天望圣激切屏营之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221533_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1221533_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在秀州知州任上，举荐陈沔。作品：《乞差陈沔充将领》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。陈沔，事迹不详。）</span><div id='poem_1221603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞差陈沔充将领劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221603")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221603'>契勘前知本州叶焕在任日奏乞武翼郎宋恩充本州准备将领，统领四县弓手一千三百馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221603_comment'></div>今来宋恩就差充东南第四将，其秀州准备将领，不可阙官训练统辖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221603_comment'></div>伏见忠训郎陈沔在宣和间系处州剑川县监当，时方贼作过，连陷婺、睦、衢、处等州，至诸县皆被残破，而沔独率县人捍御剑川，相持累月，贼不能入，不唯保全一县仓库生灵，而又障蔽福建之冲，使无侵轶之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221603_comment'></div>某不识其人，然稔闻其事，观其已试，可见其才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221603_comment'></div>某今欲乞特差陈沔充本州准备将领，填宋恩阙，庶几缓急可以倚仗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221603_comment'></div>奉圣旨依。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1221603_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月22日</a>　在秀州知州任上。四月二十二日，车驾临幸秀州，有旨赐对，奏事。作品：《四月二十二日车驾经由秀州赐对劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十六。）</span>《乞免秀州和买绢奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221546' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221546' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221546?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四月二十二日车驾经由秀州赐对劄子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221546")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221546_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221546'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221546'>臣伏见陛下复正天位，适以正阳之朔，天日明霁，气候协时，此天眷有宋而保祐陛下之符验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221546_comment'></div>御殿之初，搢绅士大夫往往感涕，诏音始下，皆欣然若更生，此又助有宋而归戴陛下之明證也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221546_comment'></div>岂非方今国势不振，宗社岋岋，安危之任在陛下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221546_comment'></div>永膺天禄，盛德日新，政事日举，赏罚施置，皆仰有以当天意，俯有以合人心，则赵氏安而社稷固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221546_comment'></div>苟惟反是，则天之所以眷佑者将恐替，人之所以欣戴者将恐离，如是则社稷危而天下乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221546_comment'></div>其间盖不容发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221546_comment'></div>方靖康京城之陷，大宗正属狼狈北徙，无遗族焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221546_comment'></div>国朝故事，亲王未有得预外廷、当事任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221546_comment'></div>而陛下乃适以亲王总兵河外，于是神器有归，宗祀绝而复续。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221546_comment'></div>日者事变之起，陛下退处别宫，不阅月而复正天位，此天所祐，非人之所能为者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221546_comment'></div>古称大福不再，而天祐陛下者再，此天下之庆，而陛下所当戒惧之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221546_comment'></div>戒惧则如之何？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221546_comment'></div>政事举措，刑罚施置，使足以当天意、合人心而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221546_comment'></div>古之人君承衰乱之世，能济大难以致中兴者，率由是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221546_comment'></div>《诗》曰：「戒之戒之，天维显思，命不易哉」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221546_comment'></div>故臣敢以是为陛下反正之初之献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221546_comment'></div>狂愚，惟陛下留听。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221546_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221553' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221553' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221553?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞免秀州和买绢奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月22日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221553")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221553_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221553'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221553'>臣迩者伏遇圣驾巡幸，道由本郡，臣以守臣，蒙恩赐对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221553_comment'></div>亲奉玉音，以谓守臣六职，当以恤民为务，所以固邦本而宁国家者，训饬甚备，令臣访察疾苦，咸以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221553_comment'></div>此以见陛下爱民泽物至诚之心出于天纵，实社稷之福，天下之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221553_comment'></div>臣时到郡曾未浃日，退即访问耆老，以谓秀州近年和买䌷绢最为民害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221553_comment'></div>盖祖宗以来，以秀州不产桑蚕，故虽夏税䌷绢，尚止令上户送纳本色，第三等以下人户皆折钱入官，转运司却于出产丝蚕处置场收买，以足岁额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221553_comment'></div>岂闻税绢之外，更加和买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221553_comment'></div>盖以苏、秀州出米至多，逐年和籴既已甲于他郡，而杭、湖等州属县多以桑蚕为业，故和买䌷绢比他郡为多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221553_comment'></div>自靖康元年，献议大臣不知祖宗朝立法之旨与夫诸州土产之宜，但见杭、湖等州和买绢数颇多，而苏、秀不及，因以为不均，于是分拨八万匹与平江府，而秀州管认四万匹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221553_comment'></div>自是秀州之民于常税之馀，和籴之外，又加此一项和买䌷绢，于是民力益困，为害浸深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221553_comment'></div>后来于建炎三年十一月中，因转运司状，以平江、秀州不产蚕桑，减秀州和买为二万疋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221553_comment'></div>然终是创添此项，责以所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221553_comment'></div>输纳之时，远于他州贵价收买，而官给价直不过八百，贫弱下户未必得钱，横被诛求，急于常赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221553_comment'></div>秀民疾苦，莫此为大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221553_comment'></div>伏望圣慈深赐详察，特赐蠲免和买䌷绢，则一州之民受惠不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221553_comment'></div>臣谨检坐皇祐五年许下户折纳税绢指挥节文如后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221553_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1221553'>皇祐五年七月十二日，州准转运司牒，准三司户部牒，准中书批状指挥节文，两浙转运司奏：「体访得苏、秀两州乡村自前例种水田，不栽桑柘，每年人户输纳夏税物帛为无所产，多被行贩之人预于起纳日前，先往出产处杭、湖州乡庄贱价㩆揽百姓合纳税物，抬价货卖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221553_comment'></div>人户要趁限了纳，费耗甚多，官中又不纳得堪好物帛，亏损官私，颇为不便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221553_comment'></div>当司昨于皇祐元年内，曾体问得苏、秀州不产蚕丝，人户送纳夏税䌷绢不便事理，遂擘画，牒苏、秀州除第一等、第二等人户各依常年例送纳本色外，所是第三等已下百姓户内税物，即告示取便折纳见钱，遂便敷与出产杭、湖、睦州，差官置场，依市价买得上等堪好匹帛，数目充备，起发上京送纳，即无遗阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221553_comment'></div>彼时官司极获济办。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221553_comment'></div>至皇祐二年，准三司户部牒，请依旧例施行，不得更令人户折纳见钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221553_comment'></div>当司看详逐州不产蚕丝，难得䌷绢送纳，不免依前于贩易人边高价买纳，下户转成困弊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221553_comment'></div>又值叠年灾伤，人民转更不易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221553_comment'></div>今本司已认定逐年苏、秀州合上供匹帛，管在不亏失元额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221553_comment'></div>只乞许令本司将纳到见钱于出产杭、越、湖、睦州收买」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221553_comment'></div>奉圣旨送三司，依所奏施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1221553_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年4月</a>　在秀州知州任上。四月，访陆贽像，图之资圣佛寺，作赞。作品：《陆宣公祠堂赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十六。唐相陆宣公贽，嘉兴人。）</span><div id='poem_1221748' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221748' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221748?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆宣公祠堂赞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221748")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221748_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221748'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221748'>唐相陆宣公贽，嘉兴人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221748_comment'></div>建炎三年夏四月，信安程俱假守秀州，始访公之像，图之资圣佛寺，率僚吏祠而拜之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221748_comment'></div>谨为之赞曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_1221748'>天下无事，湛于宴安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221748_comment'></div>视此神器，隐如太山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221748_comment'></div>是以其臣，唯得是嗜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221748_comment'></div>以谀为恭，以憸为智。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221748_comment'></div>世方纷乱，上下岌岌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221748_comment'></div>忍于其间，觊得患失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221748_comment'></div>伟哉宣公，兴元之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221748_comment'></div>夷崄一致，为君矢谟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221748_comment'></div>如彼大厦，载支载扶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221748_comment'></div>如彼赤子，以调以虞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221748_comment'></div>格君之非，砭国之肓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221748_comment'></div>卒以一旅，还之异方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221748_comment'></div>西平之功，宣公之画。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221748_comment'></div>外戡内筹，心膂惟一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221748_comment'></div>槜李之郊，吴越所虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221748_comment'></div>公生其间，种蠡汗颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221748_comment'></div>顾视故国，乔木苍然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221748_comment'></div>岂无若人，奠九㙻兮！</div><div id='poem_sentence_19_1221748_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在秀州知州任上。叶梦得、郑作肃来秀州拜访。叶梦得与程俱吾约定后死者为先死者作墓志铭之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年5月</a>　在秀州知州任上。五月，上表贺宋高宗生辰。作品：《秀州贺天申节表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_1221534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221534?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀州贺天申节表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221534")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221534_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221534'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221534'>臣某言：诞弥厥月，允昭申命之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221534_comment'></div>长发其祥，共献后天之祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221534_comment'></div>由中及外，式舞且歌<span class='inlineComment2'>（中贺。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221534_comment'></div>恭惟皇帝陛下拨乱挺生，膺期绍绪，体周行之乾健，廓继照之离明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221534_comment'></div>帝命弗违，缵二百年之基业；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221534_comment'></div>民心攸戴，过八千岁之春秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221534_comment'></div>丕承赤伏之符，适应朱明之候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221534_comment'></div>中兴有望，率土惟均。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221534_comment'></div>臣属守偏州，远违行阙，《天保》之诗《小雅》，方期如日之升；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221534_comment'></div>华封之祝圣人，徒有望云之阻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221534_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1221534_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年5月</a>　在秀州知州任上。五月，上书乞留邓根通判秀州。作品：《乞留邓根通判秀州》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221605' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221605' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221605?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞留邓根通判秀州状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年5月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221605")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221605_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221605'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221605'>窃见报状，都省劄子备坐六月十六日圣旨指挥，秀州通判朱原系先差下待阙人，邓根系明受元年三月十四日差，合行改正，令朱原赴任，邓根别与差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221605_comment'></div>某辄有诚恳，上干朝廷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221605_comment'></div>契勘本州通判邓根先任崇德县令，方陈通之变，亲部弓手，召募射生等人，至杭州城下，追奔获级，及措置把隘，堑掘来路，以制奔冲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221605_comment'></div>后来本县土军结集为乱，根率所领人兵夜半掩击，手杀数人，众乃争奋，贼以殄平，扼杭贼奔突之冲，弭一县涂炭之祸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221605_comment'></div>故吏部刘侍郎珏采于公论，应诏荐根，初不相识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221605_comment'></div>及召至行在，适在三月，崇德之政，人人知之，故庙堂除根通判秀州，以从公论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221605_comment'></div>今秀经去年残破之后，军兵阙少，廪藏空竭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221605_comment'></div>又防秋不远，训练新旧弓手，措置城池，除治器甲，某虽竭力尽心，以图微效，当得强佐相与维持，庶无败事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221605_comment'></div>今朱原尝历寺监，朝廷选用之人，必亦甚有才力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221605_comment'></div>但根已试之效，州人备知，缓急易以率众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221605_comment'></div>又尝经战斗，奋不顾身，取胜擒奸，根亦自信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221605_comment'></div>某观其人既不避事畏缩，又不悦众市恩，似肯向前协力图济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221605_comment'></div>若令因任，遇事应猝，功必倍差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221605_comment'></div>伏望钧慈留根终任，如原才能扬历，何所不堪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221605_comment'></div>某素不识根，同官才踰月，本无情好，何苦为根游说，以罔朝廷？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221605_comment'></div>但为凋瘵之郡，相次防秋，措画经营，理须强佐，不独在某有助，实欲赖其已试，共保一州，少分忧寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221605_comment'></div>真切之情，仰幸省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221605_comment'></div>僭易陈叩，伏深皇恐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221605_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1221605'>根上舍出身，乃有材武，已试之效，秀人所安，乞赐钧察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221605_comment'></div>某窃以方今州郡全藉僚吏协力向前，庶于艰危之时可望全济。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221605_comment'></div>故某昨因赐对，乞差保守剑川使臣陈沔充准备将领，已蒙朝廷矜允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221605_comment'></div>某不识其人，亦无关节，但欲得实材，以备缓急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221605_comment'></div>今者僭易，复从朝廷乞一邓根且留在任，盖非私请，伏乞矜察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221605_comment'></div>如朱原指挥不可复回，或依平江添差一员，候春暖无事日罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221605_comment'></div>更取钧裁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1221605_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在秀州知州任上。六、七月间，上书论辟官防秋事。作品：《辟官奏状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span>《申呈两府劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span>《申御营业使司乞先次勒停使臣宋卸状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span>《修城乞度牒》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221554?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辟官奏状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221554")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221554_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221554'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221554'>臣昨蒙恩差权发遣秀州军州事，即具申陈，去年秀州军兵作过，抚定之初，系差叶焕知本州事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221554_comment'></div>缘残破州郡，本官节次申请辟官等事，皆蒙朝廷施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221554_comment'></div>今本州事务繁重，又甚昔时，欲乞许候到任，检具叶焕已得指挥，申请施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221554_comment'></div>寻准建炎三年四月四日都省劄子，依所乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221554_comment'></div>今检会建炎二年九月日准尚书省劄子节文，叶焕劄子：「乞将本州见阙巡尉、添差尉，应帅司未曾奏差去处，许臣奏差一次，仍先次赴任」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221554_comment'></div>九月二日，三省同奉圣旨，依所乞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221554_comment'></div>臣契勘本州海盐县澉浦巡检袁序在任过满，蒙差到敦武郎苏敏中承替。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221554_comment'></div>其苏敏中昏耄，行步艰难，眼目不明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221554_comment'></div>见准提刑司牒，体量其澉浦是海口把隘紧要去处，委是难以放令在任。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221554_comment'></div>窃见忠翊郎毛磻孺颇有心力，乞差充澉浦巡检。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221554_comment'></div>又华亭县尉见阙，未曾差人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221554_comment'></div>窃见迪功郎、新宣州旌德县尉石茂良虽是书生，尝游西北，亦有心力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221554_comment'></div>乞差充华亭县尉，并填见阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221554_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨与差，所贵防秋之时不致阙事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1221554_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221554'><span class='label'>按：</span>奉圣旨依。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221554_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1221606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申呈两府劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221606")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221606'>本州近依朝旨，于见管禁军内抽差一半计七十三人前去镇江府防秋把隘，仍那融搜刷器甲，应副前去，各支盘缠、犒设，借请家粮外，又发一季钱米，往镇江府交纳讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221606_comment'></div>至今月五日，忽准浙西安抚都总管司牒，拣退四十三人，就令军员张雅管押归州，仍指挥别拣禁军四十三人，令本州都监王本管押前去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221606_comment'></div>仍各要黑皮笠子、衲袄、衣甲、弓弩、箭镞、鎗刀等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221606_comment'></div>本州除已依应别行拣选上件人数发遣，所有器甲并系今年三月内韩太尉勤王尽数般取前去，昨来已是那融搜刷器甲前去一番，今来若又要四十三副，如黑皮笠子等，实无从出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221606_comment'></div>所有衲袄见制造，朝廷抛降二千领尚未了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221606_comment'></div>及本州都监二员，内一员赵子震久患瘦病，自五月内在假，至今只有一员王本部押干当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221606_comment'></div>近安抚司拣退四十三人，止令军员管押归州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221606_comment'></div>今来人数一般，窃意不须兵官管押。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221606_comment'></div>除已牒都监王本不须前去，仍开析回申安抚都总管司去讫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221606_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_1221606'>〔小贴子〕契勘所换人数壮怯事艺相去不远，徒又费一番盘缠、犒设、借请等，止是徒欲本州困于应副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221606_comment'></div>如军员既押兵士四十三人回州，岂有换去人数一般，却须兵官管押？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221606_comment'></div>盖缘安抚叶待制近作发运使日，因随行兵士借支口券数少，及巡幸事务所牒阁住逃走兵士倪荣等名粮等事，尝蒙怪责，其家子弟至今<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1221606_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申御营使司乞先次勒停使臣宋卸状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221607")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221607'>臣本州见今措置防秋事务，依准近降指挥，诱谕人户修筑城壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221607_comment'></div>某日逐带领州事，于城上签书决遣，仍令官属分头管干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221607_comment'></div>有本州指使承信郎宋卸，帖委本人往来检察人夫媮惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221607_comment'></div>其宋卸自承差使后，更不前来管干，因某巡行城上，点检不见，遣人追呼，至夜不伏前来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221607_comment'></div>至次日追到，傲慢不逊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221607_comment'></div>某缘见兴众役，理当弹压，兼防秋急切，若皆似此违犯指挥，不伏驱使，切恐缓急难以使人，某已枷送司理院勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221607_comment'></div>兼本人近管押随军米至镇江府，有欠米斛，方行取问，遂就令根勘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221607_comment'></div>寻已招承自盗情罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221607_comment'></div>除候结案依条施行外，谨具申御营使司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221607_comment'></div>伏乞钧慈特赐敷奏，乞先次勒停，庶几军兴之际，缓急使人不至违慢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221607_comment'></div>伏候钧旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1221607_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221607'><span class='label'>按：</span>奉圣旨，宋卸先次勒停。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221607_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1221609' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221609' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221609?labeling=true' target='_blank'>修城乞度牒状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221609")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221609_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221609'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221609'>本州帮筑州城，里壁并已周匝，并开广城濠狭处，增筑上城慢道，及增添楼橹三十座，并皆了毕，所用砖灰砌城里壁相次了当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221609_comment'></div>除依朝旨劝诱外，先具状申，乞朝廷支降度牒紫衣各五十道，支还砖灰等钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221609_comment'></div>虽蒙省劄行下转运司，至今文移往回取会，切恐猝无给降之期，它日别有兴作，人不信从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221609_comment'></div>欲望朝廷委官径行检视，所申有实，则乞即赐指挥给降上件所乞紫衣牒各五十道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221609_comment'></div>右牒具呈，取钧旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1221609_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年闰8月12日</a>　在秀州知州任上。闰八月，奉旨与闲慢州军两易，程俱乞与衢、处州对换一处。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年9月12日</a>　在秀州知州任上。九月十二日，依旨仍知秀州，上劄子。作品：《申宰执劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221610' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221610' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221610?labeling=true' target='_blank'>申宰执劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年9月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221610")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221610_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221610'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221610'>某今月十三日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，程某治郡，民颇安之，可依旧知秀州，更不对移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221610_comment'></div>某疏远小官，才能无取，仰蒙钧造，曲赐知察，非某糜殒，所能报塞，固当夙夜廑职，死而后已，不知其他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221610_comment'></div>然有悃诚，事关利害，不敢不陈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221610_comment'></div>窃以秀州若只如今日车驾驻跸平江府，江北无事，则虽疏拙不才有如某者，竭尽驽蹇以赴事功，自度未至旷瘝，上贻朝廷之忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221610_comment'></div>若江北少有边尘之警，则秀州乃是沿边州郡，如前日臣僚之言，所谓海道不测之虞者，以某绵薄与本州事力，诚不能当，不过率众婴城，以死偿节而已，于国事未有补也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221610_comment'></div>不然，朝廷临时方议易以强敏之臣，不唯州将于郡人无拊循之素，而仓猝之际，方易郡守，转使人心不安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221610_comment'></div>又使新除者以迫于仓猝，无以集事为词，被代者有侥倖避事之谤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221610_comment'></div>此某所谓事关利害者，非以小己之私而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221610_comment'></div>伏望钧慈特赐敷陈，将秀州便比临边控扼要处，于从容无事之时，择强敏勇略之人，付以郡事，庶几不至临时颠沛，以负委使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221610_comment'></div>伏乞检详闰八月十二日圣旨指挥，早赐陶铸一闲慢州军，誓当竭力，以报恩造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221610_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1221610'>〔小贴子〕某近具劄子陈恳，乞赐陶铸与衢、处州对换一处，所贵秀州临海控扼去处，早得强能守臣，备御不测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221610_comment'></div>伏望矜察。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1221610_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年10月5日</a>　在秀州知州任上。十月五日，再上劄子，论及当前御敌形势与全盘御敌策略。作品：《十月五日车驾经由上殿劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年11月21日</a>　在秀州知州任上。十一月二十一日，至陆宣公祠堂祭祀，有祭文。作品：《陆宣公祠堂祭文》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>陆宣公祠堂祭文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年11月21日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221810")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221810'>维建炎三年岁次己酉，十一月乙巳朔，二十一日乙丑，具位程某谨以清酌果肴之奠，恭荐于唐丞相陆宣公之祠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221810_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221810_comment'></div>在唐中微，再偾再起，至于德宗，四海疮痏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221810_comment'></div>休之养之，手抚摩之，犹恐不济；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221810_comment'></div>胡宁贼之，而割而赘，而浚而膏？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221810_comment'></div>腹心内离，手足外摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221810_comment'></div>蹠盭不治，上下无交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221810_comment'></div>一夫奋呼，鱼服以跳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221810_comment'></div>公丁此时，为国亲臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221810_comment'></div>乱之未生也，固已察齐公之将病；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221810_comment'></div>乱之既生也，则又起虢君于既昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221810_comment'></div>方其安危之机，间不容穟，仓皇莫振，忧辱孔炽，而其所陈，未尝从权谲而废仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221810_comment'></div>然直而不讦，刚而能济，据正而不迁，陈古而不泥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221810_comment'></div>至于料敌之情，揣事之隐，钩深中会，物莫能遁，允所谓足以谋王体而断国论者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221810_comment'></div>而其王佐之才之学，盖施之未之尽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221810_comment'></div>某也不佞，忝兹守符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221810_comment'></div>实公故乡，墟里既芜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221810_comment'></div>始揭公像，为此世模。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221810_comment'></div>英风凛然，过者必趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221810_comment'></div>仰高山其安放，岂斯世之可诬！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221810_comment'></div>盖事有旷百世而相感者，岂为公而欷歔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221810_comment'></div>尚飨！</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1221810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在秀州知州任上，回朱司业信。作品：《秀州回朱司业启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十一。）</span><div id='poem_1221635' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221635' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221635?labeling=true' target='_blank'>秀州回朱司业启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221635")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221635_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221635'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221635'>右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221635_comment'></div>某辞职奉常，丐归故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221635_comment'></div>偶承人乏，付以郡章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221635_comment'></div>莫分宵旰之忧，窃有渊冰之惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221635_comment'></div>敢图盛礼，辱况华缄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221635_comment'></div>惟推与之过情，顾拙疏之难称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221635_comment'></div>恭以致政司业才猷宏远，望实显融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221635_comment'></div>荐更德教之官，夙著循良之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221635_comment'></div>挂冠高蹈，既钦知足之风；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221635_comment'></div>拔薤良规，方伫不言之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221635_comment'></div>属拘符组，阻造门阑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221635_comment'></div>倾佩之私，敷宣罔既。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221635_comment'></div>谨奉启谢，伏惟照察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221635_comment'></div>不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221635_comment'></div>谨启。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1221635_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在秀州知州任上，论事。作品：《论本州冗员及权官等事》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span>《论拨还平江府定慧院官田》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论本州冗员及权官等事劄子<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221602")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221602_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_1221602_0'>① 寻准尚书省劄子：奉圣旨，盐仓监官减三员。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221602'>窃见朝廷减省冗官，而盐司州郡未能上体朝廷之意，冗滥尚多，无复法制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221602_comment'></div>以本州观之，可以槩见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221602_comment'></div>今具如后：一、本州盐仓乃有监官五员，若减罢三员，未为阙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221602_comment'></div>一、依条，唯繁难县分知县及巡检、县尉、课利场务许差权官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221602_comment'></div>今本州录事参军、司理、县丞、主簿皆是权官，又有未出官人将仕、登仕郎亦权监当，或簿、尉皆不应法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221602_comment'></div>一、通惠镇旧名青龙，兼烟火公事，最为大镇，自来系京朝官窠阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221602_comment'></div>今来监镇二员，内一员是旧宰执家指使富人，初任小使臣，便得上件差遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221602_comment'></div>若系吏部差，不知用何格法？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221602_comment'></div>若系举辟，何由举辟得行？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221602_comment'></div>显见弊幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221602_comment'></div>第一二项如蒙采择，乞作访闻施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221602_comment'></div>第三项或恐庙堂要知，推此措置。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1221602_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221604' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221604' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221604?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论拨还平江府定慧院官田状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1129年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221604")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221604_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221604'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221604'>契勘平江府定慧院昨改充神霄宫日，依宝赦拨赐田十顷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221604_comment'></div>缘本院常住止有田三百一十六亩，遂拨过昆山县及本州华亭县没官田，揍足十顷之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221604_comment'></div>近缘神霄宫废罢，续准圣旨，将平江府神霄宫元管田产并拨与定慧院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221604_comment'></div>切详当时指挥，必谓元初拨过田产尽是定慧院常住，所以依旧拨还本院，不知当来为要满足十顷，于别州县摽拨官田充数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221604_comment'></div>所有拨过本州华亭县官田二百五十亩二角三十步，恐难以拨与定慧院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221604_comment'></div>本州已具状中尚书省，乞赐钧旨施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221604_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_1221604'>〔小贴子〕契勘天下神霄宫多是僧寺改充，一例拨田十顷，后来改还寺院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221604_comment'></div>窃恐似此带却官田不少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221604_comment'></div>方今兵食为急，财用无馀，朝廷不应以官田却与僧徒坐食浮费。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1221604_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
松江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3ed1aaf7e62a43ef981beb99a37e70d0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3ed1aaf7e62a43ef981beb99a37e70d0");'><span id='3ed1aaf7e62a43ef981beb99a37e70d0_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>，52岁</div><div id='3ed1aaf7e62a43ef981beb99a37e70d0' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年12月16日</a>　在秀州知州任上。十二月十六日，金人攻破杭州，遣人檄秀州，令降，程俱弃秀州保华亭，留兵马都监赵士医以守。朝廷遂命俱押米纲赴行在。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1129&endYear=1129')">1129年</a>　在秀州知州任上。得赵子昼书，有诗，创作地点不详，或在秀州至华亭途中。作品：《得赵叔问衢婺道中书作寄》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527342' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527342' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527342?labeling=true' target='_blank'>得赵叔问衢婺道中书作寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（己酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527342")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527342_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527342'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527342'>田中有秫醉渊明，石上无禾养伯龄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527342'>耸涧苍根终郁郁，拂云归翼会冥冥。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527342'>避喧人境心随远，入梦家山眼共青。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527342'>岁晚定知成二老，深惭招隐苦丁宁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527342_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527342'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527342_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
温州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='3118133018e248f88ad226f47868eea3_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("3118133018e248f88ad226f47868eea3");'><span id='3118133018e248f88ad226f47868eea3_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>，53岁</div><div id='3118133018e248f88ad226f47868eea3' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年3月</a>　三月，于温州永嘉朝见高宗，以病乞归乡，听命。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年6月30日</a>　六月三十日，归乡途中作汉儒授经图序，创作地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《汉儒授经图序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221648' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221648' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221648?labeling=true' target='_blank'>汉儒授经图序</a><span class='authorDate'>（建炎四年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221648")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221648_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221648'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221648'>古者尊师而重道，自天子达于庶人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221648_comment'></div>故孔安国授经昭后，死为之服；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221648_comment'></div>亘荣傅明帝于东宫，及即尊位，幸其第，至里门下车，拥经而前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221648_comment'></div>盖其严如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221648_comment'></div>汉兴，诸儒以经谊专门教授，故学者必有师承，源流派别皆可推考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221648_comment'></div>历东汉、二晋以迄有唐，馀风犹有存者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221648_comment'></div>然其间大儒间出，不专以一经章句授诸生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221648_comment'></div>如王通行道于河汾之间，韩愈抗颜于元和之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221648_comment'></div>故从之学者其于行己成务，作为文章，皆足以名世而垂后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221648_comment'></div>如魏徵、王圭、李翱、皇甫湜之徒是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221648_comment'></div>陋哉，夏侯胜之言也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221648_comment'></div>曰：「士病经术不明，经术苟明，取青紫如俯拾地芥耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221648_comment'></div>夫所贵于学者，岂专为是哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221648_comment'></div>而胜以利诱诸生，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221648_comment'></div>西汉之俗，固已尚通达而急进取矣，又使士专为利而学，学而仕，仕而显，则不过容悦患失之人而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221648_comment'></div>如张禹以经为帝师，位丞相，而被佞臣之目，后世议者至以谓西汉之亡以张禹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221648_comment'></div>谷永亦号博通诸经，然因灾异之对，枉公议以阿王氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221648_comment'></div>二人者，皆成帝所取决，有识所企望，而当汉之所以存亡之机者也，然且不顾，方怀奸而徇利，岂其志本在于青紫故耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221648_comment'></div>抑天姿然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221648_comment'></div>后世君子一志于青紫者众，求师务学者寡，学者亦无所师承，此余所以常恨生之晚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221648_comment'></div>方祖宗隆盛之时，如孙明复、胡翼之以经术，杨文公、欧阳文忠以学问文章为一时宗师，学者有所折衷而问业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221648_comment'></div>王荆公出，以经义授东南学者，及得君，行政于天下，靡然宗之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221648_comment'></div>元祐间，苏子瞻以文章主英俊之盟，亦云盛矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221648_comment'></div>余病卧里中，读西汉《儒林传》，观其师弟子授受之严，所谓源流派别皆可推考者，窃有感焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221648_comment'></div>且浮屠氏自释迦文佛传心法与夫讲解之宗，至于今将二千年，而源派谱谍如数一二，下至医巫祝卜、百工之伎，莫不有所师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221648_comment'></div>如吾儒，师承之道乃今蔑焉，所谓学官师弟子，如适相遇于涂耳，盖可叹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221648_comment'></div>则其事业之不竞，语言之不工，名节之不立，无足怪者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221648_comment'></div>因以汉儒授经为图，以想见汉兴之风范云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221648_comment'></div>建炎四年六月三十日，信安程俱序。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1221648_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　秋，归乡途中会毛随，具体地点不详，姑系于此。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　是年，有和柳宗元诗。归乡途中作，创作地点不详，姑系于此。作品：《和柳子厚诗十七首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷六，只存一首《觉哀》。）</span><div id='poem_527099' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527099' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527099?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和柳子厚诗十七首<span class='inlineComment2'>（庚戌）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>觉哀</a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527099")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527099_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527099'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527099'>老境一如此，羲娥日交侵。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527099'>霜毛三千丈，安问尺与寻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527099'>陈力会知止，嘉言佩周任。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527099'>归来北山北，邂逅得素心。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527099'>朝见东日升，暮见西日沉。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527099'>流运有终古，朱颜岂常今。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527099'>譬之如渑酒，岂耐无停斟。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527099'>万化未有极，谁能惜分阴。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527099'>捕影良自苦，沈哀寄微吟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527099'>安知菩提树，正在生死林。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527099_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527099'>长风振遥壑，三籁有馀音。<div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527100' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527100?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>同赵叔问涉涧伐荒蘙得大石壁立乔木苍然上蔽云日因平筑寻丈地时憩其下<span class='inlineComment2'>（《夏初雨后寻愚溪》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527100_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527100'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527100'>披榛亦扪萝，度此幽涧曲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527100'>寒藤绕苍壁，杉桂杂篁竹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527100_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527102' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527102?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>赵叔问被召赴行在<span id='poem_sentence_3_527105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527105'>窈窕烟坞中，苍阴昼森垂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
