id='poem_sentence_6_527105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527105'>谁言一丘壑，傥与汗漫期。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527105_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527105'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_527105_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527106' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527106' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527106?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其八 </span>写怀因简赵叔问<span class='inlineComment2'>（《造法华寺西亭》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527106_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527106'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527106'>胡尘暗中原，世路日以艰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527106'>脱身九死中，自笑老且顽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527106'>才志本不竞，拂衣谢尘寰。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527106'>相从莫逆人，云萝共跻攀。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527106'>固知千里驹，未免山复山<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：汉武谓刘德千里驹。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527106'>我已卜西谷，背崖结三间。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527106'>岂无风篁岭，亦有明月湾<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527106'>平生真远游，旧观忽以还。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527106'>儿童钓遨处，陈迹犹班班。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527106'>叠嶂蔼空翠，暗泉响馀潺。<div id='poem_sentence_9_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_527106'>采芝嵁岩下，长谣想商颜<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：山行得紫芝九本，金芝三。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_527106'>逋客不复驾，居然掩云关。<div id='poem_sentence_11_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_527106'>从来悟泡影，岂但忘触蛮。<div id='poem_sentence_12_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_527106'>所幸戎马际，馀生得长闲。<div id='poem_sentence_13_527106_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527107'>莫嗟无往还，正自主忘客。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527107_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527108'>醉来见闲<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作草间）</span>卧，度此风雨夕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527108'>遥遥慧日峰，法涌分一滴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527108_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527109_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527109'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527109'>急涧无止水，秋兰无故丛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527109'>别来今几年，坐阅毗岚风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527109_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527109_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527110?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十二 </span>天久不雨高田皆坼乡人祈祷阅月乃雨远近告足有足喜者<span class='inlineComment2'>（《首春逢耕者》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527110'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527110'>长夏久不雨，良田失欣荣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527110'>尘生畎浍间，小大空营营。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527110'>麻粟半乾死，所忧负春耕。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527110'>嗷嗷走香火，灵湫汲寒清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527110'>梵呗喧里社，油云被嘉生。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527110'>俄然下甘泽，驩声接柴荆。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527110'>年年镐京宴，及此万宝成。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527110'>偷生得一饱，感慨难为情。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527110'>顾念龙在野，悲歌泪纵横。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527110'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_527110_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527111?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十三 </span>寄江彦文纬<span class='inlineComment2'>（《秋晓行南谷经荒村》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527111'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527111'>往追双玉人，芒屦踏岩谷。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527111'>阿咸今独往，宰上森拱木。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527111'>公来定何时，旧唱犹能续。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527111'>寻壑复穿云，仙山看飞鹿<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527111'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527111'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_527111_0'>⑴ 自注：壬辰岁与彦文、仲嘉纵游山间，时余作诗，有双玉人大阮阿咸之句，又戏作叠韵诗为酒令。前日，复以数句相调，稍欲寻盟矣，故有旧唱犹能续之句。北山有坞曰君让，石间有马迹，相传神仙所尝居，不知君让为何人也。武夷山有飞鹿。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527111_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527112?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十四 </span>十二月二十三日大雪中种物<span class='inlineComment2'>（《巽上人以竹间自采新茶见赠》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527112'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527112'>密云弥四极，纷纷乱空华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527112'>斯须失千嶂，僵木忽以芽。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527112'>眼中万株春，璀璨通岩涯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527112'>迨此凡艳熄，坤舆净无瑕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527112'>苍根移远梅，不惮涧谷遐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527112'>含冰伴幽独，思虑无由邪。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527112'>宝树发银界，无脩證三耶。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527112'>皎皎天宇外，何劳凌绛霞<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527112_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 自注：梵语三耶三佛，亦云藐三菩陀。卢鸿《一十志歌》有云皎皎之子曰独立。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527112_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_527113' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527113' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527113?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十五 </span>野人致紫竹栽手植方丈后<span class='inlineComment2'>（《再至界围岩水帘遂宿岩下》）</span></a><span id='poem_sentence_1_527113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527113'>移家白云根，及此未春雨。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527113'>宠光松菊径，萧散烟霞聚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527113'>咄嗟勿留情，万物乃吾府<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：竹十二竿，故有嶰谷之句。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527113_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527113'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_527113_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527114' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527114' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527114?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十六 </span>得白菌引酒径醉<span id='poem_sentence_2_527114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527114'>得此径陶然，朱颜忽如昨。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527114_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527114'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527114_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_0_527115'>故岁聿其除<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去）</span>，微阳已<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作亦）</span>潜回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527115'>始兹鱼上冰，殷地惊春雷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527115'>急雨暗清夜，飞流散岩隈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527115'>迟明起四顾，妙境神所开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527115'>未信小有洞，苍崖隔凡埃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527115'>琤淙十九泉，漱玉松风哀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527115'>褰裳喜欲狂，幽兴不可裁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527115'>妙喜真断取，呼猿定飞来。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527115'>相与俯清駃，传杯聊溯洄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527115'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_527115_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

绍兴
