href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1130&endYear=1130')">1130年</a>　冬，复召赴绍兴府行在，时任朝请郎、直秘阁。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年1月6日</a>　正月六日夜，在绍兴朝请郎、直秘阁任上作。作品：《辛亥正月六日夜雷已发声大雨达旦山中流泉高下喷薄殆不啻九十九不减仇池也》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷六。）</span><div id='poem_527115' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527115' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527115?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和柳子厚诗十七首<span class='inlineComment2'>（庚戌）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其十七 </span>辛亥正月六日夜雷已发声大雨达旦山中流泉高下喷薄殆不啻九十九不减仇池也<span class='inlineComment2'>（《湘口馆潇湘二水所会》）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1130年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527115")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_527115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527115'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527115'>故岁聿其除<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：去）</span>，微阳已<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作亦）</span>潜回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527115'>始兹鱼上冰，殷地惊春雷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527115'>急雨暗清夜，飞流散岩隈。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527115'>迟明起四顾，妙境神所开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527115'>未信小有洞，苍崖隔凡埃。<div id='poem_sentence_4_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_527115'>琤淙十九泉，漱玉松风哀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_527115'>褰裳喜欲狂，幽兴不可裁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_527115'>妙喜真断取，呼猿定飞来。<div id='poem_sentence_7_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_527115'>相与俯清駃，传杯聊溯洄。<div id='poem_sentence_8_527115_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_527115'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_527115_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年3月4日</a>　在绍兴朝请郎、直秘阁任上，三月四日，上劄子论事。作品：《绍兴元年三月四日上殿劄子》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十八。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年3月7日</a>　三月七日，除秘书少监，有次韵江端友诗，时在绍兴。作品：《次韵江子我见寄长句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527345' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527345' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527345?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵江子我见寄长句<span class='inlineComment2'>（余时初忝袐书少监）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年3月7日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527345")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527345_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527345'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527345'>泥行正作龟藏穴，雾隐初徵豹一斑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527345'>岂有高标如冠玉，况无谈舌解连环。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527345'>一登文石趋宣室，三窃蟠桃向道山。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527345'>早晚共寻鸡黍约，林泉犹得半生闲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527345_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527345'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527345_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在绍兴秘书少监任上。春，访毛随。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年4月1日</a>　在绍兴秘书少监任上。四月一日，题李伯时《郦生长揖图》作品：《题郦生长揖图》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题郦生长揖图<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年4月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221649")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221649'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221649'>李伯时作《郦生长揖图》，直作高皇踞床，两女子洗，而郦生长揖，此徒见汉高无礼、食其不屈之意，而无以见高皇闻善而服，改过下士，汉所以兴之故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221649_comment'></div>要当作辍洗起衣，躧履迎客之状，乃胜耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221649_comment'></div>方是时，天下草昧，糜烂土崩之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221649_comment'></div>沛公踞见一里监门，其失亦微耳，非汉所以强弱兴亡之所系者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221649_comment'></div>而食其遽以谓将以助秦，而非所以攻秦，何也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221649_comment'></div>岂辨士专以捭阖动听为务，而其言不得不夸耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221649_comment'></div>是不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221649_comment'></div>食其为是无当之言可也，而沛公豁达聪明之君也，而可以虚言屈乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221649_comment'></div>夫得士者昌，失士者亡，有国家者皆然，而危乱之时为甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221649_comment'></div>故萧何以韩信用不用卜汉高之霸王，晋人以谢安石起不起知江左之兴亡，唐室以裴度进退为天下安危，盖士之不可失如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221649_comment'></div>使汉高失一食其可耳，然骏骨不收，绝足不至；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221649_comment'></div>巢卵不育，凤鸟不下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221649_comment'></div>士有深藏高举，望望然去之而已，况声音颜色拒之千里之外乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221649_comment'></div>则其不足以攻秦而足以自亡也明矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221649_comment'></div>是理也，非郦生之夸言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221649_comment'></div>辛亥孟夏朔，信安程俱书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221649_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年4月8日</a>　在绍兴秘书少监任上。请修日历，四月八日下诏，然朝廷多事，未克行。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年5月24日</a>　在绍兴秘书少监任上。五月二十四日，又言及修日历之事。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年7月</a>　在绍兴秘书少监任上。七月，《麟台故事》书成。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《麟台故事》共五卷，版本详参《程俱年谱》（上）第98页。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在绍兴秘书少监任上。进麟台故事申省状。作品：《进麟台故事申省状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十八。）</span><div id='poem_1221620' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221620' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221620?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进麟台故事申省状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221620")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221620_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221620'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221620'>右，某窃见车驾移跸以来，百司文书例从省记，按以从事，蠹弊或生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221620_comment'></div>日者朝廷复置秘书省，稽参旧章，稍储俊造，而某滥膺盛选，待罪省贰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221620_comment'></div>窃以谓典籍之府，宪章所由，当有记述，以存一司之守，辄采摭见闻，及方册所载，法令所该，比次为书，凡十有二篇，列为四卷，名曰《麟台故事》，缮写成二册，诣都堂呈纳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221620_comment'></div>所有进本，欲乞批状送通进司收接投进，仍乞以副本藏之省阁，以备讨论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221620_comment'></div>谨具申尚书省，伏候钧旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1221620_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年9月11日</a>　九月十一日，除中书舍人，兼侍讲，时在绍兴。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在绍兴，除中书舍人，兼侍讲，多次恳辞。作品：《辞免权侍讲状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十九。）</span>《辞免召试中书舍人状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十九。）</span>《辞免除中书舍人状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十九。）</span>《中书舍人谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_1221566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免权侍讲状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221566")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221566'>右，臣今月八日准尚书省劄子，三省同奉圣旨，差臣兼权侍讲者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221566_comment'></div>臣一介愚贱，上蒙恩简，虽是暂权，然臣伏自惟念学术浅陋，心力衰疲，今此尽瘁丝纶，尚恐速荒疏误忘之罪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221566_comment'></div>若侍经帷幄，必将有鄙拙尸素之讥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221566_comment'></div>闻命之初，惶恐无喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221566_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特降睿旨，别选时俊，罢臣上件权侍讲指挥，俾安愚分，不胜幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221566_comment'></div>谨录奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1221566_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1221566'><span class='label'>按：</span>十月十日奉圣旨不允。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1221566_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1221559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免召试中书舍人状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221559")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221559'>右，某准尚书省劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云。）</span>闻命震惶，不知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221559_comment'></div>伏念臣才术不竞，性质惷愚，加以积忧薰心，志思凋耗，问学寖废，文字荒疏，使勉就于试言，必难充于盛选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221559_comment'></div>所有召试恩命，伏望圣慈特赐寝罢，庶安愚分，不致疾颠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221559_comment'></div>无任<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1221559_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞免除中书舍人状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221560")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221560'>右，臣今月十一日准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨召试中书舍人，寻具奏辞免，乞赐寝罢上件恩命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221560_comment'></div>十三日，准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨，程俱特免试，除中书舍人，日下供职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221560_comment'></div>臣仰戴误恩，益不遑处，敢布诚悃，上渎睿聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221560_comment'></div>窃以西掖词臣，当世高选，自非文学足以资润色而备顾问，才识足以明治道而达国体，公望所属，岂敢冒居？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221560_comment'></div>而臣迂惷之质既无取材，鄙陋之文又不足道，年龄迫于耆艾，心志耗于隐忧，苟贪宠荣，不量称否，必速官谤，上负简求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221560_comment'></div>而况班著之中，俊彦甚众，以之充选，谅不乏才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221560_comment'></div>猥以命臣，实深惶惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221560_comment'></div>伏望圣慈察其恳款，收还新命，曲赐允俞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221560_comment'></div>蝼蚁之私，不胜幸愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221560_comment'></div>臣无任。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1221560_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1221536' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221536' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221536?labeling=true' target='_blank'>中书舍人谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221536")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221536_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221536'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221536'>臣某言：臣伏奉告命，授臣试中书舍人，仍赐紫章服者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221536_comment'></div>册府䌷书，误玷英髦之首；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221536_comment'></div>词垣簪笔，猥当润色之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221536_comment'></div>敢意非才，骤膺明命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221536_comment'></div>衔恩则厚，揣己若惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221536_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221536_comment'></div>臣窃以喉舌之司，繄万几之自出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221536_comment'></div>丝纶之任，实庶政之与闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221536_comment'></div>不惟有取于尔雅深厚之词，盖亦兼收于献纳论思之益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221536_comment'></div>岂非人才进退，系国体之重轻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221536_comment'></div>政事弛张，关天下之利害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221536_comment'></div>号令一出，播敷万邦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221536_comment'></div>挈维固在于股肱，补拾可无于讽议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221536_comment'></div>至于华国之具，亦责代言之工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221536_comment'></div>是以祖宗以来，制敕必由于三省；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221536_comment'></div>侍从之选，给舍每高于一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221536_comment'></div>自非识足以见微，才足以经远，文知体要，无惭苏李之能，学贯古今，可备崔高之问，则何以仰当睿简，俯厌师言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221536_comment'></div>孚德意于四方，亦中兴之一助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221536_comment'></div>如臣者少而孤陋，壮益钝顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221536_comment'></div>述业自知其不丰，缵言未足以明道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221536_comment'></div>早岁栖迟于湖海，盖将终身；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221536_comment'></div>中年出入于朝廷，诚非素意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221536_comment'></div>何图晚暮，上被奖知，察之以日月之明，施之以天地之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221536_comment'></div>比者召自庐里，赐对宴间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221536_comment'></div>曾微尘露之裨，收此桑榆之景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221536_comment'></div>麟台复建，既先诸子之鸣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221536_comment'></div>凤阁方虚，更滥群英之吹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221536_comment'></div>且于廷谢，锡以身章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221536_comment'></div>敢辞濡翼之讥，祗重临渊之惧！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221536_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧仁广被，汤德又新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221536_comment'></div>饬蛊坏于倾否之时，奋乾刚于拨乱之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221536_comment'></div>宵衣旰食，缵周室之丕基；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221536_comment'></div>藏疾纳污，廓汉皇之大度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221536_comment'></div>故待人也轻以约，亦嘉善而矜不能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221536_comment'></div>致是逖疏，有斯遭遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221536_comment'></div>臣敢不稍寻旧学，益慕前修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221536_comment'></div>披肝胆以献诚，或能千虑而有得；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221536_comment'></div>竭铅驽以自效，庶几十驾而可希。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221536_comment'></div>敢怀患失之心，永矢捐躯之报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221536_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221536_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1221536_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年10月4日</a>　在绍兴中书舍人任上，十月四日，上书言耿延禧和议误国事。作品：《缴词头状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十九。耿延禧事迹不详。）</span><div id='poem_1221562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴词头状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年10月4日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221562")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221562'>今月二十七日，准中书门下省刑房送到词头一道，内朝请郎耿延禧复龙图阁学士，令臣命行者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221562_comment'></div>右，臣窃以谓刑赏进退，皆当览天下之公议而行之，则劝沮明而天下服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221562_comment'></div>夫致天下之乱者，蔡京、王黼、童贯及京之子攸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221562_comment'></div>致京城之陷者，耿南仲及其子延禧者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221562_comment'></div>此天下之公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221562_comment'></div>当靖康时，南仲以官僚之旧，虽避宰相之位，而实当宰相之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221562_comment'></div>爱子延禧，乃一时之宗主，陷京城者，非此而谁？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221562_comment'></div>臣以谓南仲、延禧之罪不在于议和，而在于沮天下之兵，盖兵威振而后和可成也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221562_comment'></div>以古今之迹考之，则可知已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221562_comment'></div>其所谓沮天下已到之兵者，前日臣寮言之备矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221562_comment'></div>今二圣之北狩未还，宗社之艰危未济，上下岌岌，宵旰靡宁，南仲、延禧不得不任其责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221562_comment'></div>而乃起自废放，尽复旧职，无乃废天下之公议乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221562_comment'></div>所有延禧复龙图阁学士词头，臣未敢命行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1221562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年11月</a>　在绍兴中书舍人任上，十一月，举荐冯楫、许德之、许亢宗、吴表臣、郑作肃。作品：《应诏荐士状》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十九。据《建炎以来系年要录》卷四十八：绍兴元年十月二十六日己丑升越州为绍兴府。）</span><div id='poem_1221571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221571' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221571?labeling=true' target='_blank'>应诏荐士状</a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221571")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221571_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221571'>准尚书吏部牒，准尚书省劄子，备奉十一月十九日手诏，令侍从官举三人已上，同罪保举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221571_comment'></div>臣今以所知保举如后：朝奉郎、权发遣巴州军州事冯楫，劲直敢言，通理性之学，故临大事而不惧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221571_comment'></div>尝说二凶贼，得其要领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221571_comment'></div>其忧国救时之志甚切，若备台谏之选，必能知无不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221571_comment'></div>朝散郎、主管江州太平观许德之，端靖有守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221571_comment'></div>宣和初任太常少卿，遽求外补，则其恬退可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221571_comment'></div>其性行学问，可备师儒议论之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221571_comment'></div>朝散郎、主管临安府洞霄宫许亢宗，静粹有立，学问亦优。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221571_comment'></div>靖康元年，尝任起居郎、朝散郎、尚书考功员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221571_comment'></div>潘良贵，性质刚方，辅以学识，投闲累岁，涵养益深，议论正平，有志许国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221571_comment'></div>朝散郎、尚书司勋员外郎吴表臣，学有师承，性行纯静。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221571_comment'></div>承议郎、权通判临安府事郑作肃，嗜学知方，思虑详审，清修有立，可任以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221571_comment'></div>右，谨件如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221571_comment'></div>臣所举冯楫等，如蒙擢用，后不如所举，臣甘当同罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221571_comment'></div>谨录奏闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221571_comment'></div>谨状。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在绍兴中书舍人任上，有和江纬诗。作品：《和答江彦文送行长句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527343' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527343' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527343?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和答江彦文送行长句<span class='inlineComment2'>（二首　辛亥）</span><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527343")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527343_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527343'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527343'>醉里求名苦不情，翛然谁信万缘轻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527343'>却观尘境端如梦，更喜幽栖得此生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527343'>游客乍归寒雀噪，山人还去晓猿惊。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527343'>会当蜡屐同幽讨，无限青山照眼明。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527343_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527343'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527343_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527344' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527344' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527344?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527344_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527344'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527344'>赠行新句比阳春，朝奏当年竦缙绅。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527344'>素业异时应有待，玄谈高处亦无论。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527344'>平生肮脏皆华首，阅世崎岖信损神。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527344'>只恐鹤书还赴陇，未容公作独醒人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527344_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527344'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527344_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在绍兴中书舍人任上，为毛随作墓志铭。作品：《朝散大夫行尚书司封员外郎致仕毛公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1221797' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221797' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221797?labeling=true' target='_blank'>朝散大夫行尚书司封员外郎致仕毛公墓志铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴元年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1131年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221797")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221797_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221797'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221797'>建炎四年秋，有旨召朝散大夫毛随诣行在所，尚书下衢州趣为驾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221797_comment'></div>既至，始见政事堂，陈天下利害，慷慨明白，有言动听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221797_comment'></div>先是，虏比岁大入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221797_comment'></div>是年春，猖蹶至东南并海郡回，留兵淮南，须凉秋，示必渡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221797_comment'></div>君言：「按《汉志》，岁星所在，国不可伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221797_comment'></div>昔汤之元祀，岁星顺行，与日合于房。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221797_comment'></div>房心，宋亳分也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221797_comment'></div>周之兴也，武王还自盟津，至于丰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221797_comment'></div>明年，岁星顺行，与日合于柳，建留于张，其分实河洛之墟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221797_comment'></div>故武王定鼎洛邑而周公迄营成周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221797_comment'></div>今年冬岁星当躔于斗，岁主福德，斗吴越之会，盖与商周之事略同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221797_comment'></div>天其或者将厌乱而兴宋乎，虏不南渡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221797_comment'></div>然敌人进退，本不足言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221797_comment'></div>自古御戎上策，莫先自治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221797_comment'></div>今六军在行日久，岂无致果杀敌之心，在朝廷所以用之耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221797_comment'></div>为今日计，莫若保天险、增战备，权宜都邑，不为轻动，以系四方之观听，则人心不摇，士气日壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221797_comment'></div>此孙武所谓恃吾有以待之者也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221797_comment'></div>因条上三策，所以措画之宜甚悉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221797_comment'></div>已而诏以为尚书司封员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221797_comment'></div>明年春，有荐公材中御史者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221797_comment'></div>方召对，而君病矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221797_comment'></div>会余亦召至行在所，备官兰台，间至君舍问所苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221797_comment'></div>病寖剧，则日一至其舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221797_comment'></div>君上气加肿，奄奄息仅属，言及天下事，辄奋髯扼掔，语吃吃不能尽意，则太息而止，不以后事一语属人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221797_comment'></div>余未尝不悲其志而惜其病且死也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221797_comment'></div>请老，诏以本官朝散大夫、尚书司封员外郎致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221797_comment'></div>竟以绍兴元年四月己巳卒于越州大善僧寺之寓舍，享年五十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221797_comment'></div>季子叔度实从以丧归其家，将以某月某甲子葬君于其乡某山之原，来请铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221797_comment'></div>崇宁初，当国者取士大夫所上书举为二籍，余与彦时在邪籍中，皆罢吏归乡郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221797_comment'></div>彦时固邑子，至是始识面，与游驩甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221797_comment'></div>时年皆未壮，平居相与言，必天下所以治乱兴衰之槩，与夫出处去就之宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221797_comment'></div>所从游往往一世英豪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221797_comment'></div>后十五年，上皇稍更政事，去泰甚，党禁少弛，余寖被收录为尚书郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221797_comment'></div>君才脱州县，因以类进，得为秘书省校书郎，迁著作佐郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221797_comment'></div>会二府三公相倾夺，思以不克绍述致罪宰相者，出君通判虔州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221797_comment'></div>已而相以它罪罢，党事复缓，而北方兵起矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221797_comment'></div>余知君最深，其出处又如此，是安得辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221797_comment'></div>君讳随，字彦时，衢州江山县人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221797_comment'></div>其世所自出与徙著之由，则有先世之谱谍在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221797_comment'></div>曾祖讳焕，赠中大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221797_comment'></div>祖讳恺，朝请郎、赠正议大夫，清约有古人之介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221797_comment'></div>父讳勉，朝奉郎、赠中大夫，躬行有家法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221797_comment'></div>母江氏，累赠令人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221797_comment'></div>君年始冠，中绍圣四年进士第，调秀州华亭县尉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221797_comment'></div>其持身效官，为邑人之所钦爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221797_comment'></div>秩满，调明州鄞县主簿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221797_comment'></div>迁文林郎，为江宁府司户曹事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221797_comment'></div>丁外艰，服除，监大观东库，改宣教郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221797_comment'></div>丁内艰，服除，遂入秘书省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221797_comment'></div>其在虔州也，靖康初，朝廷调诸郡将吏防秋北边，虏犯河南，经制使复裒见卒援京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221797_comment'></div>虔居江西上游，俗喜斗轻死，群不逞乘间起，啸聚山泽，众且数千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221797_comment'></div>郡吏凭虚堞、张空弮以示备，君驰喻诸邑，索土豪大猾、拳勇奇技，得数十人，彻卫与语，开怀见诚，人人感奋，争自效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221797_comment'></div>因使各部其众，淬励须战，则又榜盗区曰所取渠魁耳，胁从皆吾人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221797_comment'></div>凡散归闾里，持锄耰者，不为盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221797_comment'></div>居数日，贼党散三之二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221797_comment'></div>公择所募，授以方略曰：「贼酋以其众今在某山中，若为我生致之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221797_comment'></div>期三日反报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221797_comment'></div>公还，未及城，渠魁以生得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221797_comment'></div>朝廷嘉其功，进官三等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221797_comment'></div>时中原新罹虏祸，剧盗溃卒，惊剽相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221797_comment'></div>君方摄行郡事，益募士除戎器、谨关候、侍糇粮，郡以无事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221797_comment'></div>军兴调发，应时趣办，而人不扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221797_comment'></div>君幼则警敏，尝读《汉书》一传三千言，数过辄成诵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221797_comment'></div>长游学校，有俊声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221797_comment'></div>一出仕，即坐上书不得调，于是刻意为己之学，涵泳六经、诸史、百氏之间，穷理尽性之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221797_comment'></div>至天文、地理、历数、卜筮，无不学，学必穷日夜，书必汗牛马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1221797_comment'></div>至占验消息，猝然失之，即弃去，又学不休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1221797_comment'></div>其为文历落平易，独写其意所欲道，意尽便止，粲然立成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1221797_comment'></div>论事抗颜不疑，视天下事若无难者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1221797_comment'></div>其为吏自县簿尉、参幕府至监一郡，随事不苟，必有所裨助建立，所历有能声，然人卒不能以能吏名也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1221797_comment'></div>妻李氏，故朝奉大夫秠之女，累封宜人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1221797_comment'></div>二男子，曰伯亮，将仕郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1221797_comment'></div>曰叔度，举进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1221797_comment'></div>一女子，嫁从政郎詹尧谟，前卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1221797_comment'></div>孙男一人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1221797_comment'></div>集其文，得十五卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1221797_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_76_1221797'>士有才奋，勇于敢为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1221797_comment'></div>火驰机张，蹈险若夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1221797_comment'></div>不奠其发，以颠以危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1221797_comment'></div>亦有君子，负绳抱规。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1221797_comment'></div>择地而行，惟古是稽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1221797_comment'></div>诡以应变，昧时与几。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1221797_comment'></div>君学而思，又敏于施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1221797_comment'></div>吏不蕲能，不苟不隳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1221797_comment'></div>学不蕲言，期见于时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1221797_comment'></div>而阨于初，而陨方跻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1221797_comment'></div>匪死之哀，君志是悲。</div><div id='poem_sentence_86_1221797_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1131&endYear=1131')">1131年</a>　在绍兴中书舍人任上，喜得家书，有诗。作品：《会稽喜得家书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527462' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527462' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527462?labeling=true' target='_blank'>会稽喜得家书</a><span class='authorDate'>（辛亥）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527462")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527462_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527462'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527462'>黄耳东来一破颜，直从松竹报平安。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527462'>遥知云顶峰前住，霜鬣风篁六月寒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527462_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527462'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527462_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1132&endYear=1132')">1132年1月10日</a>　在绍兴中书舍人任上，正月十日，随高宗发绍兴。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='578775ddcc54440493994566ba68b1b4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("578775ddcc54440493994566ba68b1b4");'><span id='578775ddcc54440493994566ba68b1b4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1135')">1134-1135年</a>，57-58岁</div><div id='578775ddcc54440493994566ba68b1b4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1134&endYear=1134')">1134年</a>　差知漳州，以病辞，改提举台州崇道观，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1135&endYear=1135')">1135年</a>　复集英殿修撰，上谢表，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《集英殿修撰谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_1221538' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221538' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221538?labeling=true' target='_blank'>集英殿修撰谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1135年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221538")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221538_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221538'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221538'>臣某言：今月十九日，伏奉告命，授臣依前左朝奉大夫、充集英殿修撰，差遣赐如故者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221538_comment'></div>负衅投闲，居怀惴惕，均釐肆眚，与被甄收。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221538_comment'></div>承命若惊，衔恩知感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221538_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221538_comment'></div>伏念臣戆而自信，愚不知机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221538_comment'></div>少也好修，弗踰绳墨之外；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221538_comment'></div>壮而多事，妄怀畎亩之忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221538_comment'></div>叩阍蚤丽于丹书，随牒俄嗟于皓首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221538_comment'></div>及稍宽于党禁，遂浸列于周行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221538_comment'></div>再游东观著作之廷，三与南宫笺奏之末。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221538_comment'></div>邅回久次，黾勉一心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221538_comment'></div>辞职奉常，获守匹夫之志；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221538_comment'></div>分忧槜李，敢言循吏之能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221538_comment'></div>属当隉杌凋敝之馀，而行还定安辑之政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221538_comment'></div>军旅诚非于素学，抚绥方尽于夙心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221538_comment'></div>决知绵薄之才，难抗猖狂之虏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221538_comment'></div>利兵坚甲，既无吴会之师屯；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221538_comment'></div>高城深池，又异江湖之天险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221538_comment'></div>度不能婴城而死节，固不敢开门而请降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221538_comment'></div>蚤夜以思，进退惟谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221538_comment'></div>先奉宰臣之委教，且言朝命之已颁，茍守御之力既穷，则迁避而行亦可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221538_comment'></div>方出城之次日，适被召于行朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221538_comment'></div>而宣抚使藏怒久深，幸灾而发，怵吏兵而诱乱，揭捕赏以见要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221538_comment'></div>劾以深文，期于必死。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221538_comment'></div>仰赖皇明之旁烛，不俾怙威而肆行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221538_comment'></div>趣至永嘉，许归故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221538_comment'></div>恭惟拯溺救焚之意，可谓生死肉骨之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221538_comment'></div>顾影扪心，沦肌刻骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221538_comment'></div>晚蒙睿奖，擢寘从班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221538_comment'></div>念小己之难胜，繄厚恩之宜报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221538_comment'></div>事君尽礼，敢萌贪荣患失之思；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221538_comment'></div>操心也危，每有私忧过计之累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221538_comment'></div>宿愆难赦，孤迹易摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221538_comment'></div>谴诃实出于自贻，全贷终归于天造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221538_comment'></div>旋膺出綍，误俾分符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221538_comment'></div>复再致于烦言，徒仰喧于聪听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221538_comment'></div>兹缘大享，爰发涣恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221538_comment'></div>敢图雨露之沾，俯暨朽枯之质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221538_comment'></div>稍垂甄叙，曲被记怜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221538_comment'></div>念畴昔以知非，皆冥顽之所致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221538_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下尧仁丕冒，汤德又新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221538_comment'></div>日就月将，方缉熙于大学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221538_comment'></div>云行雨施，期润泽于群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221538_comment'></div>思以任贤使能而致中兴，故虽片善寸长而不终弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221538_comment'></div>顾惟奇贱，适有遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221538_comment'></div>愚闇无知，悔莫追于往咎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221538_comment'></div>衰迟待尽，情犹切于慕君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221538_comment'></div>寒灰无冀于复然，病马尚蕲于终惠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221538_comment'></div>誓当糜陨，少谢生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221538_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221538_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1221538_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='fc550b93bbfc46fdaaf4d3d8fda9458a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fc550b93bbfc46fdaaf4d3d8fda9458a");'><span id='fc550b93bbfc46fdaaf4d3d8fda9458a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1137')">1136-1137年</a>，59-60岁</div><div id='fc550b93bbfc46fdaaf4d3d8fda9458a' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　春，为富延年作墓志铭，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《宋故右迪功郎监潭州南岳庙富君墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十一。）</span><div id='poem_1221783' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221783' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221783?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故右迪功郎监潭州南岳庙富君墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221783")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221783_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221783'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221783'>君讳延年，字季长，富氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221783_comment'></div>世家京洛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221783_comment'></div>君之大父司空讳严，嘉祐中以秘书监守苏州，秩满，上章告老。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221783_comment'></div>既得请，将归河南，吴人争挽留。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221783_comment'></div>父老前曰：「公之惠爱在此邦，邦人怀思将无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221783_comment'></div>愿毋去我，百岁后，吴人谨蒸尝、护松槚，当世世如桐乡朱仲卿也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221783_comment'></div>公平时固已乐吴中风物之美，因留居不去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221783_comment'></div>没，葬吴县之宝华山，子孙遂为吴郡人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221783_comment'></div>父讳临，官至朝散郎、守池州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221783_comment'></div>君池州府君之季子也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221783_comment'></div>幼颖悟，长力学问，行修谨，笃孝养，不妄交游，乡里后生往往从之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221783_comment'></div>乡举三上不第，建炎二年，礼部特奏名释褐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221783_comment'></div>浙西盐香使者取以为江浦盐官察廉，遂以为使属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221783_comment'></div>未几，乞监潭州南岳庙以归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221783_comment'></div>绍兴六年正月一日，以疾卒于家，享年六十五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221783_comment'></div>三月十七日，其孤与贤、直惠葬君宝华山先茔之侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221783_comment'></div>夫人龚氏，池州府君夫人之侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221783_comment'></div>令淑有闻，后君二年卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221783_comment'></div>五女，皆嫁士族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221783_comment'></div>君资和厚，与人交尽诚无表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221783_comment'></div>家故贫，衣食间有馀，则以周族属之急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221783_comment'></div>时具酒食、延宾客，常以读书赋诗自娱，泊无陨穫之态。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221783_comment'></div>今资政殿学士衢州使君，君之从侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221783_comment'></div>直惠自吴走千里，以君行状来谋所以著君之美而垂不朽者，资政以诿某。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221783_comment'></div>某惟郑国忠文公忠节直道、丰功伟烈，平生仰之如北斗泰山；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221783_comment'></div>司空之耆德遗爱东南，搢绅至今能道之，而君实其家令子孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221783_comment'></div>绍圣初，某方客吴下，尝过林德祖大云坊，遇君从容食顷，今四十六年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221783_comment'></div>德祖善士，所与游亦可知其槩矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221783_comment'></div>又某辱资政使君知与之旧，铭其可辞？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221783_comment'></div>则叙而为之铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221783_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1221783'>学而敏，友则端兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221783_comment'></div>沽不沽，恬以安兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221783_comment'></div>老而仕，世方艰兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221783_comment'></div>日崦嵫，道阻邅兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221783_comment'></div>全而归，从厥先兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1221783_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年6月9日</a>　六月九日，除徽猷阁待制，上谢表，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《除徽猷阁待制谢表》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷二十。）</span><div id='poem_1221539' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221539' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221539?labeling=true' target='_blank'>徽猷阁待制谢表</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年6月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221539")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221539_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221539'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221539'>臣某言：伏奉告命，授臣依前左朝奉大夫、充徽猷阁待制，差遣赐如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221539_comment'></div>臣寻具奏辞免，准尚书省劄子，奉圣旨不允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221539_comment'></div>臣已望阙祗受讫者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221539_comment'></div>窃禄真祠，久惭素食；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221539_comment'></div>升华延阁，复玷清班。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221539_comment'></div>仰戴圣恩，俯惭非据。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221539_comment'></div>臣诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221539_comment'></div>伏念臣才非强济，性实戆迂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221539_comment'></div>仕则慕君，不自量其愚贱；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221539_comment'></div>学思为己，期无玷于操修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221539_comment'></div>不敢枉尺以直寻，率常进寸而退尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221539_comment'></div>名书邪籍，知芹献之已疏；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221539_comment'></div>力尽陈编，愧管窥之时见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221539_comment'></div>晚逢睿哲，骤辱奖知，拯之水火之中，召自渔樵之野。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221539_comment'></div>冠蓬山之众俊，已愧无堪；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221539_comment'></div>陟凤阁之华资，深知不称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221539_comment'></div>仍持末学，入侍清光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221539_comment'></div>尘飞何益于太山，萤照难施于赫日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221539_comment'></div>曾微补报，自取谴诃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221539_comment'></div>庇身俾托于殊庭，就食即安于故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221539_comment'></div>感恩念咎，劫扫杜门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221539_comment'></div>想魏阙以驰神，卧漳滨而永叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221539_comment'></div>何图洪造，曲记孤踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221539_comment'></div>不遗簪履之馀，复置论思之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221539_comment'></div>恳辞不遂，成命莫回。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221539_comment'></div>昔张敞以罪废屏居，卒见收于后效；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221539_comment'></div>刘毅虽年耆偏疾，亦不弃于公朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221539_comment'></div>顾臣何人，有此厚幸！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221539_comment'></div>此盖伏遇皇帝陛下乾坤侔大，日月并明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221539_comment'></div>沛然雨露之施，涣若风雷之发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221539_comment'></div>春生秋肃，莫非成物之仁；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221539_comment'></div>赏庆刑威，咸出至公之造。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221539_comment'></div>求贤用吉士，方远迹于周王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221539_comment'></div>嘉善矜不能，每同符于古训。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221539_comment'></div>市骨冀来于驵骏，采葑无间于卑微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221539_comment'></div>有如愞愚，弗忍遐弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221539_comment'></div>臣敢不永思报称，仰服恩荣？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221539_comment'></div>顾虽颠沛之间，无忘素守；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221539_comment'></div>苟有捐糜之会，敢爱馀生！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221539_comment'></div>臣无任感天荷圣激切屏营之至，谨奉表称谢以闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221539_comment'></div>臣某诚惶诚恐，顿首顿首，谨言。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1221539_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年8月6日</a>　八月六日，感怀赋诗，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《丙辰八月六日作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527348' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527348' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527348?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丙辰八月六日作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年8月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527348")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527348_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527348'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527348'>负痾今日四周年，药裹关心雪满颠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527348'>坐失分阴嗟倏忽，行扶跬步苦跰𨇤。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527348'>支离徒费三<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作千）</span>钟粟，潦倒仍依二顷田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527348'>身在山林名绛阙，无功饱食愧前贤。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527348_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527348'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527348_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年9月</a>　九月，题《八师经》，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《题八师经后》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221652' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221652' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221652?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题八师经后<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221652")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221652_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221652'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221652'>余观《八师经》所说虽非无上般若圆顿法门，然实毗尼梵纲之权舆，普贤净行之门户，而生死畏途之梁筏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221652_comment'></div>明白切近，虽涂之人皆若可解。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221652_comment'></div>使四海之内横目之人普皆信受，坚持不退，为善而不为恶，如佛所云，则坐證四果，长揖三涂，何远之有？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221652_comment'></div>且人人推不杀之心而充之，可使冤亲平等，慈心相向，而岂有斗狠贼害、伏尸流血之事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221652_comment'></div>人人推不盗之心而充之，可使廉逊兴行，货弃于地，于非其有，一介不取，而岂有夺攘贪鄙、攫金胠箧之事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221652_comment'></div>人人推不淫之心而充之，可使男如柳下惠，女如共伯姬，贞洁自持，不欺闇室，而岂有侵凌诱略、罗欲乱伦之事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221652_comment'></div>人人推不饮酒之心而充之，可使饮食语言离诸过患，端虚正念，齐圣温克，而岂有淫酗昏暴、流连荒亡之事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221652_comment'></div>人人推无妄言绮语、两舌恶口之心而充之，可使笃实诚信，不訾不欺，而岂有诳诬交扇之事哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221652_comment'></div>人人知老病死苦之无常，少壮盛强之不可恃，而操心爱日、远恶为善之不可不勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221652_comment'></div>夫如是，何畏乎生死？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221652_comment'></div>何怖乎恶道？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221652_comment'></div>无疑无慊，俯仰无怍，终日尽世，泰然安乐，而相与倘佯于仁寿之域，是则极乐之土、可封之俗已，岂非立言垂教者之本意，爱人治国者之至愿，而有生之所甚乐者乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221652_comment'></div>故余思广其传焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221652_comment'></div>绍兴六年九月日，俱谨识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_13_1221652_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年11月1日</a>　十一月一日，题杜范欧公帖，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《题杜范欧公帖》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221650' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221650' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221650?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题杜范欧公帖<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴六年十一月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1136年11月1日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221650")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221650_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221650'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221650'>正献公之全德元老，文正公之宏才伟望，文忠公之端亮文学，端委庙堂，不动声气，而可使夷夏乂安，风俗清美矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221650_comment'></div>时非不逢，而不既其用，仁人志士未尝不叹息于斯焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221650_comment'></div>绍兴六年十一月旦，信安程俱获观于西安长寿僧舍，谨题。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1221650_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1136&endYear=1136')">1136年</a>　过徐节之宅有感赋诗，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《过徐节之宅有感三首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十一。）</span><div id='poem_527506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过徐节之宅有感三首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丙辰）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527506")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527506'>颐庆堂成未一年，窗中紫翠列千山。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527506'>重来前日持杯地，桃李飘零春自阑。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527506'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527506_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527507' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527507' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527507?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丙辰）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527507_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527507'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527507'>市骏不应遗泛驾，更刀犹足中桑林。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527507'>故知老骥思千里，未害鸱夷致万金。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527507_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527507'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527507_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_527508' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527508' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527508?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（丙辰）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_527508_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527508'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527508'>游倦归来老境侵，炎凉薄俗见升沉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527508'>东阡北陌追游处，独对春风泪满襟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527508_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527508'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_527508_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月2日</a>　正月二日，题《温公帖石刻》，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《题温公帖石刻》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十五。）</span><div id='poem_1221651' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221651' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221651?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题温公帖石刻<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴七年正月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年1月2日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221651")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221651_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221651'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221651'>文正温公之清节直道，内相高平公之懿行硕学，盖朝廷之蓍龟，搢绅之标表也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221651_comment'></div>事在国史，誉在天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221651_comment'></div>然其造次之间，理言遗事，士夫莫不宝而传之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221651_comment'></div>衢州学舍尝得温公贻高平公帖，摹而刻之石，置诸公堂之壁，使学者出入观省，以想见醇儒硕德遗风馀烈之无穷，与夫著书立言之不苟如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221651_comment'></div>且《资治通鉴》之书，文正实挈其维纲，而笔削裁成之功繄高平公之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221651_comment'></div>是时二公以道义相从于寂寞之滨，凡前古是非成败之端，治乱安危之致，足以劝惩后世与启沃吾君者，盖未尝一日而忘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221651_comment'></div>卒以备迩英之读，布于学官而行于天下，是岂小补也哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221651_comment'></div>初，书成而上之，帝为亲制美名，冠以序引，其所以尊德乐道之意，不唯彰信于一时而无愧，不刊之书又以为百世之赖，可谓盛矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221651_comment'></div>梦得，高平公少时字也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221651_comment'></div>初，太夫人怀公弥月，梦古丈夫盛服入其门者，左右曰汉大司徒邓禹也，故命名如此，而字梦得。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221651_comment'></div>后温公更其字曰淳父，犹取《高密侯传》赞语云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221651_comment'></div>高平孙仲熊与州学教授陆君俊民惧后生不知梦得之为公也，要余述于其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221651_comment'></div>俱常以谓观元祐之时而可知宰执近臣之选，观宰执近臣之懿而可知元祐之时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221651_comment'></div>无求之他，观于此而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221651_comment'></div>俱生晚，不得登二公之门，以观道德于后前，听教诲于左右，兹获挂名公书刻石之末，以寄宿昔欣慕之心焉，亦云幸矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221651_comment'></div>绍兴七年正月甲子，信安程俱谨识。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221651_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年1月23日</a>　正月二十三日，葬母于云台乡云门山之原。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1137&endYear=1137')">1137年9月9日</a>　九月九日，与赵叔问登通道门楼，有诗，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《丁巳九日携酒要叔问登通道门楼而江彦文寄玉友适至因用已未岁吴下九日诗韵作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527356' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527356' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527356?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丁巳九日携酒要叔问登通道门楼而江彦文寄玉友适至因用己未岁吴下九日诗韵作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1137年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527356")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527356_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527356'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527356'>凉秋风物正清华，极目高楼不见花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527356'>老境固知无乐事，醉乡聊欲寄生涯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527356'>银钩远寄清桐滑，玉液亲题赤印斜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527356'>笑引壶觞成一醉，歌筵遥想鬓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_527356", 527356, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>堆鸦</span><span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：闻彦文是日有盛集。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527356_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527356'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527356_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='5eacc3d6596d4467a36cbc9d6aa499c2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("5eacc3d6596d4467a36cbc9d6aa499c2");'><span id='5eacc3d6596d4467a36cbc9d6aa499c2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1144')">1139-1144年</a>，62-67岁</div><div id='5eacc3d6596d4467a36cbc9d6aa499c2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年3月</a>　三月，在衢州西安长寿僧舍之西修屋一间，名“实相斋”，有铭。作品：《实相斋铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_1221715' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221715' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221715?labeling=true' target='_blank'>实相斋铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（并跋　绍兴九年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1139年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221715")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221715_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221715'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221715'>观身实相，如梦幻响。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221715_comment'></div>亦如虚空，有无边际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221715_comment'></div>无作无受，无去来今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221715_comment'></div>无空不空，有愿无愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221715_comment'></div>生住异灭，一切皆无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221715_comment'></div>如如此身，威仪差别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221715_comment'></div>如是如是，皆如实知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221715_comment'></div>万境现前，如水镜像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221715_comment'></div>繁兴用处，而常湛然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221715_comment'></div>观一切法，无不皆空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221715_comment'></div>是为觉知，诸法实相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221715_comment'></div>相即是空，空即是实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221715_comment'></div>无能观者，亦无了知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221715_comment'></div>观佛亦然，一相无相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221715_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_1221715'>绍兴己未，北山老人寓止长寿五年矣，春三月，于寓舍之西为屋一间，挟以二厦，于是游息焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221715_comment'></div>名之曰实相斋，而为之铭。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1221715_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年10月24日</a>　十月二十四日，秦桧荐俱领史事，故除充实录院修撰，提举万寿观。俱以疾不至。时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年10月</a>　程俱以风痹之疾力辞，遂改提举亳州明道宫，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1139&endYear=1139')">1139年</a>　是年前后，请叶梦得为集作序，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1140&endYear=1140')">1140年10月25日</a>　寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。十月二十五日夜梦至一堂上……因索烛疾书而作。作品：《临池》<span class='inlineComment2'>（赋见《北山小集》卷十二。）</span><div id='poem_1221287' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221287' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221287?labeling=true' target='_blank'>临池</a><span class='authorDate'>（1140年10月25日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221287")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221287_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221287'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221287'>庚申十月丙申，子夜梦至一堂上，栋宇宏敞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221287_comment'></div>或出法书纵观，盖岳麓真迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221287_comment'></div>又一种，云是钟王绢素，极尘暗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221287_comment'></div>顾堂上板壁明净，因大书其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221287_comment'></div>书所谓「不令执简候亭馆」者，观之似不减传师令字，尤觉精采逼真，意颇欣然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221287_comment'></div>念欲以绢素好书，遽寤，则已营度赋句在口，心开意朗，思如涌泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221287_comment'></div>衰年乃犹有少时情思，窃自喜也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221287_comment'></div>因索烛疾书之纸，将以示同好云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221287_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_1221287'>若夫敞晴日之轩窗，临惠风之池阁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221287_comment'></div>山榧陈几，海珊置格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221287_comment'></div>濯玉海于清泉，饮霜毛于松壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221287_comment'></div>渰玄云之霮䨴，散晨鸦之纷泊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221287_comment'></div>舒白茧与乌丝，弃禾麻之凡恶；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221287_comment'></div>捐鸡羊之狞陋，罗象犀之䌽错。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221287_comment'></div>指实无间，掌虚似握。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221287_comment'></div>乍手和而笔调，亦神凝而虑却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221287_comment'></div>出重匮之深藏，发脩梁之秘凿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221287_comment'></div>还神明之旧观，鄙元和之新脚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221287_comment'></div>初凫戏于汪洋，俄鸿惊于寥廓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221287_comment'></div>轩轩跨海之鹏，冉冉游云之鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221287_comment'></div>焕出水之芙蓉，韵绕梁之清角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221287_comment'></div>宾主揖让，阴阳磅礴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221287_comment'></div>云澹烟霏，崖崩石落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221287_comment'></div>波三折而导送，势千钧而沈着。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221287_comment'></div>纷舞凤之参差，骇怒猊之喷薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221287_comment'></div>八分聊使于张军，掘笔宁甘于示弱！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221287_comment'></div>百金论价以犹轻，十部推贤而不怍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221287_comment'></div>竦危峰之障日，矫孤松之秀擢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221287_comment'></div>异婢子之羞涩，粲舞姝之婥约。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221287_comment'></div>婉如援镜以笑春，劲若剑挥而弩彍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221287_comment'></div>峭快若吴兴之童稚，退缩匪深山之鄙朴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221287_comment'></div>居然王谢之风流，俨若帝皇之濩蠖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221287_comment'></div>登山逶迤于嵩华，陷阵回旋于骝骆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221287_comment'></div>笼鹅无惮于空群，宝剑不虞于诈略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221287_comment'></div>逍遥散圣之禅，窘束毗尼之缚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221287_comment'></div>纷异态而殊能，有彼馀而此觳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221287_comment'></div>天然则不择而能精，积习则有资于力学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221287_comment'></div>践铁阈以屡穿，仰天门而苦卓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221287_comment'></div>嗟余老以缠痾，方捐书而静乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221287_comment'></div>顾志在而力疲，徒心劳而梦噩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221287_comment'></div>嗟土炭之殊嗜，笑偃濛之善谑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221287_comment'></div>虽习气之未除，羌才疏而技薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221287_comment'></div>与画史其何殊，眩精神于幻药。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221287_comment'></div>本变现于吾心，浪妍媸而喜愕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221287_comment'></div>苟戏好之犹存，庶犹贤于弈博。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221287_comment'></div>当知锵金入木，辞华虽照于荆相；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221287_comment'></div>二妙一台，筋骨终惭于张、索也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_46_1221287_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1141&endYear=1141')">1141年</a>　寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。夜梦崇宁乙酉，寓衢之天王僧舍，时方专气辟谷……念之慨然。作品：《记梦》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷十七。）</span><div id='poem_1221697' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221697' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221697?labeling=true' target='_blank'>记梦<span class='inlineComment2'>（并跋）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1141年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221697")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221697_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221697'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221697'>我梦异人，云善相者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221697_comment'></div>其所称道，飞仙真人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221697_comment'></div>而其结盘，乃祖师意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221697_comment'></div>手循我颈，揣相骨法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221697_comment'></div>后至我顶，云囟门开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221697_comment'></div>此是禅定，及修真效。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221697_comment'></div>复引我手，自挃其顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221697_comment'></div>如指面大，如小儿囟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221697_comment'></div>虚而微动，我大欢喜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221697_comment'></div>归语室家，令挃我头，虚动如故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221697_comment'></div>此何因缘，而梦斯事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221697_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1221697'>崇宁乙酉，寓衢之天王僧舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221697_comment'></div>时方专气辟谷，夜梦如此，记之药方册后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221697_comment'></div>它日忽见末后增四句云：「说此梦已，知是妄想。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221697_comment'></div>以手挃头，坚实如故」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221697_comment'></div>盖江仲嘉窃见书之，以相戏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221697_comment'></div>今三十六年矣，念之慨然。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221697_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1142&endYear=1142')">1142年</a>　寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。四月至七月间，为友人赵子昼作墓志铭。作品：《宋故徽猷阁直学士左中奉大夫致仕常山县开国伯食邑九百户赠左通奉大夫赵公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十三。）</span><div id='poem_1221803' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221803' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221803?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宋故徽猷阁直学士左中奉大夫致仕常山县开国伯食邑九百户赠左通奉大夫赵公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1142年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221803")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221803_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221803'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221803'>公讳子昼，字叔问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221803_comment'></div>五世祖德昭封于燕，是为燕懿王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221803_comment'></div>子曰惟和，永清军节度观察留后、安定郡公，公之高祖也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221803_comment'></div>曾祖讳从审，宁海军节度观察留后、宣城郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221803_comment'></div>祖讳世祎，镇海军节度观察留后、北海郡公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221803_comment'></div>父讳令佥，中亮大夫、荣州防御使，累赠少保。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221803_comment'></div>母王氏，封定国夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221803_comment'></div>叔问幼则端厚警敏，秀颖特异，中亮爱之甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221803_comment'></div>稍长，于读书如嗜欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221803_comment'></div>中亮藏书三万卷，号书窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221803_comment'></div>叔问日肄习其间，沈涵薰浃，不舍昼夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221803_comment'></div>中亮遇大礼任子，当及叔问，顾而曰：「是儿能自致，何以此为」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221803_comment'></div>取楷笏予之，因舍公而任其次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221803_comment'></div>初入南京国子监，于经籍固已贯穿便习，视当时场屋之文，意以谓殆可不学而能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221803_comment'></div>每较艺试闱，日未中，文已就，徜徉笑谑，若不经意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221803_comment'></div>及榜名，屡出诸生上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221803_comment'></div>年未冠，遂中大观元年进士第，为宗子第一，起家授承奉郎，签书大名府判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221803_comment'></div>魏固大府，宾幕僚史时宴饮相追逐，叔问常以事辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221803_comment'></div>公退，手未尝释卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221803_comment'></div>历佐二留守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221803_comment'></div>许特进将庄重谨绳墨，大器重之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221803_comment'></div>后尹梁资政子美为治强敏任威，一路畏詟，僚属唯唯进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221803_comment'></div>叔问恂恂少年耳，独能因事白其已甚者，尹或舍己意而行其说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221803_comment'></div>秩满，调湖州司录事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221803_comment'></div>代归，持所生母心丧三年，调宪州通判。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221803_comment'></div>宣和元年，差充详定九域图志所编修官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221803_comment'></div>会书局例罢，除知泽州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221803_comment'></div>未赴，改知密州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221803_comment'></div>召对，为刑部员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221803_comment'></div>自元丰新官制初除令铄为郎，久无继者，至是始除叔问，族属荣之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1221803_comment'></div>未几，丁中亮忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1221803_comment'></div>中亮居家刚严有常度，叔问自幼及壮在亲侧，目未尝迕视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1221803_comment'></div>虽盛夏，冠带终日，出入虞侍，时温凊、视膳羞，朝夕左右，便便唯谨，盖訚訚侃侃，尽色养之驩焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1221803_comment'></div>中亮以其敦朴，常曰：「是质实儿竟自佳」！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1221803_comment'></div>其于兄弟笃友爱，鞠其孤犹己子，宦学婚嫁，皆身任之，无失其时者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1221803_comment'></div>于亲故咸有恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1221803_comment'></div>靖康虏寇大入，自宋流寓淮浙，道丁母夫人忧，间关南渡，窜伏信安山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1221803_comment'></div>建炎四年，车驾驻跸会稽，诏以吏部员外郎召，俄迁左司员外郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1221803_comment'></div>时范丞相当国，叔问举职不懈，裨益居多，迁太常少卿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1221803_comment'></div>艰难以来，有司文籍散已，典礼或阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1221803_comment'></div>公学既通博，随事讨论，稽参古今，绵蕝草创，礼无违者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1221803_comment'></div>会礼部侍郎阙，除权官，上以公为可，遂以命之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1221803_comment'></div>明年，除徽猷阁待制、枢密都承旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1221803_comment'></div>宗室任三省密院从官，实自公始，人以为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1221803_comment'></div>又明年，迁兵部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1221803_comment'></div>绍兴三年冬，虏使李永寿、王诩来，上命公馆伴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1221803_comment'></div>时虏使久不至，至是虏情叵测，人以馆客为难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1221803_comment'></div>叔问自廷劳燕好至于赠贿，弥缝应对，无不得宜，虏使卒入见，成礼而去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1221803_comment'></div>其在朝廷恬旷靖共，无所适莫，思不出位，从容以和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1221803_comment'></div>踰年，请外补，以徽猷阁直学士知秀州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1221803_comment'></div>明年，移知平江府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1221803_comment'></div>其为治安静不扰，循理去甚，不为赫赫名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1221803_comment'></div>久之，恳请祠宫，以兵部侍郎召至行在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1221803_comment'></div>力申前请，遂以旧职提举江州太平观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1221803_comment'></div>寓止衢州凡七年，未尝有留滞之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1221803_comment'></div>自言慕司马徽之为人，若所谓入兽不乱群舍者，与之争席，盖优为之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1221803_comment'></div>得宽闲之地城南之郊，为池亭林圃，间与交旧游息其閒，浩浩然若将终身而不厌者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1221803_comment'></div>晨起，诵六经率若干卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1221803_comment'></div>又身教子侄，讲论经史，日有常课。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1221803_comment'></div>间则报谢宾客，不以寒暑风雨高下易其度也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1221803_comment'></div>十二年夏四月，以疾告老，迁左中奉大夫致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1221803_comment'></div>壬辰，以不起闻，享年五十四，诏赠左通奉大夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1221803_comment'></div>交游皆失声相吊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1221803_comment'></div>余初识叔问吴兴，一面定交，今三十年，情好弥厚，终始如一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1221803_comment'></div>观其刚而不亢，通而不流，不为利回，行己有耻，至于广览强记，直谅多闻，盖余之益友也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1221803_comment'></div>其文敏而粹，其家集而藏之，得二十卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1221803_comment'></div>于游艺往往精诸，书法尤为识者所推，篆、籀、楷、隶皆力追古人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1221803_comment'></div>至训诂形声之末与夫礼乐度数名物之微，莫不审其是而知其说也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1221803_comment'></div>其孤将以七月己酉葬公西安县道泰乡甘泉之原，厥既得卜，其孤号踊请铭于俱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1221803_comment'></div>余惟叔问之交友知旧，其名位文词足以耸动一时而传信于后者为不少，盍请铭于彼而俱是求？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1221803_comment'></div>不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1221803_comment'></div>其孤叩头见要曰：「先友之久且厚莫先丈人，知先人平生又详。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1221803_comment'></div>况远日既迫，傥辞避引日，将不及事，无以掩诸幽，以没先人之美，而重不孝之罪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1221803_comment'></div>泣血固请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1221803_comment'></div>余义不得终辞，则叙其治行而系以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1221803_comment'></div>公配郡氏，封硕人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1221803_comment'></div>三男，长曰伯赐，右承务郎，提点坑冶铸钱司检踏官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1221803_comment'></div>次曰伯昂，右承务郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1221803_comment'></div>幼曰伯量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1221803_comment'></div>二女，长嫁右修职郎、监临江军赡军酒库冯作，次已嫁而归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1221803_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_80_1221803'>太支惟四，仲封于燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1221803_comment'></div>纯嘏有衍，流光邈绵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1221803_comment'></div>五世弥昌，允艺且贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1221803_comment'></div>惟叔问甫，奋由厥躬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1221803_comment'></div>抗志厉行，光享有终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1221803_comment'></div>骥堕地走，兰茁而芳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1221803_comment'></div>绝出群辈，凤翔高冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1221803_comment'></div>瑞此王室，家廷之庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1221803_comment'></div>垂髫就傅，束发试吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1221803_comment'></div>至于艾耆，出守入侍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1221803_comment'></div>靖共明哲，纯美无颣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1221803_comment'></div>进斯匪懈，退以求志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1221803_comment'></div>风流江左，术业洙泗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1221803_comment'></div>胡不百年，益用于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1221803_comment'></div>向、歆七略，间、平六艺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1221803_comment'></div>庶几有成，斧藻皇治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1221803_comment'></div>甘泉之幽，盘郁森邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1221803_comment'></div>藏之孔安，遗祉嗣裔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_97_1221803_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1143&endYear=1143')">1143年</a>　寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年6月</a>　寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。六月，乞致仕，转左中奉大夫。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1144&endYear=1144')">1144年6月12日</a>　六月十二日壬辰，卒于衢州西安长寿僧舍，赠左通奉大夫。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
衢江
-----detail
