href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　夏，读藏经，编次图，题偈句，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《题三界四禅天图偈句》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十六。）</span><div id='poem_1221736' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221736' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221736?labeling=true' target='_blank'>题三界四禅天图偈句<span class='inlineComment2'>（并跋　绍兴八年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221736")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221736_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221736'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221736'>如火宅喻，三界无安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221736_comment'></div>是故众生，应求出要。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221736_comment'></div>而此三界，亦如空华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221736_comment'></div>分别说三，实无所有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221736_comment'></div>我观如来，不可思议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221736_comment'></div>出入三界，如游观园。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221736_comment'></div>而常湛然，处菩提座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221736_comment'></div>应知亦有，上上根人，不历阶梯，径超佛地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221736_comment'></div>四双八辈，如焦谷牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221736_comment'></div>十地四禅，如隔罗縠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221736_comment'></div>凡此世界，能忍众生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221736_comment'></div>若见若闻，应知希有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221736_comment'></div>思地狱苦，发菩提心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221736_comment'></div>如救头然，慎勿放逸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221736_comment'></div>诸恶莫作，众善奉行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221736_comment'></div>是虽常谈，是佛教诲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221736_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_1221736'>绍兴八年，北山程俱长寿寓舍读藏经毕，于解夏日编次图，仍题偈句。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1221736_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年9月9日</a>　九月九日，又与赵叔问登城楼，有诗，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《戊午岁九日，复与叔问登城楼再用前韵作》<span class='inlineComment2'>（诗见《北山小集》卷十。）</span><div id='poem_527357' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_527357' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/527357?labeling=true' target='_blank'>戊午岁九日复与叔问登城楼再用前韵作</a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年9月9日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_527357")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_527357_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_527357'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_527357'>兀坐空哦服九华，衰颓深觉负黄花。<div id='poem_sentence_0_527357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_527357'>但令无事长相见，敢叹百年生有涯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_527357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_527357'>雉堞晓登千嶂抱，縠波秋净一溪斜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_527357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_527357'>归来更展新诗卷，醉墨淋漓似老鸦<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_527357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_527357'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_527357_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_527357'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_527357_0'>⑴ 自注：卢仝有却来案上翻墨汁，涂抹诗书如老鸦之句。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_527357_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1138&endYear=1138')">1138年</a>　是年四月至九月间，为僧修意作墓志铭，时寓居衢州西安长寿僧舍。作品：《衢州开化县龙华院意上座塔铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（文见《北山小集》卷三十三。据程俱《北山小集》卷三十三《衢州开化县龙华院意上座塔铭》：绍兴“八年……师之弟子庆居以书来告：‘师以四月己卯晨……寂……将以九月丁酉，奉师遗骨藏于寺之东南隅而建塔焉。’”，时间当在是年四月至九月间。）</span><div id='poem_1221796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1221796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1221796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>衢州开化县龙华院意上座塔铭<span class='inlineComment2'>（绍兴八年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1138年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(30728, "宋", "程俱", "poem_title_1221796")'>程俱</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1221796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1221796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1221796'>师名修意，字无言，开化人，姓魏氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1221796_comment'></div>田家子，幼勤恪不欺，不事敖戏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1221796_comment'></div>年十五，受业于龙华传教师道圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1221796_comment'></div>后七年，削发受具戒，圆稍授以天台章句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1221796_comment'></div>未几，已能贯习，益纵之游学他郡，凡名师哲匠，皆从之隶业焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1221796_comment'></div>居数年间，有传正法眼藏出世间、了生死者，弃所习往从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1221796_comment'></div>初入天童齐公之室，后至新定之广灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1221796_comment'></div>时佛印祖禅师道化方隆，师又入其室，刳心遗形，刮摩淘汰，晨夕不懈，殆忘寝食，佛印器之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1221796_comment'></div>卒之能所两忘，尽得其奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1221796_comment'></div>会佛印去广灵，里居士夫自江公人表皆请以师继其法席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1221796_comment'></div>师力辞，亟归开化灵山之故栖，盖去龙华十八年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1221796_comment'></div>结庵安居，名之曰「安养」，足不踰阈，修长忏者三年，以回向般若，施度有情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1221796_comment'></div>崇宁间，余上书罢吏太湖，归乡邑，寓灵山寺之西轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1221796_comment'></div>始识师，颀然众中，麻衣芒屦，韵孤而貌寂，固异之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1221796_comment'></div>与之言，盖明道眼、饱丛林者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1221796_comment'></div>余方幽忧块处，往往日至其庐，语必移晷，相对萧然，忘其身之穷而世道隘也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1221796_comment'></div>大观初，余迫于禄养，又出而求仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1221796_comment'></div>是年冬，师亦复归龙华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1221796_comment'></div>其后余归省松楸，必与师会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1221796_comment'></div>绍兴二年春，余罢职西省，归而过师于龙华，则师病且衰矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1221796_comment'></div>八年，余寓郡郊四年矣，师之弟子庆居以书来告，师以四月己卯晨起，沐浴更衣，集众告辞，趺坐奄然而寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1221796_comment'></div>茶毗，齿牙独不坏散，其徒以谓真实无诳诞之所致云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1221796_comment'></div>寿七十九，僧蜡五十八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1221796_comment'></div>弟子庆居、戒月、妙辩、善信、希声将以九月丁酉奉师遗骨藏于寺之东南隅而建塔焉，庆居走余门，以铭为请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1221796_comment'></div>余惟师慧目既清，履行无玷，于教席为阿阇梨，而无鄙吝封执贡高之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1221796_comment'></div>能舍有为而从无学，于禅林为第一座，而未尝有几微营保社、希利养之意，盖闻人巨刹请留而不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1221796_comment'></div>视世之释子贪浊狂乱，区区汲汲于权利之间者，岂不贤哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1221796_comment'></div>又与之有故，是宜铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1221796_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1221796'>是惟意公之塔，云壑萦带，莲峰秀发，风林演唱，山谷响答。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1221796_comment'></div>师曾不亡，常说妙法。</div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1221796_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
